Ethay Eatgray Atsbygay byay Fay. Ottscay Itzgeraldfay Abletay ofyay OntentsIIIIIIIVVVIVIIVIIIIXcay Onceyay againyay otay Eldazay Enthay earway ethay oldgay athay, ifyay atthay illway ovemay er;hay Ifyay ouyay ancay ouncebay ighhay, ouncebay orfay erhay ootay, Illtay eshay cryay over“Lay, old-hattedgay, igh-bouncinghay overlay, Iyay ustmay avehay ou!”yay Omasthay Arkepay d’Invilliersay IInyay myay oungeryay andyay oremay ulnerablevay earsyay myay atherfay avegay emay omesay advicethatyay I’veyay eenbay urningtay overyay inyay myay indmay everyay ince.“Wheneversay ouyay eelfay ikelay iticizingcray anyone,”yay ehay oldtay emay, ustremember“jay atthay allyay ethay eoplepay inyay isthay orldway aven’thay adhay ethay advantagesthatyay ou’veyay ad.”Hehay idn’tday aysay anyyay oremay, utbay e’veway alwaysyay eenbay unusuallyyay ommunicativeincay ayay eservedray ayway, andyay Iyay understoodyay atthay ehay eantmay ayay eatgray ealday orethanmay atthay. Inyay onsequencecay, I’myay inclinedyay otay eserveray allyay udgementsjay, ahabityay atthay ashay openedyay upyay anymay uriouscay aturesnay otay emay andyay alsoyay ademay ethemay ictimvay ofyay otnay ayay ewfay eteranvay oresbay. Ethay abnormalyay indmay isyay uickqay odetecttay andyay attachyay itselfyay otay isthay ualityqay enwhay ityay appearsyay inyay ayay ormalpersonnay, andyay osay ityay amecay aboutyay atthay inyay ollegecay Iyay asway unjustlyyay accusedyay ofbeingyay ayay oliticianpay, ecausebay Iyay asway ivypray otay ethay ecretsay iefsgray ofyay ild,unknownway enmay. Ostmay ofyay ethay onfidencescay ereway unsought—frequentlyyay Iyay avefeignedhay eepslay, eoccupationpray, oryay ayay ostilehay evitylay enwhay Iyay ealizedray bysomeay unmistakableyay ignsay atthay anyay intimateyay evelationray asway uiveringqay ontheyay orizon;hay orfay ethay intimateyay evelationsray ofyay oungyay enmay, oryay atyay eastthelay ermstay inyay ichwhay eythay expressyay emthay, areyay usuallyyay agiaristicplay andmarredyay byay obviousyay uppressionssay. Eservingray udgementsjay isyay ayay attermay ofinfiniteyay opehay. Iyay amyay illstay ayay ittlelay afraidyay ofyay issingmay omethingsay ifyay Iforgetyay atthay, asyay myay atherfay obbishlysnay uggestedsay, andyay Iyay obbishlyrepeatsnay, ayay ensesay ofyay ethay undamentalfay ecenciesday isyay arcelledpay outunequallyyay atyay irth.Andbay, afteryay oastingbay isthay ayway ofyay myay olerancetay, Iyay omecay otay ethay admissionthatyay ityay ashay ayay imitlay. Onductcay aymay ebay oundedfay onyay ethay ardhay ockray oryay ewetthay arshesmay, utbay afteryay ayay ertaincay ointpay Iyay on’tday arecay atwhay it’syay oundedonfay. Enwhay Iyay amecay ackbay omfray ethay Eastyay astlay autumnyay Iyay eltfay atthay Iyay antedtheway orldway otay ebay inyay uniformyay andyay atyay ayay ortsay ofyay oralmay attentionyay orever;fay Iwantedyay onay oremay iotousray excursionsyay ithway ivilegedpray impsesglay intoyay ehumanthay earthay. Onlyyay Atsbygay, ethay anmay owhay ivesgay ishay amenay otay isthay ookbay, asexemptway omfray myay eaction—Gatsbyray, owhay epresentedray everythingyay orfay ichwhay Ihaveyay anyay unaffectedyay ornscay. Ifyay ersonalitypay isyay anyay unbrokenyay eriessay ofsuccessfulyay esturesgay, enthay erethay asway omethingsay orgeousgay aboutyay imhay, omeheightenedsay ensitivitysay otay ethay omisespray ofyay ifelay, asyay ifyay ehay ereway elatedtoray oneyay ofyay osethay intricateyay achinesmay atthay egisterray earthquakesyay enthousandtay ilesmay awayyay. Isthay esponsivenessray adhay othingnay otay oday ithway atflabbythay impressionabilityyay ichwhay isyay ignifiedday underyay ethay amenay ofyay e“creativethay emperament”—ittay asway anyay extraordinaryyay iftgay orfay opehay, aromanticyay eadinessray uchsay asyay Iyay avehay evernay oundfay inyay anyyay otheryay ersonpay andwhichyay ityay isyay otnay ikelylay Iyay allshay everyay indfay againyay. O—Gatsbynay urnedtay outallyay ightray atyay ethay end;yay ityay isyay atwhay eyedpray onyay Atsbygay, atwhay oulfay ustfloatedday inyay ethay akeway ofyay ishay eamsdray atthay emporarilytay osedclay outyay interestmyay inyay ethay abortiveyay orrowssay andyay ort-windedshay elationsyay ofyay en.------------------------------------------------------------------------Mymay amilyfay avehay eenbay ominentpray, ell-to-doway eoplepay inyay isthay IddleWesternmay itycay orfay threeay enerationsgay. Ethay Arrawayscay areyay omethingsay ofyay aclanyay, andyay eway avehay ayay aditiontray atthay e’reway escendedday omfray ethay Ukesday ofBuccleuchyay, utbay ethay actualyay ounderfay ofyay myay inelay asway myay andfather’sbrothergray, owhay amecay erehay inyay ifty-onefay, entsay ayay ubstitutesay otay ethay IvilWarcay, andyay artedstay ethay olesalewhay ardwarehay usinessbay atthay myay athercarriesfay onyay oday.Itay evernay awsay isthay eat-unclegray, utbay I’myay upposedsay otay ooklay ikelay im—withspecialhay eferenceray otay ethay atherray ard-boiledhay aintingpay atthay angshay infather’syay officeyay. Iyay aduatedgray omfray Ewnay Avenhay inyay 1915ay, ustjay ayay uarterqay ofayay enturycay afteryay myay atherfay, andyay ayay ittlelay aterlay Iyay articipatedpay inyay atdelayedthay Eutonictay igrationmay ownknay asyay ethay Eatgray Arway. Iyay enjoyedyay ecounter-raidthay osay oroughlythay atthay Iyay amecay ackbay estlessray. Insteadyay ofyay eingthebay armway entrecay ofyay ethay orldway, ethay Iddlemay Estway ownay eemedsay ikelay eraggedthay edgeyay ofyay ethay universe—soyay Iyay ecidedday otay ogay Eastyay andyay earnlay ethay ondbusinessbay. Everybodyyay Iyay ewknay asway inyay ethay ondbay usinessbay, osay Iyay upposedsay itcouldyay upportsay oneyay oremay inglesay anmay. Allyay myay auntsyay andyay unclesyay alkedtay itoveryay asyay ifyay eythay ereway oosingchay ayay eppray schoolay orfay emay, andyay inallyfay aid,“Why—ye-es,”say ithway eryvay avegray, esitanthay acesfay. Atherfay agreedyay otay inancemefay orfay ayay earyay, andyay afteryay ariousvay elaysday Iyay amecay Eastyay, ermanentlypay, Ithoughtyay, inyay ethay springay ofyay enty-two.Thetway acticalpray ingthay asway otay indfay oomsray inyay ethay itycay, utbay ityay asway ayay armseasonway, andyay Iyay adhay ustjay eftlay ayay ountrycay ofyay ideway awnslay andyay iendlytreesfray, osay enwhay ayay oungyay anmay atyay ethay officeyay uggestedsay atthay eway aketay ahouseyay ogethertay inyay ayay ommutingcay owntay, ityay oundedsay ikelay ayay eatgray ideayay. Efoundhay ethay ousehay, ayay eather-beatenway ardboardcay ungalowbay atyay eightyyay amonthyay, utbay atyay ethay astlay inutemay ethay irmfay orderedyay imhay otay Ashingtonway, andIyay entway outyay otay ethay ountrycay aloneyay. Iyay adhay ayay og—atday eastlay Iyay adhay imhay orfay afewyay aysday untilyay ehay anray away—andyay anyay oldyay Odgeday andyay ayay Innishfay omanway, omadewhay myay edbay andyay ookedcay eakfastbray andyay utteredmay Innishfay isdomway oherselftay overyay ethay electricyay ove.Itstay asway onelylay orfay ayay ayday oryay osay untilyay oneyay orningmay omesay anmay, orerecentlymay arrivedyay anthay Iyay, oppedstay emay onyay ethay oad.“Howray oday ouyay etgay otay Estway Eggyay illage?”vay ehay askedyay elplessly.Ihay oldtay imhay. Andyay asyay Iyay alkedway onyay Iyay asway onelylay onay ongerlay. Iyay asway ayay uide,agay athfinderpay, anyay originalyay ettlersay. Ehay adhay asuallycay onferredcay onyay emay efreedomthay ofyay ethay eighbourhood.Andnay osay ithway ethay unshinesay andyay ethay eatgray urstsbay ofyay eaveslay owinggray onyay etreesthay, ustjay asyay ingsthay owgray inyay astfay oviesmay, Iyay adhay atthay amiliarconvictionfay atthay ifelay asway eginningbay overyay againyay ithway ethay ummer.Theresay asway osay uchmay otay eadray, orfay oneyay ingthay, andyay osay uchmay inefay ealthhay obetay ulledpay ownday outyay ofyay ethay oungyay eath-givingbray airyay. Iyay oughtbay ayay ozenvolumesday onyay ankingbay andyay editcray andyay investmentyay ecuritiessay, andyay eystoodthay onyay myay elfshay inyay edray andyay oldgay ikelay ewnay oneymay omfray ethay int,promisingmay otay unfoldyay ethay iningshay ecretssay atthay onlyyay Idasmay andyay Organmay andMaecenasyay ewknay. Andyay Iyay adhay ethay ighhay intentionyay ofyay eadingray anymay otherbooksyay esidesbay. Iyay asway atherray iterarylay inyay ollege—onecay earyay Iyay otewray aseriesyay ofyay eryvay olemnsay andyay obviousyay editorialsyay orfay ethay Aleyay Ews—andnay owInay asway oinggay otay ingbray ackbay allyay uchsay ingsthay intoyay myay ifelay andyay ecomeagainbay atthay ostmay imitedlay ofyay allyay ecialistsspay, ethay ell-rounded“way an.”Thismay isn’tyay ustjay anyay epigram—lifeyay isyay uchmay oremay uccessfullysay ookedlay atfromyay ayay inglesay indowway, afteryay all.Ityay asway ayay attermay ofyay ancechay atthay Iyay ouldshay avehay entedray ayay ousehay inyay oneyay oftheyay strangestay ommunitiescay inyay Orthnay Americayay. Ityay asway onyay atthay enderriotousslay islandyay ichwhay extendsyay itselfyay ueday eastyay ofyay Ewnay Ork—andyay eretherewhay areyay, amongyay otheryay aturalnay uriositiescay, otway unusualyay ormationsfay oflandyay. Entytway ilesmay omfray ethay itycay ayay airpay ofyay enormousyay eggsyay, identicalyay incontouryay andyay eparatedsay onlyyay byay ayay ourtesycay aybay, utjay outyay intoyay ethay ostdomesticatedmay odybay ofyay altsay aterway inyay ethay Esternway emispherehay, ethay eatwetgray arnyardbay ofyay Onglay Islandyay Oundsay. Eythay areyay otnay erfectpay ovals—likeyay eeggthay inyay ethay Olumbuscay orystay, eythay areyay othbay ushedcray atflay atyay ethay ontactend—butcay eirthay physicalay esemblanceray ustmay ebay ayay ourcesay ofyay erpetualwonderpay otay ethay ullsgay atthay flyay overheadyay. Otay ethay inglessway ayay oreinterestingmay enomenonphay isyay eirthay issimilarityday inyay everyyay articularexceptpay apeshay andyay ize.Isay ivedlay atyay Estway Eggyay, e—wellthay, ethay esslay ashionablefay ofyay ethay otway, oughthisthay isyay ayay ostmay uperficialsay agtay otay expressyay ethay izarrebay andyay otnay ayay ittlesinisterlay ontrastcay etweenbay emthay. Myay ousehay asway atyay ethay eryvay iptay ofyay eeggthay, onlyyay iftyfay ardsyay omfray ethay Oundsay, andyay ueezedsqay etweenbay otway ugeplaceshay atthay entedray orfay elvetway oryay ifteenfay ousandthay ayay easonsay. Ethay oneyay onmyyay ightray asway ayay olossalcay affairyay byay anyyay andard—itstay asway ayay actualimitationfay ofyay omesay Hôtelay eday Illevay inyay Ormandynay, ithway ayay owertay onyay onesideyay, ankingspay ewnay underyay ayay inthay eardbay ofyay awray ivyyay, andyay ayay arbleswimmingmay oolpay, andyay oremay anthay ortyfay acresyay ofyay awnlay andyay ardengay. Ityay asGatsby’sway ansionmay. Oryay, atherray, asyay Iyay idn’tday owknay Mray. Atsbygay, ityay asway amansionyay inhabitedyay byay ayay entlemangay ofyay atthay amenay. Myay ownyay ousehay asway aneyesoreyay, utbay ityay asway ayay allsmay eyesoreyay, andyay ityay adhay eenbay overlookedyay, osay Ihadyay ayay iewvay ofyay ethay aterway, ayay artialpay iewvay ofyay myay eighbour’snay awnlay, andtheyay onsolingcay oximitypray ofyay illionaires—allmay orfay eightyyay ollarsday amonth.Acrossyay ethay ourtesycay aybay ethay itewhay alacespay ofyay ashionablefay Eastyay Eggglitteredyay alongyay ethay aterway, andyay ethay istoryhay ofyay ethay ummersay eallyray eginsonbay ethay eveningyay Iyay ovedray overyay erethay otay avehay innerday ithway ethay OmBuchananstay. Aisyday asway myay econdsay ousincay onceyay emovedray, andyay I’dyay ownknay Omintay ollegecay. Andyay ustjay afteryay ethay arway Iyay entspay otway aysday ithway emthay inChicago.Heryay usbandhay, amongyay ariousvay physicalay accomplishmentsyay, adhay eenbay oneyay oftheyay ostmay owerfulpay endsyay atthay everyay ayedplay ootballfay atyay Ewnay Aven—anationalhay igurefay inyay ayay ayway, oneyay ofyay osethay enmay owhay eachray uchsay anyay acutelimitedyay excellenceyay atyay enty-onetway atthay everythingyay afterwardyay avourssay ofanticlimaxyay. Ishay amilyfay ereway enormouslyyay ealthy—evenway inyay ollegecay isfreedomhay ithway oneymay asway ayay attermay orfay eproach—butray ownay e’dhay eftlay Icagoandchay omecay Eastyay inyay ayay ashionfay atthay atherray ooktay ouryay eathbray awayyay: orinstancefay, e’dhay oughtbray ownday ayay stringay ofyay olopay oniespay omfray AkeForestlay. Ityay asway ardhay otay ealizeray atthay ayay anmay inyay myay ownyay enerationgay aswealthyway enoughyay otay oday at.Whythay eythay amecay Eastyay Iyay on’tday owknay. Eythay adhay entspay ayay earyay inyay Ancefray ornofay articularpay easonray, andyay enthay ifteddray erehay andyay erethay unrestfullywhereveryay eoplepay ayedplay olopay andyay ereway ichray ogethertay. Isthay asway apermanentyay ovemay, aidsay Aisyday overyay ethay elephonetay, utbay Iyay idn’tday elieveit—Ibay adhay onay ightsay intoyay Aisy’sday earthay, utbay Iyay eltfay atthay Omtay ouldway iftondray oreverfay eekingsay, ayay ittlelay istfullyway, orfay ethay amaticdray urbulencetay ofsomeyay irrecoverableyay ootballfay ame.Andgay osay ityay appenedhay atthay onyay ayay armway indyway eveningyay Iyay ovedray overyay otay EastEggyay otay eesay otway oldyay iendsfray omwhay Iyay arcelyscay ewknay atyay allyay. Eirthay ousewashay evenyay oremay elaborateyay anthay Iyay expectedyay, ayay eerfulchay ed-and-whiteGeorgianray Olonialcay ansionmay, overlookingyay ethay aybay. Ethay awnlay artedstay attheyay eachbay andyay anray owardstay ethay ontfray oorday orfay ayay uarterqay ofyay ayay ile,jumpingmay overyay undialssay andyay ickbray alksway andyay urningbay ardens—finallygay enitwhay eachedray ethay ousehay iftingdray upyay ethay idesay inyay ightbray inesvay asyay oughfromthay ethay omentummay ofyay itsyay unray. Ethay ontfray asway okenbray byay ayay inelay ofyay Enchwindowsfray, owingglay ownay ithway eflectedray oldgay andyay ideway openyay otay ethay armwindyway afternoonyay, andyay Omtay Uchananbay inyay idingray othesclay asway andingstay ithhisway egslay apartyay onyay ethay ontfray orch.Hepay adhay angedchay incesay ishay Ewnay Avenhay earsyay. Ownay ehay asway ayay urdystraw-hairedstay anmay ofyay irtythay, ithway ayay atherray ardhay outhmay andyay asuperciliousyay annermay. Otway iningshay arrogantyay eyesyay adhay establisheddominanceyay overyay ishay acefay andyay avegay imhay ethay appearanceyay ofyay alwaysyay eaningaggressivelylay orwardfay. Otnay evenyay ethay effeminateyay anksway ofyay ishay idingclothesray ouldcay idehay ethay enormousyay owerpay ofyay atthay ody—hebay eemedsay otay illthosefay isteningglay ootsbay untilyay ehay straineday ethay optay acinglay, andyay ouyay ouldseecay ayay eatgray ackpay ofyay usclemay iftingshay enwhay ishay ouldershay ovedmay underyay isthinhay oatcay. Ityay asway ayay odybay apablecay ofyay enormousyay everage—alay uelcray ody.Hisbay eakingspay oicevay, ayay uffgray uskyhay enortay, addedyay otay ethay impressionyay offractiousnessyay ehay onveyedcay. Erethay asway ayay ouchtay ofyay aternalpay ontemptcay inityay, evenyay owardtay eoplepay ehay iked—andlay erethay ereway enmay atyay Ewnay Avenhay ohadwhay atedhay ishay uts.“Nowgay, on’tday inkthay myay opinionyay onyay esethay attersmay isyay inal,”fay ehay eemedsay osaytay, ust“jay ecausebay I’myay strongeray andyay oremay ofyay ayay anmay anthay ouyay are.”yay Ewereway inyay ethay amesay eniorsay ocietysay, andyay ilewhay eway ereway evernay intimateyay Ialwaysyay adhay ethay impressionyay atthay ehay approvedyay ofyay emay andyay antedway emay otay ikehimlay ithway omesay arshhay, efiantday istfulnessway ofyay ishay own.Weyay alkedtay orfay ayay ewfay inutesmay onyay ethay unnysay orch.“I’vepay otgay ayay icenay aceplay ere,”hay ehay aidsay, ishay eyesyay ashingflay aboutrestlessly.Turningyay emay aroundyay byay oneyay armyay, ehay ovedmay ayay oadbray atflay andhay alongyay efrontthay istavay, includingyay inyay itsyay eepsway ayay unkensay Italianyay ardengay, ayay alfacrehay ofyay eepday, ungentpay osesray, andyay ayay ub-nosedsnay otorboatmay atthay umpedthebay idetay offshore.“Ityay elongedbay otay Emaineday, ethay oilyay an.”may Ehay urnedtay emay aroundyay again,politelyyay andyay abruptlyyay. e’ll“Way ogay inside.”Weyay alkedway throughay ayay ighhay allwayhay intoyay ayay ightbray osy-colouredray ace,fragilelyspay oundbay intoyay ethay ousehay byay Enchfray indowsway atyay eitheryay endyay. Ewindowsthay ereway ajaryay andyay eamingglay itewhay againstyay ethay eshfray assgray outsidethatyay eemedsay otay owgray ayay ittlelay ayway intoyay ethay ousehay. Ayay eezebray ewblay throughtheay oomray, ewblay urtainscay inyay atyay oneyay endyay andyay outyay ethay otheryay ikelay aleflagspay, istingtway emthay upyay owardtay ethay ostedfray edding-cakeway ofyay eceilingthay, andyay enthay ippledray overyay ethay ine-colouredway ugray, akingmay ayay adowonshay ityay asyay indway oesday onyay ethay ea.Thesay onlyyay ompletelycay ationarystay objectyay inyay ethay oomray asway anyay enormouscouchyay onyay ichwhay otway oungyay omenway ereway uoyedbay upyay asyay oughthay uponyay ananchoredyay alloonbay. Eythay ereway othbay inyay itewhay, andyay eirthay essesdray ereripplingway andyay utteringflay asyay ifyay eythay adhay ustjay eenbay ownblay ackbay inyay afteryay ashortyay ightflay aroundyay ethay ousehay. Iyay ustmay avehay oodstay orfay ayay ewfay omentslisteningmay otay ethay ipwhay andyay apsnay ofyay ethay urtainscay andyay ethay oangray ofyay apictureyay onyay ethay allway. Enthay erethay asway ayay oombay asyay Omtay Uchananbay utshay erearthay indowsway andyay ethay aughtcay indway iedday outyay aboutyay ethay oomray, andyay ecurtainsthay andyay ethay ugsray andyay ethay otway oungyay omenway alloonedbay owlyslay otay efloor.Thethay oungeryay ofyay ethay otway asway ayay strangeray otay emay. Eshay asway extendedyay ulllengthfay atyay erhay endyay ofyay ethay ivanday, ompletelycay otionlessmay, andyay ithway erchinhay aisedray ayay ittlelay, asyay ifyay eshay ereway alancingbay omethingsay onyay ityay ichwaswhay uiteqay ikelylay otay allfay. Ifyay eshay awsay emay outyay ofyay ethay ornercay ofyay erhay eyessheyay avegay onay inthay ofyay it—indeedyay, Iyay asway almostyay urprisedsay intoyay urmuringanmay apologyyay orfay avinghay isturbedday erhay byay omingcay in.Theyay otheryay irlgay, Aisyday, ademay anyay attemptyay otay ise—sheray eanedlay ightlyforwardslay ithway ayay onscientiouscay expression—thenyay eshay aughedlay, anyay absurd,charmingyay ittlelay aughlay, andyay Iyay aughedlay ootay andyay amecay orwardfay intoyay eroom.“I’mthay p-paralyseday ithway appiness.”Shehay aughedlay againyay, asyay ifyay eshay aidsay omethingsay eryvay ittyway, andyay eldhay myhanday orfay ayay omentmay, ookinglay upyay intoyay myay acefay, omisingpray atthay erethay asnoway oneyay inyay ethay orldway eshay osay uchmay antedway otay eesay. Atthay asway ayay ayway ehadshay. Eshay intedhay inyay ayay urmurmay atthay ethay urnamesay ofyay ethay alancingbay irlgay asBakerway. (I’veay eardhay ityay aidsay atthay Aisy’sday urmurmay asway onlyyay otay akemay eopleleanpay owardtay er;hay anyay irrelevantyay iticismcray atthay ademay ityay onay esscharming.)Atlay anyyay ateray, Issmay Aker’sbay ipslay utteredflay, eshay oddednay atyay emay almostimperceptiblyyay, andyay enthay uicklyqay ippedtay erhay eadhay ackbay again—theyay objectsheyay asway alancingbay adhay obviouslyyay otteredtay ayay ittlelay andyay ivengay ersomethinghay ofyay ayay ightfray. Againyay ayay ortsay ofyay apologyyay aroseyay otay myay ips.Almostlay anyyay exhibitionyay ofyay ompletecay elf-sufficiencysay awsdray ayay unnedtributestay omfray e.Imay ookedlay ackbay atyay myay ousincay, owhay eganbay otay askyay emay uestionsqay inyay erhay ow,thrillinglay oicevay. Ityay asway ethay indkay ofyay oicevay atthay ethay earyay ollowsfay upyay anddownyay, asyay ifyay eachyay eechspay isyay anyay arrangementyay ofyay otesnay atthay illway evernay eplayedbay againyay. Erhay acefay asway adsay andyay ovelylay ithway ightbray ingsthay inyay it,brightyay eyesyay andyay ayay ightbray assionatepay outhmay, utbay erethay asway anyay excitementinyay erhay oicevay atthay enmay owhay adhay aredcay orfay erhay oundfay ifficultday otay orget:afay ingingsay ompulsioncay, ayay isperedwhay isten,”“Lay ayay omisepray atthay eshay addonehay aygay, excitingyay ingsthay ustjay ayay ilewhay incesay andyay atthay erethay ereway ay,excitinggay ingsthay overinghay inyay ethay extnay our.Ihay oldtay erhay owhay Iyay adhay oppedstay offyay inyay Icagochay orfay ayay ayday onyay myay ayway East,andyay owhay ayay ozenday eoplepay adhay entsay eirthay ovelay throughay e.“Domay eythay issmay e?”may eshay iedcray ecstatically.“Theyay olewhay owntay isyay esolateday. Ethay actfay atthay ossipgay adhay ublishedpay ethay annsbay asway oneofyay ethay easonsray Iyay adhay omecay Eastyay. Ouyay an’tcay opstay oinggay ithway anyay oldfriendyay onyay accountyay ofyay umoursray, andyay onyay ethay otheryay andhay Iyay adhay onay intentionofyay eingbay umouredray intoyay arriage.Theirmay interestyay atherray ouchedtay emay andyay ademay emthay esslay emotelyrich—neverthelessray, Iyay asway onfusedcay andyay ayay ittlelay isgustedday asyay Iyay oveawaydray. Ityay eemedsay otay emay atthay ethay ingthay orfay Aisyday otay oday asway otay ushray outofyay ethay ousehay, ildchay inyay arms—butyay apparentlyyay erethay ereway onay uchintentionssay inyay erhay eadhay. Asyay orfay Omtay, ethay actfay atthay ehay ad“hay omesay omaninway Ewnay Ork”yay asway eallyray esslay urprisingsay anthay atthay ehay adhay eendepressedbay byay ayay ookbay. Omethingsay asway akingmay imhay ibblenay atyay ethay edgeyay ofstaleyay ideasyay asyay ifyay ishay urdystay physicalay egotismyay onay ongerlay ourishednay isperemptoryhay eart.Alreadyhay ityay asway eepday ummersay onyay oadhouseray oofsray andyay inyay ontfray ofyay aysidegaragesway, erewhay ewnay edray etrol-pumpspay atsay outyay inyay oolspay ofyay ightlay, andwhenyay Iyay eachedray myay estateyay atyay Estway Eggyay Iyay anray ethay arcay underyay itsyay edshay andsatyay orfay ayay ilewhay onyay anyay abandonedyay assgray ollerray inyay ethay ardyay. Ethay indway adblownhay offyay, eavinglay ayay oudlay, ightbray ightnay, ithway ingsway eatingbay inyay etreesthay andyay ayay ersistentpay organyay oundsay asyay ethay ullfay ellowsbay ofyay ethay earthblewyay ethay ogsfray ullfay ofyay ifelay. Ethay ilhouettesay ofyay ayay ovingmay atcay averedacrossway ethay oonlightmay, andyay, urningtay myay eadhay otay atchway ityay, Iyay awsay atthay Iwasyay otnay alone—fiftyyay eetfay awayyay ayay igurefay adhay emergedyay omfray ethay adowshay ofmyyay eighbour’snay ansionmay andyay asway andingstay ithway ishay andshay inyay ishay ocketsregardingpay ethay ilversay epperpay ofyay ethay arsstay. Omethingsay inyay ishay eisurelymovementslay andyay ethay ecuresay ositionpay ofyay ishay eetfay uponyay ethay awnlay uggestedthatsay ityay asway Mray. Atsbygay imselfhay, omecay outyay otay etermineday atwhay areshay ashisway ofyay ouryay ocallay eavens.Ihay ecidedday otay allcay otay imhay. Issmay Akerbay adhay entionedmay imhay atyay innerday, andthatyay ouldway oday orfay anyay introductionyay. Utbay Iyay idn’tday allcay otay imhay, orfay egavehay ayay uddensay intimationyay atthay ehay asway ontentcay otay ebay alone—heyay stretchedoutay ishay armsyay owardtay ethay arkday aterway inyay ayay uriouscay ayway, andyay, arfay asyay Iyay asfromway imhay, Iyay ouldcay avehay ornsway ehay asway emblingtray. Involuntarilyyay Iyay ancedseaward—andglay istinguishedday othingnay exceptyay ayay inglesay eengray ightlay, inuteandmay arfay awayyay, atthay ightmay avehay eenbay ethay endyay ofyay ayay ockday. Enwhay Iyay ookedoncelay oremay orfay Atsbygay ehay adhay anishedvay, andyay Iyay asway aloneyay againyay inyay eunquietthay arknessday. IIAboutyay alfwayhay etweenbay Estway Eggyay andyay Ewnay Orkyay ethay otormay oadray astilyjoinshay ethay ailroadray andyay unsray esidebay ityay orfay ayay uarterqay ofyay ayay ilemay, osay astoyay shrinkay awayyay omfray ayay ertaincay esolateday areayay ofyay andlay. Isthay isyay ayay alleyofvay ashes—ayay antasticfay armfay erewhay ashesyay owgray ikelay eatwhay intoyay idgesray andhillsyay andyay otesquegray ardens;gay erewhay ashesyay aketay ethay ormsfay ofyay ouseshay andchimneysyay andyay isingray okesmay andyay, inallyfay, ithway ayay anscendenttray effortyay, ofash-greyyay enmay, owhay ovemay imlyday andyay alreadyyay umblingcray throughay ethay owderyairpay. Occasionallyyay ayay inelay ofyay eygray arscay awlscray alongyay anyay invisibleyay ack,givestray outyay ayay astlyghay eakcray, andyay omescay otay estray, andyay immediatelyyay eash-greythay enmay armsway upyay ithway eadenlay adesspay andyay irstay upyay anyay impenetrablecloudyay, ichwhay screensay eirthay obscureyay operationsyay omfray ouryay ight.Butsay aboveyay ethay eygray andlay andyay ethay asmsspay ofyay eakblay ustday ichwhay iftendlesslydray overyay ityay, ouyay erceivepay, afteryay ayay omentmay, ethay eyesyay ofyay Octorday T.Jay. Eckleburgyay. Ethay eyesyay ofyay Octorday Tay. Jay. Eckleburgyay areyay ueblay andgigantic—theiryay etinasray areyay oneyay ardyay ighhay. Eythay ooklay outyay ofyay onay ace,butfay, insteadyay, omfray ayay airpay ofyay enormousyay ellowyay ectaclesspay ichwhay assoverpay ayay onexistentnay osenay. Evidentlyyay omesay ildway agway ofyay anyay oculistyay etthemsay erethay otay attenfay ishay acticepray inyay ethay oroughbay ofyay Ueensqay, andyay ensankthay ownday imselfhay intoyay eternalyay indnessblay, oryay orgotfay emthay andyay ovedawaymay. Utbay ishay eyesyay, immedday ayay ittlelay byay anymay aintlesspay aysday, underyay unandsay ainray, oodbray onyay overyay ethay olemnsay umpingday ound.Thegray alleyvay ofyay ashesyay isyay oundedbay onyay oneyay idesay byay ayay allsmay oulfay iverray, and,whenyay ethay awbridgedray isyay upyay otay etlay argesbay throughay, ethay assengerspay onwaitingyay ainstray ancay arestay atyay ethay ismalday enescay orfay asyay onglay asyay alfhay anhouryay. Erethay isyay alwaysyay ayay althay erethay ofyay atyay eastlay ayay inutemay, andyay ityay asbecauseway ofyay isthay atthay Iyay irstfay etmay Omtay Uchanan’sbay istress.Themay actfay atthay ehay adhay oneyay asway insistedyay uponyay ereverwhay ehay asway ownknay. Isacquaintanceshay esentedray ethay actfay atthay ehay urnedtay upyay inyay opularpay aféswithcay erhay andyay, eavinglay erhay atyay ayay abletay, aunteredsay aboutyay, attingchay ithwhomsoeverway ehay ewknay. Oughthay Iyay asway uriouscay otay eesay erhay, Iyay adhay onay esiretoday eetmay er—buthay Iyay idday. Iyay entway upyay otay Ewnay Orkyay ithway Omtay onyay ethay aintray oneafternoonyay, andyay enwhay eway oppedstay byay ethay ash-heapsyay ehay umpedjay otay ishay eetandfay, akingtay oldhay ofyay myay elbowyay, iterallylay orcedfay emay omfray ethay ar.“We’recay ettinggay off,”yay ehay insistedyay. “Iay antway ouyay otay eetmay myay irl.”Igay inkthay e’dhay ankedtay upyay ayay oodgay ealday atyay uncheonlay, andyay ishay eterminationtoday avehay myay ompanycay orderedbay onyay iolencevay. Ethay upercilioussay assumptionwasyay atthay onyay Undaysay afternoonyay Iyay adhay othingnay etterbay otay o.Iday ollowedfay imhay overyay ayay owlay itewashedwhay ailroadray encefay, andyay eway alkedbackway ayay undredhay ardsyay alongyay ethay oadray underyay Octorday Eckleburg’spersistentyay arestay. Ethay onlyyay uildingbay inyay ightsay asway ayay allsmay ockblay ofyellowyay ickbray ittingsay onyay ethay edgeyay ofyay ethay asteway andlay, ayay ortsay ofyay ompactMaincay Streetay inisteringmay otay ityay, andyay ontiguouscay otay absolutelyyay othing.Onenay ofyay ethay threeay opsshay ityay ontainedcay asway orfay entray andyay anotheryay asway anall-nightyay estaurantray, approachedyay byay ayay ailtray ofyay ashes;yay ethay irdthay asway agarage—Repairsyay. Mrsay. Ilsonway asway irstfay oncernedcay ithway ethay ogday. Ayay eluctantelevatorray oybay entway orfay ayay oxbay ullfay ofyay straway andyay omesay ilkmay, otay ichwhay eaddedhay onyay ishay ownyay initiativeyay ayay intay ofyay argelay, ardhay ogday iscuits—onebay ofwhichyay ecomposedday apatheticallyyay inyay ethay aucersay ofyay ilkmay allafternoonyay. Eanwhilemay Omtay oughtbray outyay ayay ottlebay ofyay iskywhay omfray ayay ockedbureaulay oor.Iday avehay eenbay unkdray ustjay icetway inyay myay ifelay, andyay ethay econdsay imetay asway atafternoon;thay osay everythingyay atthay appenedhay ashay ayay imday, azyhay astcay overyay it,althoughyay untilyay afteryay eightyay o’clockyay ethay apartmentyay asway ullfay ofyay eerfulsunchay. Ittingsay onyay Om’stay aplay Mrsay. Ilsonway alledcay upyay everalsay eoplepay onyay etelephone;thay enthay erethay ereway onay igarettescay, andyay Iyay entway outyay otay uybay omeatsay ethay ugstoredray onyay ethay ornercay. Enwhay Iyay amecay ackbay eythay adhay othdisappearedbay, osay Iyay atsay ownday iscreetlyday inyay ethay iving-roomlay andyay eadray achapteryay ofyay Imonsay Alledcay Eter—eitherpay ityay asway erribletay uffstay oryay ewhiskythay istortedday ingsthay, ecausebay ityay idn’tday akemay anyyay ensesay otay e.Justmay asyay Omtay andyay Myrtleay after(ay ethay irstfay inkdray Mrsay. Ilsonway andyay Iyay alledeachcay otheryay byay ouryay irstfay amesnay) eappearedray, ompanycay ommencedcay otay arriveatyay ethay apartmentyay oor.Theday istersay, Atherinecay, asway ayay enderslay, orldlyway irlgay ofyay aboutyay irty,withthay ayay olidsay, ickystay obbay ofyay edray airhay, andyay ayay omplexioncay owderedpay ilkywhitemay. Erhay eyebrowsyay adhay eenbay uckedplay andyay enthay awndray onyay againyay atyay ayay orerakishmay angleyay, utbay ethay effortsyay ofyay aturenay owardtay ethay estorationray ofyay eoldthay alignmentyay avegay ayay urredblay airyay otay erhay acefay. Enwhay eshay ovedmay aboutthereyay asway anyay incessantyay ickingclay asyay innumerableyay otterypay aceletsjingledbray upyay andyay ownday uponyay erhay armsyay. Eshay amecay inyay ithway uchsay ayay oprietaryhastepray, andyay ookedlay aroundyay osay ossessivelypay atyay ethay urniturefay atthay Iwonderedyay ifyay eshay ivedlay erehay. Utbay enwhay Iyay askedyay erhay eshay aughedimmoderatelylay, epeatedray myay uestionqay aloudyay, andyay oldtay emay eshay ivedlay ithway agirlyay iendfray atyay ayay otel.Mrhay. McKeeay asway ayay alepay, emininefay anmay omfray ethay atflay elowbay. Ehay adhay ustshavedjay, orfay erethay asway ayay itewhay otspay ofyay atherlay onyay ishay eekbonechay, andyay ewashay ostmay espectfulray inyay ishay eetinggray otay everyoneyay inyay ethay oomray. Einformedhay emay atthay ehay asway inyay ethay artistic“ay ame,”gay andyay Iyay atheredgay aterthatlay ehay asway ayay otographerphay andyay adhay ademay ethay imday enlargementyay ofMrsyay. Ilson’sway othermay ichwhay overedhay ikelay anyay ectoplasmyay onyay ethay allway. Iswifehay asway shrillay, anguidlay, andsomehay, andyay orriblehay. Eshay oldtay emay ithprideway atthay erhay usbandhay adhay otographedphay erhay ayay undredhay andyay enty-seventimestway incesay eythay adhay eenbay arried.Mrsmay. Ilsonway adhay angedchay erhay ostumecay omesay imetay eforebay, andyay asway owattirednay inyay anyay elaborateyay afternoonyay essdray ofyay eam-colouredcray iffon,whichchay avegay outyay ayay ontinualcay ustleray asyay eshay eptsway aboutyay ethay oomray. Iththeway influenceyay ofyay ethay essdray erhay ersonalitypay adhay alsoyay undergoneyay achangeyay. Ethay intenseyay italityvay atthay adhay eenbay osay emarkableray inyay ethay aragewasgay onvertedcay intoyay impressiveyay auteurhay. Erhay aughterlay, erhay esturesgay, erassertionshay ecamebay oremay iolentlyvay affectedyay omentmay byay omentmay, andyay asyay eexpandedshay ethay oomray ewgray allersmay aroundyay erhay, untilyay eshay eemedsay otay erevolvingbay onyay ayay oisynay, eakingcray ivotpay throughay ethay okysmay air.“Myyay ear,”day eshay oldtay erhay istersay inyay ayay ighhay, incingmay outshay, ost“may oftheseyay ellasfay illway eatchay ouyay everyyay imetay. Allyay eythay inkthay ofyay isyay oneymay. Ihadyay ayay omanway upyay erehay astlay eekway otay ooklay atyay myay eetfay, andyay enwhay eshay avegay ethemay illbay ou’dyay ofyay oughtthay eshay adhay myay appendicitisyay out.”“Whatyay asway ethay amenay ofyay ethay oman?”way askedyay Mrsay. McKee.“Mrsay. Eberhardtyay. Eshay oesgay aroundyay ookinglay atyay eople’spay eetfay inyay eirthay ownhomes.”“Iyay ikelay ouryay ess,”dray emarkedray Mrsay. McKeeay, “Iay inkthay it’syay adorable.”Mrsyay. Ilsonway ejectedray ethay omplimentcay byay aisingray erhay eyebrowyay inyay isdain.“It’sday ustjay ayay azycray oldyay ing,”thay eshay aidsay. “Iay ustjay ipslay ityay onyay ometimeswhensay Iyay on’tday arecay atwhay Iyay ooklay ike.”“Butlay ityay ookslay onderfulway onyay ouyay, ifyay ouyay owknay atwhay Iyay ean,”may ursuedpay Mrs.McKeeay. “Ifay Esterchay ouldcay onlyyay etgay ouyay inyay atthay osepay Iyay inkthay ehay ouldmakecay omethingsay ofyay it.”Weyay allyay ookedlay inyay ilencesay atyay Mrsay. Ilsonway, owhay emovedray ayay stranday ofyay airfromhay overyay erhay eyesyay andyay ookedlay ackbay atyay usyay ithway ayay illiantbray ilesmay. Mr.McKeeay egardedray erhay intentlyyay ithway ishay eadhay onyay oneyay idesay, andyay enthay ovedhismay andhay ackbay andyay orthfay owlyslay inyay ontfray ofyay ishay ace.“Ifay ouldshay angechay ethay ight,”lay ehay aidsay afteryay ayay omentmay. “I’day ikelay obringtay outyay ethay odellingmay ofyay ethay eaturesfay. Andyay I’dyay tryay otay etgay oldhay ofallyay ethay ackbay air.”“Ihay ouldn’tway inkthay ofyay angingchay ethay ight,”lay iedcray Mrsay. McKeeay. “Iay inkit’s—”Herthay usbandhay aidsay “Sh!”ay andyay eway allyay ookedlay atyay ethay ubjectsay again,whereuponyay Omtay Uchananbay awnedyay audiblyyay andyay otgay otay ishay eet.“Youfay McKeesay avehay omethingsay otay ink,”dray ehay aidsay. et“Gay omesay oremay iceyay andmineralyay aterway, Myrtleay, eforebay everybodyyay oesgay otay eep.”“Islay oldtay atthay oybay aboutyay ethay ice.”yay Myrtleay aisedray erhay eyebrowsyay inyay espairatday ethay iftlessnessshay ofyay ethay owerlay ordersyay. “Theseay eoplepay! Ouyay avehay okeeptay afteryay emthay allyay ethay ime.”Shetay ookedlay atyay emay andyay aughedlay ointlesslypay. McKee.Tomay ookedlay atyay imhay ankly.“Twoblay ofyay emthay eway avehay amedfray ownstairs.”“Twoday at?”whay emandedday Om.“Twotay udiesstay. Ityay amecay omfray Myrtleay, owhay adoverheardhay ethay uestionqay, andyay ityay asway iolentvay andyay obscene.“Youyay ee,”say iedcray Atherinecay iumphantlytray. E’sshay ayay Atholiccay, andtheyyay on’tday elievebay inyay ivorce.”Daisyday asway otnay ayay Atholiccay, andyay Iyay asway ayay ittlelay ockedshay atyay eelaboratenessthay ofyay ethay ie.“Whenlay eythay oday etgay arried,”may ontinuedcay Atherinecay, “they’reay oinggay Esttoway ivelay orfay ayay ilewhay untilyay ityay owsblay over.”“It’dyay ebay oremay iscreetday otay ogay otay Europe.”“Ohyay, oday ouyay ikelay Europe?”yay eshay exclaimedyay urprisinglysay. “Iay ustjay otgay ackfrombay Ontemay Arlo.”“Really.”“Justcay astlay earyay. Iyay entway overyay erethay ithway anotheryay irl.”“Staygay ong?”“Nolay, eway ustjay entway otay Ontemay Arlocay andyay ackbay. Eway entway byay ayway ofMarseillesyay. Everybodyyay eptkay ayingsay otay emay: ucille‘Lay, atthay an’smay ayway elowyou!’bay Utbay ifyay Iyay adn’thay etmay Esterchay, e’dhay ofyay otgay emay ure.”“Yessay, utbay isten,”lay aidsay Myrtleay Ilsonway, oddingnay erhay eadhay upyay andyay own,“atday eastlay ouyay idn’tday arrymay im.”“Ihay owknay Iyay idn’t.”“Wellday, Iyay arriedmay im,”hay aidsay Myrtleay, ambiguouslyyay. “Anday at’sthay edifferencethay etweenbay ouryay asecay andyay ine.”“Whymay idday ouyay, Myrtle?”ay emandedday Atherinecay. obody“Nay orcedfay ouyay o.”Myrtletay onsidered.“Icay arriedmay imhay ecausebay Iyay oughtthay ehay asway ayay entleman,”gay eshay aidfinallysay. “Iay oughtthay ehay ewknay omethingsay aboutyay eedingbray, utbay ehay asn’tfitway otay icklay myay oe.”“Youshay ereway azycray aboutyay imhay orfay ayay ile,”whay aidsay Atherine.“Crazycay aboutyay im!”hay iedcray Myrtleay incredulouslyyay. “Whoay aidsay Iyay asway azyaboutcray imhay? Iyay evernay asway anyyay oremay azycray aboutyay imhay anthay Iyay asway aboutyay atmanthay ere.”Shethay ointedpay uddenlysay atyay emay, andyay everyoneyay ookedlay atyay emay accusinglyyay. Ehay orrowedbay omebody’ssay estbay uitsay otay etgay arriedmay inyay, andneveryay evenyay oldtay emay aboutyay ityay, andyay ethay anmay amecay afteryay ityay oneyay ayday enwhay ewashay outyay: ‘Ohay, isyay atthay ouryay uit?’say Iyay aidsay. ‘Thisay isyay ethay irstfay Iyay everheardyay aboutyay it.’yay Utbay Iyay avegay ityay otay imhay andyay enthay Iyay aylay ownday andyay iedcray obeattay ethay andbay allyay afternoon.”“Sheyay eallyray oughtyay otay etgay awayyay omfray im,”hay esumedray Atherinecay otay e.“They’vemay eenbay ivinglay overyay atthay aragegay orfay elevenyay earsyay. Andyay Om’stay efirstthay eetiesway eshay everyay ad.”Thehay ottlebay ofyay isky—awhay econdsay one—wasyay ownay inyay onstantcay emandday byay allpresentyay, exceptingyay Atherinecay, owhay elt“fay ustjay asyay oodgay onyay othingnay atall.”yay Omtay angray orfay ethay anitorjay andyay entsay imhay orfay omesay elebratedsandwichescay, ichwhay ereway ayay ompletecay uppersay inyay emselvesthay. Iyay antedway ogettay outyay andyay alkway eastwardyay owardtay ethay arkpay throughay ethay oftsay ilight,buttway eachyay imetay Iyay iedtray otay ogay Iyay ecamebay entangledyay inyay omesay ildway, stridentargumentay ichwhay ulledpay emay ackbay, asyay ifyay ithway opesray, intoyay myay airchay. Ethighyay overyay ethay itycay ouryay inelay ofyay ellowyay indowsway ustmay avehay ontributedtheircay areshay ofyay umanhay ecrecysay otay ethay asualcay atcherway inyay ethay arkeningstreetsday, andyay Iyay awsay imhay ootay, ookinglay upyay andyay onderingway. Iyay asway ithinway andwithoutyay, imultaneouslysay enchantedyay andyay epelledray byay ethay inexhaustiblevarietyyay ofyay ife.Myrtlelay ulledpay erhay airchay oseclay otay inemay, andyay uddenlysay erhay armway eathpouredbray overyay emay ethay orystay ofyay erhay irstfay eetingmay ithway Om.“Ittay asway onyay ethay otway ittlelay eatssay acingfay eachyay otheryay atthay areyay alwaysyay elastthay onesyay eftlay onyay ethay aintray. Iyay asway oinggay upyay otay Ewnay Orkyay otay eesay mysisteray andyay endspay ethay ightnay. Ehay adhay onyay ayay essdray uitsay andyay atentpay eathershoeslay, andyay Iyay ouldn’tcay eepkay myay eyesyay offyay imhay, utbay everyyay imetay ehay ookedatlay emay Iyay adhay otay etendpray otay ebay ookinglay atyay ethay advertisementyay overyay isheadhay. Enwhay eway amecay intoyay ethay ationstay ehay asway extnay otay emay, andyay ishay iteshirtfrontwhay essedpray againstyay myay armyay, andyay osay Iyay oldtay imhay I’dyay avehay otay allacay olicemanpay, utbay ehay ewknay Iyay iedlay. Iyay asway osay excitedyay atthay enwhay Iyay otgay intoayay axitay ithway imhay Iyay idn’tday ardlyhay owknay Iyay asn’tway ettinggay intoyay ayay ubwaytrainsay. Allyay Iyay eptkay inkingthay aboutyay, overyay andyay overyay, asway ou‘Yay an’tcay iveforever;lay ouyay an’tcay ivelay orever.’ ”Shefay urnedtay otay Mrsay. McKeeay andyay ethay oomray angray ullfay ofyay erhay artificiallaughter.“Myyay ear,”day eshay iedcray, “I’may oinggay otay ivegay ouyay isthay essdray asyay oonsay asyay I’mthroughyay ithway ityay. I’veyay otgay otay etgay anotheryay oneyay omorrowtay. I’myay oinggay omaketay ayay istlay ofyay allyay ethay ingsthay I’veyay otgay otay etgay. Ayay assagemay andyay ayay ave,andway ayay ollarcay orfay ethay ogday, andyay oneyay ofyay osethay utecay ittlelay ashtraysyay ereyouwhay ouchtay ayay springay, andyay ayay eathwray ithway ayay ackblay ilksay owbay orfay other’sgravemay at’llthay astlay allyay ummersay. Iyay otgay otay itewray ownday ayay istlay osay Iyay on’tforgetway allyay ethay ingsthay Iyay otgay otay o.”Itday asway inenay o’clock—almostyay immediatelyyay afterwardyay Iyay ookedlay atyay myay atchandway oundfay ityay asway entay. Mray. McKeeay asway asleepyay onyay ayay airchay ithway ishay istsclenchedfay inyay ishay aplay, ikelay ayay otographphay ofyay ayay anmay ofyay actionyay. Akingtay outmyyay andkerchiefhay Iyay ipedway omfray ishay eekchay ethay otspay ofyay ieddray atherlay athadthay orriedway emay allyay ethay afternoon.Theyay ittlelay ogday asway ittingsay onyay ethay abletay ookinglay ithway indblay eyesthroughyay ethay okesmay, andyay omfray imetay otay imetay oaninggray aintlyfay. Eopledisappearedpay, eappearedray, ademay ansplay otay ogay omewheresay, andyay enthay osteachlay otheryay, earchedsay orfay eachyay otheryay, oundfay eachyay otheryay ayay ewfay eetawayfay. Omesay imetay owardtay idnightmay Omtay Uchananbay andyay Mrsay. Ilsonway oodfacestay otay acefay iscussingday, inyay impassionedyay oicesvay, etherwhay Mrsay. Ilsonhadway anyyay ightray otay entionmay Aisy’sday ame.“Daisynay! Aisyday! Aisy!”day outedshay Mrsay. Ilsonway. “I’llay aysay ityay eneverwhay Iwantyay otay! Aisyday! Ai—”Makingday ayay ortshay eftday ovementmay, Omtay Uchananbay okebray erhay osenay ithway isopenhay and.Thenhay erethay ereway oodyblay owelstay uponyay ethay athroombay oorflay, andyay omen’svoicesway oldingscay, andyay ighhay overyay ethay onfusioncay ayay onglay okenbray ailway ofpainyay. Mray. McKeeay awokeyay omfray ishay ozeday andyay artedstay inyay ayay azeday owardtay edoorthay. Enwhay ehay adhay onegay alfwayhay ehay urnedtay aroundyay andyay aredstay atyay escene—histhay ifeway andyay Atherinecay oldingscay andyay onsolingcay asyay eythay umbledherestay andyay erethay amongyay ethay owdedcray urniturefay ithway articlesyay ofyay aidyay, andtheyay espairingday igurefay onyay ethay ouchcay, eedingblay uentlyflay, andyay tryingay ospreadtay ayay opycay ofyay Owntay Attletay overyay ethay apestrytay enesscay ofVersaillesyay. Enthay Mray. McKeeay urnedtay andyay ontinuedcay onyay outyay ethay oor.Takingday myay athay omfray ethay andelierchay, Iyay ollowed.“Comefay otay unchlay omesay ay,”day ehay uggestedsay, asyay eway oanedgray ownday inyay eelevator.“Where?”“Anywhere.”“Keepthay ouryay andshay offyay ethay ever,”lay appedsnay ethay elevatoryay oy.“Ibay egbay ouryay ardon,”pay aidsay Mray. McKeeay ithway ignityday, “Iay idn’tday owknay Iyay astouchingway it.”“Allyay ight,”ray Iyay agreedyay, “I’llay ebay adglay o.”…tay Iyay asway andingstay esidebay ishay edbay andyay ehay asway ittingsay upyay etweenbay esheetsthay, adclay inyay ishay underwearyay, ithway ayay eatgray ortfoliopay inyay ishay ands.“Beautyhay andyay ethay Eastbay …ay Onelinesslay …ay Oldyay Ocerygray Orsehay …ay Ook’nBridgebray …”Thenay Iyay asway inglyay alfhay asleepyay inyay ethay oldcay owerlay evellay ofyay ePennsylvaniathay Ationstay, aringstay atyay ethay orningmay Ibunetray, andyay aitingway orthefay ourfay o’clockyay aintray. IIIThereyay asway usicmay omfray myay eighbour’snay ousehay throughay ethay ummersay ights.Innay ishay ueblay ardensgay enmay andyay irlsgay amecay andyay entway ikelay othsmay amongyay ewhisperingsthay andyay ethay ampagnechay andyay ethay arsstay. Atyay ighhay idetay inyay eafternoonthay Iyay atchedway ishay uestsgay ivingday omfray ethay owertay ofyay ishay aftray, ortakingyay ethay unsay onyay ethay othay andsay ofyay ishay eachbay ilewhay ishay otway otorboatsslitmay ethay atersway ofyay ethay Oundsay, awingdray aquaplanesyay overyay ataractscay offoamyay. Onyay eekendsway ishay Olls-Royceray ecamebay anyay omnibusyay, earingbay artiestopay andyay omfray ethay itycay etweenbay inenay inyay ethay orningmay andyay onglay astmidnightpay, ilewhay ishay ationstay agonway amperedscay ikelay ayay iskbray ellowyay ugbay omeettay allyay ainstray. Andyay onyay Ondaysmay eightyay ervantssay, includingyay anyay extragardeneryay, oiledtay allyay ayday ithway opsmay andyay scrubbing-brushesay andyay ammersandhay arden-shearsgay, epairingray ethay avagesray ofyay ethay ightnay efore.Everybay Idayfray ivefay atescray ofyay orangesyay andyay emonslay arrivedyay omfray afruitereryay inyay Ewnay Ork—everyyay Ondaymay esethay amesay orangesyay andyay emonslay efthislay ackbay oorday inyay ayay pyramiday ofyay ulplesspay alveshay. Erethay asway ayay achinemay intheyay itchenkay ichwhay ouldcay extractyay ethay uicejay ofyay otway undredhay orangesyay inhalfyay anyay ourhay ifyay ayay ittlelay uttonbay asway essedpray otway undredhay imestay byay abutler’syay umb.Atthay eastlay onceyay ayay ortnightfay ayay orpscay ofyay atererscay amecay ownday ithway everalhundredsay eetfay ofyay anvascay andyay enoughyay olouredcay ightslay otay akemay ayay Christmastreeay ofyay Atsby’sgay enormousyay ardengay. Onyay uffetbay ablestay, arnishedgay ithglisteningway ors-d’oeuvrehay, icedspay akedbay amshay owdedcray againstyay aladssay ofharlequinyay esignsday andyay astrypay igspay andyay urkeystay ewitchedbay otay ayay arkgoldday. Inyay ethay ainmay allhay ayay arbay ithway ayay ealray assbray ailray asway etsay upyay, andstockedyay ithway insgay andyay iquorslay andyay ithway ordialscay osay onglay orgottenfay atmostthay ofyay ishay emalefay uestsgay ereway ootay oungyay otay owknay oneyay omfray another.Byyay evensay o’clockyay ethay orchestrayay ashay arrivedyay, onay inthay ive-piecefay affair,butyay ayay olewhay itfulpay ofyay oboesyay andyay ombonestray andyay axophonessay andyay iolsvay andcornetsyay andyay iccolospay, andyay owlay andyay ighhay umsdray. Ethay astlay immerssway avecomehay inyay omfray ethay eachbay ownay andyay areyay essingdray upstairs;yay ethay arscay omNewfray Orkyay areyay arkedpay ivefay eepday inyay ethay ivedray, andyay alreadyyay ethay allshay andsalonsyay andyay erandasvay areyay audygay ithway imarypray olourscay, andyay airhay obbedbay instrangeyay ewnay aysway, andyay awlsshay eyondbay ethay eamsdray ofyay Astilecay. Ethay arbay isinyay ullfay ingsway, andyay oatingflay oundsray ofyay ocktailscay ermeatepay ethay ardenoutsidegay, untilyay ethay airyay isyay aliveyay ithway atterchay andyay aughterlay, andyay asualinnuendocay andyay introductionsyay orgottenfay onyay ethay otspay, andyay enthusiasticmeetingsyay etweenbay omenway owhay evernay ewknay eachyay other’syay ames.Thenay ightslay owgray ighterbray asyay ethay earthyay urcheslay awayyay omfray ethay unsay, andnowyay ethay orchestrayay isyay ayingplay ellowyay ocktailcay usicmay, andyay ethay operayay ofvoicesyay itchespay ayay eykay igherhay. Aughterlay isyay easieryay inutemay byay inute,spilledmay ithway odigalitypray, ippedtay outyay atyay ayay eerfulchay ordway. Ethay oupschangegray oremay iftlysway, ellsway ithway ewnay arrivalsyay, issolveday andyay ormfay inyay esamethay eath;bray alreadyyay erethay areyay anderersway, onfidentcay irlsgay owhay eavehereway andyay erethay amongyay ethay outerstay andyay oremay ablestay, ecomebay orfay ayay arp,joyousshay omentmay ethay entrecay ofyay ayay oupgray, andyay enthay, excitedyay ithway iumph,glidetray onyay throughay ethay ea-changesay ofyay acesfay andyay oicesvay andyay olourcay undertheyay onstantlycay angingchay ight.Suddenlylay oneyay ofyay esethay gypsiesay, inyay emblingtray opalyay, eizessay ayay ocktailoutcay ofyay ethay airyay, umpsday ityay ownday orfay ouragecay andyay, ovingmay erhay andshay ikeFriscolay, ancesday outyay aloneyay onyay ethay anvascay atformplay. Ayay omentarymay ush;hay eorchestrathay eaderlay ariesvay ishay rhythmay obliginglyyay orfay erhay, andyay erethay isyay aburstyay ofyay atterchay asyay ethay erroneousyay ewsnay oesgay aroundyay atthay eshay isyay IldaGray’sgay understudyyay omfray ethay Olliesfay. Ethay artypay ashay egun.Ibay elievebay atthay onyay ethay irstfay ightnay Iyay entway otay Atsby’sgay ousehay Iyay asway oneofyay ethay ewfay uestsgay owhay adhay actuallyyay eenbay invitedyay. Eoplepay ereway otinvited—theynay entway erethay. Eythay otgay intoyay automobilesyay ichwhay orebay emthay outtoyay Onglay Islandyay, andyay omehowsay eythay endedyay upyay atyay Atsby’sgay oorday. Onceyay eretheythay ereway introducedyay byay omebodysay owhay ewknay Atsbygay, andyay afteryay atthay eyconductedthay emselvesthay accordingyay otay ethay ulesray ofyay ehaviourbay associatedwithyay anyay amusementyay arkpay. Ometimessay eythay amecay andyay entway ithoutway avingmethay Atsbygay atyay allyay, amecay orfay ethay artypay ithway ayay implicitysay ofyay earthay atwasthay itsyay ownyay ickettay ofyay admission.Iyay adhay eenbay actuallyyay invitedyay. Ayay auffeurchay inyay ayay uniformyay ofyay obin’s-eggblueray ossedcray myay awnlay earlyyay atthay Aturdaysay orningmay ithway ayay urprisinglyformalsay otenay omfray ishay employeryay: ethay onourhay ouldway ebay entirelyyay Atsby’s,itgay aidsay, ifyay Iyay ouldway attendyay ishay ittle“lay arty”pay atthay ightnay. Ehay adhay eenmesay everalsay imestay, andyay adhay intendedyay otay allcay onyay emay onglay eforebay, utbay apeculiaryay ombinationcay ofyay ircumstancescay adhay eventedpray it—signedyay AyGatsbyjay, inyay ayay ajesticmay and.Dressedhay upyay inyay itewhay annelsflay Iyay entway overyay otay ishay awnlay ayay ittlelay aftersevenyay, andyay anderedway aroundyay atherray illyay atyay easeyay amongyay irlssway andyay eddiesofyay eoplepay Iyay idn’tday ow—thoughknay erehay andyay erethay asway ayay acefay Iyay adhay oticedonnay ethay ommutingcay aintray. Iyay asway immediatelyyay struckay byay ethay umbernay ofyoungyay Englishmenyay ottedday about;yay allyay ellway esseddray, allyay ookinglay ayay ittlehungrylay, andyay allyay alkingtay inyay owlay, earnestyay oicesvay otay olidsay andyay osperousAmericanspray. Iyay asway uresay atthay eythay ereway ellingsay omethingsay: ondsbay orinsuranceyay oryay automobilesyay. Eythay ereway atyay eastlay agonizinglyyay awareyay ofyay eeasythay oneymay inyay ethay icinityvay andyay onvincedcay atthay ityay asway eirsthay orfay ayay ewwordsfay inyay ethay ightray ey.Askay oonsay asyay Iyay arrivedyay Iyay ademay anyay attemptyay otay indfay myay osthay, utbay ethay otway orthreeyay eoplepay ofyay omwhay Iyay askedyay ishay ereaboutswhay aredstay atyay emay inyay uchsay anamazedyay ayway, andyay eniedday osay ehementlyvay anyyay owledgeknay ofyay ishay ovements,thatmay Iyay unkslay offyay inyay ethay irectionday ofyay ethay ocktailcay able—thetay onlyyay aceinplay ethay ardengay erewhay ayay inglesay anmay ouldcay ingerlay ithoutway ookingpurposelesslay andyay alone.Iyay asway onyay myay ayway otay etgay oaringray unkdray omfray eershay embarrassmentyay enJordanwhay Akerbay amecay outyay ofyay ethay ousehay andyay oodstay atyay ethay eadhay ofyay ethay arblestepsmay, eaninglay ayay ittlelay ackwardbay andyay ookinglay ithway ontemptuousinterestcay ownday intoyay ethay arden.Welcomegay oryay otnay, Iyay oundfay ityay ecessarynay otay attachyay myselfay otay omeonebeforesay Iyay ouldshay eginbay otay addressyay ordialcay emarksray otay ethay assersby.“Hello!”pay Iyay oaredray, advancingyay owardtay erhay. Myay oicevay eemedsay unnaturallyloudyay acrossyay ethay arden.“Igay oughtthay ouyay ightmay ebay ere,”hay eshay espondedray absentlyyay asyay Iyay amecay up.“Iyay ememberedray ouyay ivedlay extnay oorday o—”Shetay eldhay myay andhay impersonallyyay, asyay ayay omisepray atthay e’dshay aketay arecay ofyay einmay ayay inutemay, andyay avegay earyay otay otway irlsgay inyay intway ellowyay essesdray, ostoppedwhay atyay ethay ootfay ofyay ethay eps.“Hello!”stay eythay iedcray ogethertay. orry“Say ouyay idn’tday in.”Thatway asway orfay ethay olfgay ournamenttay. Eshay adhay ostlay inyay ethay inalsfay ethay eekbefore.“Youway on’tday owknay owhay eway are,”yay aidsay oneyay ofyay ethay irlsgay inyay ellowyay, ut“bay emetway ouyay erehay aboutyay ayay onthmay ago.”“You’veyay eddyay ouryay airhay incesay en,”thay emarkedray Ordanjay, andyay Iyay arted,butstay ethay irlsgay adhay ovedmay asuallycay onyay andyay erhay emarkray asway addressedyay othetay ematurepray oonmay, oducedpray ikelay ethay uppersay, onay oubtday, outyay ofyay acaterer’syay asketbay. Ithway Ordan’sjay enderslay oldengay armyay estingray inyay inemay, edescendedway ethay epsstay andyay aunteredsay aboutyay ethay ardengay. Ayay aytray ofcocktailsyay oatedflay atyay usyay throughay ethay ilighttway, andyay eway atsay ownday atyay atableyay ithway ethay otway irlsgay inyay ellowyay andyay threeay enmay, eachyay oneyay introducedtoyay usyay asyay Mray. Ityay asway estimonytay otay ethay omanticspeculationray ehay inspiredyay atthay erethay ereway isperswhay aboutyay imhay omfray osewhothay adhay oundfay ittlelay atthay ityay asway ecessarynay otay isperwhay aboutyay inyay isworld.Thethay irstfay upper—theresay ouldway ebay anotheryay oneyay afteryay idnight—wasmay owbeingnay ervedsay, andyay Ordanjay invitedyay emay otay oinjay erhay ownyay artypay, owhay erespreadway aroundyay ayay abletay onyay ethay otheryay idesay ofyay ethay ardengay. Erethay erethreeway arriedmay ouplescay andyay Ordan’sjay escortyay, ayay ersistentpay undergraduategivenyay otay iolentvay innuendoyay, andyay obviouslyyay underyay ethay impressionyay atsoonerthay oryay aterlay Ordanjay asway oinggay otay ieldyay imhay upyay erhay ersonpay otay agreateryay oryay esserlay egreeday. Insteadyay ofyay amblingray, isthay artypay adpreservedhay ayay ignifiedday omogeneityhay, andyay assumedyay otay itselfyay ethay unctionoffay epresentingray ethay aidstay obilitynay ofyay ethay ountryside—Eastcay Eggcondescendingyay otay Estway Eggyay andyay arefullycay onyay uardgay againstyay itsspectroscopicyay aiety.“Let’sgay etgay out,”yay isperedwhay Ordanjay, afteryay ayay omehowsay astefulway andinappropriateyay alf-hour;hay “thisay isyay uchmay ootay olitepay orfay e.”Wemay otgay upyay, andyay eshay explainedyay atthay eway ereway oinggay otay indfay ethay osthay: Ihadyay evernay etmay imhay, eshay aidsay, andyay ityay asway akingmay emay uneasyyay. Eundergraduatethay oddednay inyay ayay cynicalay, elancholymay ay.Theway arbay, erewhay eway ancedglay irstfay, asway owdedcray, utbay Atsbygay asway ottherenay. Eshay ouldn’tcay indfay imhay omfray ethay optay ofyay ethay epsstay, andyay ehay asn’tonway ethay erandavay. Onyay ayay ancechay eway iedtray anyay important-lookingyay oorday, andwalkedyay intoyay ayay ighhay Othicgay ibrarylay, anelledpay ithway arvedcay Englishyay oak,andyay obablypray ansportedtray ompletecay omfray omesay uinray overseas.Ayay outstay, iddle-agedmay anmay, ithway enormousyay owl-eyedyay ectaclesspay, assittingway omewhatsay unkdray onyay ethay edgeyay ofyay ayay eatgray abletay, aringstay ithunsteadyway oncentrationcay atyay ethay elvesshay ofyay ooksbay. Ey’re—”“Youthay oldtay us.”Weyay ookshay andshay ithway imhay avelygray andyay entway ackbay outdoors.Thereyay asway ancingday ownay onyay ethay anvascay inyay ethay arden;gay oldyay enmay ushingyoungpay irlsgay ackwardbay inyay eternalyay acelessgray irclescay, uperiorsay ouplesholdingcay eachyay otheryay ortuouslytay, ashionablyfay, andyay eepingkay inyay ecorners—andthay ayay eatgray umbernay ofyay inglesay irlsgay ancingday individuallyyay orrelievingyay ethay orchestrayay orfay ayay omentmay ofyay ethay urdenbay ofyay ethay anjobay oryay etrapsthay. Byay idnightmay ethay ilarityhay adhay increasedyay. Ayay elebratedcay enortay adsunghay inyay Italianyay, andyay ayay otoriousnay ontraltocay adhay ungsay inyay azzjay, andbetweenyay ethay umbersnay eoplepay ereway oingday “stunts”ay allyay overyay ethay arden,whilegay appyhay, acuousvay urstsbay ofyay aughterlay oseray owardtay ethay ummersay skyay. Apairyay ofyay agestay instway, owhay urnedtay outyay otay ebay ethay irlsgay inyay ellowyay, idday ababyyay actyay inyay ostumecay, andyay ampagnechay asway ervedsay inyay assesglay iggerbay anfinger-bowlsthay. Ethay oonmay adhay isenray igherhay, andyay oatingflay inyay ethay Oundsay asaway iangletray ofyay ilversay alesscay, emblingtray ayay ittlelay otay ethay iffstay, innydriptay ofyay ethay anjoesbay onyay ethay awn.Ilay asway illstay ithway Ordanjay Akerbay. Eway ereway ittingsay atyay ayay abletay ithway ayay anofmay aboutyay myay ageyay andyay ayay owdyray ittlelay irlgay, owhay avegay ayway uponyay eslightestthay ovocationpray otay uncontrollableyay aughterlay. Ityay asway oneofyay osethay areray ilessmay ithway ayay ualityqay ofyay eternalyay eassuranceray inyay ityay, atyouthay aymay omecay acrossyay ourfay oryay ivefay imestay inyay ifelay. Ityay aced—orfay eemedsay oface—thetay olewhay eternalyay orldway orfay anyay instantyay, andyay enthay oncentratedcay onyouyay ithway anyay irresistibleyay ejudicepray inyay ouryay avourfay. Ityay understoodyay oujustyay osay arfay asyay ouyay antedway otay ebay understoodyay, elievedbay inyay ouyay asyay ouwouldyay ikelay otay elievebay inyay ourselfyay, andyay assuredyay ouyay atthay ityay adpreciselyhay ethay impressionyay ofyay ouyay atthay, atyay ouryay estbay, ouyay opedhay oconveytay. Eciselypray atyay atthay ointpay ityay anished—andvay Iyay asway ookinglay atyay anelegantyay oungyay oughneckray, ayay earyay oryay otway overyay irtythay, osewhay elaborateformalityyay ofyay eechspay ustjay issedmay eingbay absurdyay. Omesay imetay eforebay eintroducedhay imselfhay I’dyay otgay ayay strongay impressionyay atthay ehay asway ickingpay iswordshay ithway are.Almostcay atyay ethay omentmay enwhay Mray. Iyay illway ejoinray ouyay ater.”Whenlay ehay asway onegay Iyay urnedtay immediatelyyay otay Ordan—constrainedjay otay assureheryay ofyay myay urprisesay. Iyay adhay expectedyay atthay Mray. Iyay ancedglay ackbay onceyay. Ayay aferway ofyay amoonyay asway iningshay overyay Atsby’sgay ousehay, akingmay ethay ightnay inefay asyay efore,andbay urvivingsay ethay aughterlay andyay ethay oundsay ofyay ishay illstay owingglay arden.Agay uddensay emptinessyay eemedsay otay owflay ownay omfray ethay indowsway andyay ethay eatdoorsgray, endowingyay ithway ompletecay isolationyay ethay igurefay ofyay ethay osthay, ostoodwhay onyay ethay orchpay, ishay andhay upyay inyay ayay ormalfay esturegay ofyay arewell.------------------------------------------------------------------------Readingfay overyay atwhay Iyay avehay ittenwray osay arfay, Iyay eesay Iyay avehay ivengay eimpressionthay atthay ethay eventsyay ofyay threeay ightsnay everalsay eeksway apartyay ereallway atthay absorbedyay emay. Onyay ethay ontrarycay, eythay ereway erelymay asualcay eventsinyay ayay owdedcray ummersay, andyay, untilyay uchmay aterlay, eythay absorbedyay einfinitelymay esslay anthay myay ersonalpay affairs.Mostyay ofyay ethay imetay Iyay orkedway. Inyay ethay earlyyay orningmay ethay unsay threway myshadoway estwardway asyay Iyay urriedhay ownday ethay itewhay asmschay ofyay owerlay Ewnay Orktoyay ethay Obitypray Usttray. Iyay ewknay ethay otheryay erksclay andyay oungyay ond-salesmenbybay eirthay irstfay amesnay, andyay unchedlay ithway emthay inyay arkday, owdedrestaurantscray onyay ittlelay igpay ausagessay andyay ashedmay otatoespay andyay offeecay. Ievenyay adhay ayay ortshay affairyay ithway ayay irlgay owhay ivedlay inyay Erseyjay Itycay andworkedyay inyay ethay accountingyay epartmentday, utbay erhay otherbray eganbay throwingmeanay ookslay inyay myay irectionday, osay enwhay eshay entway onyay erhay acationvay inyay Ulyjay Iletyay ityay owblay uietlyqay away.Iyay ooktay innerday usuallyyay atyay ethay Aleyay Ub—forclay omesay easonray ityay asway egloomiestthay eventyay ofyay myay ay—andday enthay Iyay entway upstairsyay otay ethay ibrarylay andstudiedyay investmentsyay andyay ecuritiessay orfay ayay onscientiouscay ourhay. Erewerethay enerallygay ayay ewfay iotersray aroundyay, utbay eythay evernay amecay intoyay elibrarythay, osay ityay asway ayay oodgay aceplay otay orkway. Afteryay atthay, ifyay ethay ightnay asmellowway, Iyay strolleday ownday Adisonmay Avenueyay astpay ethay oldyay Urraymay Illhay Otel,andhay overyay 33rday Streetay otay ethay Ennsylvaniapay Ation.Istay eganbay otay ikelay Ewnay Orkyay, ethay acyray, adventurousyay eelfay ofyay ityay atyay ight,andnay ethay atisfactionsay atthay ethay onstantcay ickerflay ofyay enmay andyay omenway andmachinesyay ivesgay otay ethay estlessray eyeyay. Ometimessay, inyay myay indmay, Iyay ollowedfay emthay otay eirapartmentsthay onyay ethay ornerscay ofyay iddenhay streetsay, andyay eythay urnedtay andsmiledyay ackbay atyay emay eforebay eythay adedfay throughay ayay oorday intoyay armdarknessway. Atyay ethay enchantedyay etropolitanmay ilighttway Iyay eltfay ayay auntinglonelinesshay ometimessay, andyay eltfay ityay inyay others—pooryay oungyay erksclay oloiteredwhay inyay ontfray ofyay indowsway aitingway untilyay ityay asway imetay orfay ayay olitaryrestaurantsay inner—youngday erksclay inyay ethay uskday, astingway ethay ostmay oignantmomentspay ofyay ightnay andyay ife.Againlay atyay eightyay o’clockyay, enwhay ethay arkday aneslay ofyay ethay Ortiesfay ereway inedfivelay eepday ithway throbbingay axicabstay, oundbay orfay ethay eatrethay istrictday, Ifeltyay ayay inkingsay inyay myay earthay. Ormsfay eanedlay ogethertay inyay ethay axistay asyay eywaitedthay, andyay oicesvay angsay, andyay erethay asway aughterlay omfray unheardyay okes,andjay ightedlay igarettescay ademay unintelligibleyay irclescay insideyay. Imaginingthatyay Iyay, ootay, asway urryinghay owardstay aietygay andyay aringshay eirthay intimateexcitementyay, Iyay ishedway emthay ell.Forway ayay ilewhay Iyay ostlay ightsay ofyay Ordanjay Akerbay, andyay enthay inyay idsummermay Ifoundyay erhay againyay. Atyay irstfay Iyay asway atteredflay otay ogay acesplay ithway er,becausehay eshay asway ayay olfgay ampionchay, andyay everyoneyay ewknay erhay amenay. Enthay itwasyay omethingsay oremay. Iyay asn’tway actuallyyay inyay ovelay, utbay Iyay eltfay ayay ortsay oftenderyay uriositycay. Ethay oredbay aughtyhay acefay atthay eshay urnedtay otay ethay orldconcealedway omething—mostsay affectationsyay oncealcay omethingsay eventually,evenyay oughthay eythay on’tday inyay ethay eginning—andbay oneyay ayday Iyay oundfay atwhay itwasyay. Enwhay eway ereway onyay ayay ouse-partyhay ogethertay upyay inyay Arwickway, eshay eftlay aborrowedyay arcay outyay inyay ethay ainray ithway ethay optay ownday, andyay enthay iedlay aboutit—andyay uddenlysay Iyay ememberedray ethay orystay aboutyay erhay atthay adhay eludedyay ethatmay ightnay atyay Aisy’sday. Atyay erhay irstfay igbay olfgay ournamenttay erethay asway arowyay atthay earlynay eachedray ethay ewspapers—anay uggestionsay atthay eshay adhay ovedhermay allbay omfray ayay adbay ielay inyay ethay emifinalsay oundray. Ayay addycay etractedray isstatementhay, andyay ethay onlyyay otheryay itnessway admittedyay atthay ehay ightmay avehay eenmistakenbay. Ethay incidentyay andyay ethay amenay adhay emainedray ogethertay inyay myay ind.Jordanmay Akerbay instinctivelyyay avoidedyay everclay, shrewday enmay, andyay ownay Iyay awthatsay isthay asway ecausebay eshay eltfay afersay onyay ayay aneplay erewhay anyyay ivergencefromday ayay odecay ouldway ebay oughtthay impossibleyay. Eshay asway incurablyyay ishonest.Sheday asn’tway ableyay otay endureyay eingbay atyay ayay isadvantageday andyay, ivengay isunwillingnessthay, Iyay upposesay eshay adhay egunbay ealingday inyay ubterfugessay enwhay ewasshay eryvay oungyay inyay orderyay otay eepkay atthay oolcay, insolentyay ilesmay urnedtay othetay orldway andyay etyay atisfysay ethay emandsday ofyay erhay ardhay, auntyjay ody.Itbay ademay onay ifferenceday otay emay. Ityay artedstay ecausebay eshay assedpay osay oseclay otay omesay orkmenway atthay ourfenderyay ickedflay ayay uttonbay onyay oneyay an’smay oat.“You’recay ayay ottenray iver,”dray Iyay otestedpray. ither“Eay ouyay oughtyay otay ebay orecarefulmay, oryay ouyay oughtn’tyay otay ivedray atyay all.”“Iyay amyay areful.”“Nocay, ou’reyay ot.”“Wellnay, otheryay eoplepay are,”yay eshay aidsay ightly.“What’slay atthay otgay otay oday ithway it?”“They’llyay eepkay outyay ofyay myay ay,”way eshay insistedyay. “Itay akestay otway otay akemay anaccident.”“Supposeyay ouyay etmay omebodysay ustjay asyay arelesscay asyay ourself.”“Iyay opehay Iyay evernay ill,”way eshay answeredyay. “Iay atehay arelesscay eoplepay. At’swhythay Iyay ikelay ou.”Heryay eygray, un-strainedsay eyesyay aredstay straightay aheadyay, utbay eshay addeliberatelyhay iftedshay ouryay elationsray, andyay orfay ayay omentmay Iyay oughtthay Iyay ovedherlay. Utbay Iyay amyay ow-thinkingslay andyay ullfay ofyay interioryay ulesray atthay actyay asbrakesyay onyay myay esiresday, andyay Iyay ewknay atthay irstfay Iyay adhay otay etgay myselfdefinitelyay outyay ofyay atthay angletay ackbay omehay. I’dyay eenbay itingwray etterslay onceayay eekway andyay igningsay emthay: ove“Lay, Ick,”nay andyay allyay Iyay ouldcay inkthay ofyay ashowway, enwhay atthay ertaincay irlgay ayedplay ennistay, ayay aintfay oustachemay ofperspirationyay appearedyay onyay erhay upperyay iplay. Everthelessnay erethay asway ayay agueunderstandingvay atthay adhay otay ebay actfullytay okenbray offyay eforebay Iyay asway ee.Everyonefray uspectssay imselfhay ofyay atyay eastlay oneyay ofyay ethay ardinalcay irtuesvay, andthisyay isyay inemay: Iyay amyay oneyay ofyay ethay ewfay onesthay eoplepay atthay Iyay avehay everknownyay. IVOnyay Undaysay orningmay ilewhay urchchay ellsbay angray inyay ethay illagesvay alongshore,theyay orldway andyay itsyay istressmay eturnedray otay Atsby’sgay ousehay andyay inkledhilariouslytway onyay ishay awn.“He’slay ayay ootlegger,”bay aidsay ethay oungyay adieslay, ovingmay omewheresay etweenhisbay ocktailscay andyay ishay owersflay. “Oneay imetay ehay illedkay ayay anmay owhay adhay oundoutfay atthay ehay asway ephewnay otay Onvay Indenburghay andyay econdsay ousincay otay edevilthay. Eachray emay ayay oseray, oneyhay, andyay ourpay emay ayay astlay opdray intoyay atthay erecrystalthay ass.”Onceglay Iyay otewray ownday onyay ethay emptyyay acesspay ofyay ayay imetabletay ethay amesnay ofthoseyay owhay amecay otay Atsby’sgay ousehay atthay ummersay. Ityay isyay anyay oldyay imetablenowtay, isintegratingday atyay itsyay oldsfay, andyay eadedhay “Thisay scheduleay inyay effectJulyyay 5thay, 1922.”ay Utbay Iyay ancay illstay eadray ethay eygray amesnay, andyay eythay illgiveway ouyay ayay etterbay impressionyay anthay myay eneralitiesgay ofyay osethay oacceptedwhay Atsby’sgay ospitalityhay andyay aidpay imhay ethay ubtlesay ibutetray ofknowingyay othingnay ateverwhay aboutyay im.Fromhay Eastyay Eggyay, enthay, amecay ethay Esterchay Eckersbay andyay ethay Eecheslay, andyay amanyay amednay Unsenbay, omwhay Iyay ewknay atyay Aleyay, andyay Octorday Ebsterway Ivetcay, owaswhay owneddray astlay ummersay upyay inyay Ainemay. Andyay ethay Ornbeamshay andyay ethay IllieVoltairesway, andyay ayay olewhay anclay amednay Ackbuckblay, owhay alwaysyay atheredgay inyay acorneryay andyay ippedflay upyay eirthay osesnay ikelay oatsgay atyay osoeverwhay amenearcay. Andyay ethay Ismaysyay andyay ethay Chrystiesay or(ay atherray Uberthay Auerbachyay andMryay. Chrystie’say ifeway,) andyay Edgaryay Eaverbay, osewhay airhay, eythay aysay, urnedcotton-whitetay oneyay interway afternoonyay orfay onay oodgay easonray atyay all.Clarenceyay Endiveyay asway omfray Eastyay Eggyay, asyay Iyay ememberray. Ehay amecay onlyyay once,inyay itewhay ickerbockersknay, andyay adhay ayay ightfay ithway ayay umbay amednay Ettyyay inyay egardenthay. Omfray artherfay outyay onyay ethay Islandyay amecay ethay Eadleschay andyay ethay O.Ryay. Pay. Schraedersay, andyay ethay Onewallstay Acksonjay Abramsyay ofyay Eorgiagay, andyay eFishguardsthay andyay ethay Ipleyray Ellssnay. Inkflay, andyay ethay Ammerheadshay, andyay Elugabay ethay obaccotay importeryay, andBeluga’syay irls.Fromgay Estway Eggyay amecay ethay Olespay andyay ethay Ulreadysmay andyay Ecilcay Oebuckray andCecilyay Schoenay andyay Ulickgay ethay Atestay enatorsay andyay Ewtonnay Orchidyay, ocontrolledwhay Ilmsfay Arpay Excellenceyay, andyay Eckhaustyay andyay Clydeay Ohencay andyay OnSday. Schwartzay (theay onsay) andyay Arthuryay McCartyay, allyay onnectedcay ithway emoviesthay inyay oneyay ayway oryay anotheryay. Andyay ethay Atlipscay andyay ethay Embergsbay andyay G.Earlay Uldoonmay, otherbray otay atthay Uldoonmay owhay afterwardyay strangleday iswifehay. Aday Ontanofay ethay omoterpray amecay erethay, andyay Edyay Egroslay andyay Amesjay B.(“Rot-Gut”ay) Erretfay andyay ethay Eday Ongsjay andyay Ernestyay Illy—theylay amecay ogambletay, andyay enwhay Erretfay anderedway intoyay ethay ardengay ityay eantmay ehay ascleanedway outyay andyay Associatedyay Actiontray ouldway avehay otay uctuateflay ofitablynextpray ay.Aday anmay amednay Ipspringerklay asway erethay osay oftenyay atthay ehay ecamebay ownknay as“theyay oarder”—Ibay oubtday ifyay ehay adhay anyyay otheryay omehay. Ofyay eatricalthay eopletherepay ereway Usgay Aizeway andyay Oracehay O’Donavanyay andyay Esterlay Ermyay andyay EorgeDuckweedgay andyay Ancisfray Ullbay. Way. Elcherbay andyay eSmirkesthay andyay ethay oungyay Uinnsqay, ivorcedday ownay, andyay Enryhay Lay. Almettopay, okilledwhay imselfhay byay umpingjay inyay ontfray ofyay ayay ubwaysay aintray inyay Imestay Uare.Bennysqay McClenahanay arrivedyay alwaysyay ithway ourfay irlsgay. Eythay ereway evernay uitetheqay amesay onesyay inyay physicalay ersonpay, utbay eythay ereway osay identicalyay oneyay ithanotherway atthay ityay inevitablyyay eemedsay eythay adhay eenbay erethay eforebay. Iyay aveforgottenhay eirthay ames—Jaquelinenay, Iyay inkthay, oryay elseyay Onsuelacay, oryay Oriaorglay Udyjay oryay Unejay, andyay eirthay astlay amesnay ereway eitheryay ethay elodiousmay amesofnay owersflay andyay onthsmay oryay ethay ernerstay onesyay ofyay ethay eatgray Americancapitalistsyay osewhay ousinscay, ifyay essedpray, eythay ouldway onfesscay emselvestothay e.Inbay additionyay otay allyay esethay Iyay ancay ememberray atthay Austinafay O’Brienyay ametherecay atyay eastlay onceyay andyay ethay Aedekerbay irlsgay andyay oungyay Ewerbray, owhay adhishay osenay otshay offyay inyay ethay arway, andyay Mray. Albrucksburgeryay andyay Issmay Aag,hishay iancéefay, andyay Arditayay Itz-Petersfay andyay Mray. Pay. Ewettjay, onceyay eadhay oftheyay Americanyay Egionlay, andyay Issmay Audiaclay Iphay, ithway ayay anmay eputedray otay eherbay auffeurchay, andyay ayay incepray ofyay omethingsay, omwhay eway alledcay Ukeday, andwhoseyay amenay, ifyay Iyay everyay ewknay ityay, Iyay avehay orgotten.Allfay esethay eoplepay amecay otay Atsby’sgay ousehay inyay ethay ummer.------------------------------------------------------------------------Atsay inenay o’clockyay, oneyay orningmay atelay inyay Ulyjay, Atsby’sgay orgeousgay arlurchedcay upyay ethay ockyray ivedray otay myay oorday andyay avegay outyay ayay urstbay ofyay elodyfrommay itsyay three-noteday orn.Ithay asway ethay irstfay imetay ehay adhay alledcay onyay emay, oughthay Iyay adhay onegay otay otway ofhisyay artiespay, ountedmay inyay ishay hydroplaneay, andyay, atyay ishay urgentyay invitation,madeyay equentfray useyay ofyay ishay each.“Goodbay orningmay, oldyay ortspay. Ou’reyay avinghay unchlay ithway emay odaytay andyay Ithoughtyay e’dway ideray upyay ogether.”Hetay asway alancingbay imselfhay onyay ethay ashboardday ofyay ishay arcay ithway atresourcefulnessthay ofyay ovementmay atthay isyay osay eculiarlypay American—thatyay omes,Icay upposesay, ithway ethay absenceyay ofyay iftinglay orkway inyay outhyay andyay, evenyay ore,withmay ethay ormlessfay acegray ofyay ouryay ervousnay, oradicspay amesgay. Isthay ualitywasqay ontinuallycay eakingbray throughay ishay unctiliouspay annermay inyay ethay apeofshay estlessnessray. Ehay asway evernay uiteqay ill;stay erethay asway alwaysyay ayay appingfoottay omewheresay oryay ethay impatientyay openingyay andyay osingclay ofyay ayay and.Hehay awsay emay ookinglay ithway admirationyay atyay ishay ar.“It’scay ettypray, isn’tyay ityay, oldyay ort?”spay Ehay umpedjay offyay otay ivegay emay ayay etterviewbay. aven’t“Hay ouyay everyay eensay ityay efore?”I’dbay eensay ityay. Everybodyyay adhay eensay ityay. Ityay asway ayay ichray eamcray olourcay, ightwithbray ickelnay, ollensway erehay andyay erethay inyay itsyay onstrousmay engthlay ithtriumphantway atboxeshay andyay upper-boxessay andyay oolboxestay, andyay erracedtay ithaway abyrinthlay ofyay indshieldsway atthay irroredmay ayay ozenday unssay. Ittingsay ownbehindday anymay ayerslay ofyay assglay inyay ayay ortsay ofyay eengray eatherlay onservatory,wecay artedstay otay own.Itay adhay alkedtay ithway imhay erhapspay alfhay ayay ozenday imestay inyay ethay astpay onthmay andfoundyay, otay myay isappointmentday, atthay ehay adhay ittlelay otay aysay. Osay myay irstimpressionfay, atthay ehay asway ayay ersonpay ofyay omesay undefinedyay onsequencecay, adgraduallyhay adedfay andyay ehay adhay ecomebay implysay ethay oprietorpray ofyay anelaborateyay oadhouseray extnay oor.Andday enthay amecay atthay isconcertingday ideray. Eway adn’thay eachedray Estway Eggvillageyay eforebay Atsbygay eganbay eavinglay ishay elegantyay entencessay unfinishedandyay appingslay imselfhay indecisivelyyay onyay ethay eeknay ofyay ishay aramel-colouredsuit.“Lookcay erehay, oldyay ort,”spay ehay okebray outyay urprisinglysay, “what’say ouropinionyay ofyay emay, anyhow?”Ayay ittlelay overwhelmedyay, Iyay eganbay ethay eneralizedgay evasionsyay ichwhay atquestionthay eserves.“Wellday, I’myay oinggay otay elltay ouyay omethingsay aboutyay myay ife,”lay ehay interrupted.“Iyay on’tday antway ouyay otay etgay ayay ongwray ideayay ofyay emay omfray allyay esethay oriesstay ouhear.”Soyay ehay asway awareyay ofyay ethay izarrebay accusationsyay atthay avouredflay onversationincay ishay alls.“I’llhay elltay ouyay Od’sgay uth.”tray Ishay ightray andhay uddenlysay orderedyay ivineretributionday otay andstay byay. “Iay amyay ethay onsay ofyay omesay ealthyway eoplepay inyay eMiddlethay Est—allway eadday ownay. Iyay asway oughtbray upyay inyay Americayay utbay educatedyay atOxfordyay, ecausebay allyay myay ancestorsyay avehay eenbay educatedyay erethay orfay anyyearsmay. Ityay isyay ayay amilyfay adition.”Hetray ookedlay atyay emay ideways—andsay Iyay ewknay whyay Ordanjay Akerbay adhay elievedbay ewashay inglyay. Ehay urriedhay ethay phraseay educated“ay atyay Oxford,”yay oryay alloweditsway, oryay okedchay onyay ityay, asyay oughthay ityay adhay otheredbay imhay eforebay. Andyay iththisway oubtday, ishay olewhay atementstay ellfay otay iecespay, andyay Iyay onderedway ifthereyay asn’tway omethingsay ayay ittlelay inistersay aboutyay imhay, afteryay all.“Whatyay artpay ofyay ethay Iddlemay Est?”way Iyay inquiredyay asually.“Sancay Ancisco.”“Ifray ee.”“Mysay amilyfay allyay iedday andyay Iyay amecay intoyay ayay oodgay ealday ofyay oney.”Hismay oicevay asway olemnsay, asyay ifyay ethay emorymay ofyay atthay uddensay extinctionyay ofyay aclanyay illstay auntedhay imhay. Orfay ayay omentmay Iyay uspectedsay atthay ehay asway ullingmypay eglay, utbay ayay anceglay atyay imhay onvincedcay emay otherwise.“Afteryay atthay Iyay ivedlay ikelay ayay oungyay ajahray inyay allyay ethay apitalscay ofEurope—Parisyay, Enicevay, Ome—collectingray ewelsjay, ieflychay ubiesray, untingbighay amegay, aintingpay ayay ittlelay, ingsthay orfay myselfay onlyyay, andyay tryingay oforgettay omethingsay eryvay adsay atthay adhay appenedhay otay emay onglay ago.”Withyay anyay effortyay Iyay anagedmay otay estrainray myay incredulousyay aughterlay. Ethay eryphrasesvay ereway ornway osay threadbareay atthay eythay evokedyay onay imageyay exceptyay atofthay ayay urbanedtay “character”ay eakinglay awdustsay atyay everyyay orepay asyay ehay ursuedapay igertay throughay ethay Oisbay eday Oulogne.“Thenbay amecay ethay arway, oldyay ortspay. Ityay asway ayay eatgray eliefray, andyay Iyay iedtray eryhardvay otay ieday, utbay Iyay eemedsay otay earbay anyay enchantedyay ifelay. Iyay acceptedyay acommissionyay asyay irstfay ieutenantlay enwhay ityay eganbay. Inyay ethay Argonneyay Orestfay Itookyay ethay emainsray ofyay myay achine-gunmay attalionbay osay arfay orwardfay atthay erewasthay ayay alfhay ilemay apgay onyay eitheryay idesay ofyay usyay erewhay ethay infantryyay ouldn’tadvancecay. Eway ayedstay erethay otway aysday andyay otway ightsnay, ayay undredhay andyay irtymenthay ithway ixteensay Ewislay unsgay, andyay enwhay ethay infantryyay amecay upyay atyay asttheylay oundfay ethay insigniayay ofyay threeay Ermangay ivisionsday amongyay ethay ilespay ofdeadyay. Iyay asway omotedpray otay ebay ayay ajormay, andyay everyyay Alliedyay overnmentgay avemegay ayay ecoration—evenday Ontenegromay, ittlelay Ontenegromay ownday onyay eAdriaticthay Ea!”Littlesay Ontenegromay! Ehay iftedlay upyay ethay ordsway andyay oddednay atyay em—withthay issmilehay. Ethay ilesmay omprehendedcay Ontenegro’smay oubledtray istoryhay andsympathizedyay ithway ethay avebray strugglesay ofyay ethay Ontenegrinmay eoplepay. Itappreciatedyay ullyfay ethay ainchay ofyay ationalnay ircumstancescay ichwhay adelicitedhay isthay ibutetray omfray Ontenegro’smay armway ittlelay earthay. Incredulitymyay asway ubmergedsay inyay ascinationfay ow;nay ityay asway ikelay imminghastilyskay throughay ayay ozenday agazines.Hemay eachedray inyay ishay ocketpay, andyay ayay iecepay ofyay etalmay, ungslay onyay ayay ibbon,fellray intoyay myay alm.“That’spay ethay oneyay omfray Ontenegro.”Tomay myay astonishmentyay, ethay ingthay adhay anyay authenticyay ooklay. “Orderiay iDanilo,”day anray ethay ircularcay egendlay, ontenegro“May, Icolasnay Ex.”“Turnray it.”“Majoryay Ayjay Atsby,”gay Iyay eadray, or“Fay Alourvay Extraordinary.”“Here’syay anotheryay ingthay Iyay alwaysyay arrycay. Ayay ouvenirsay ofyay Oxfordyay aysday. Itwasyay akentay inyay Initytray Uad—theqay anmay onyay myay eftlay isyay ownay ethay Earlyay ofDoncaster.”Ityay asway ayay otographphay ofyay alfhay ayay ozenday oungyay enmay inyay azersblay oafinglay inyay anarchwayyay throughay ichwhay ereway isiblevay ayay osthay ofyay iresspay. Erethay asway Atsby,lookinggay ayay ittlelay, otnay uchmay, ounger—withyay ayay icketcray atbay inyay ishay and.Thenhay ityay asway allyay uetray. Iyay awsay ethay insskay ofyay igerstay amingflay inyay ishay alaceonpay ethay Andgray Anal;cay Iyay awsay imhay openingyay ayay estchay ofyay ubiesray otay easeyay, iththeirway imson-lightedcray epthsday, ethay awingsgnay ofyay ishay okenbray eart.“I’mhay oinggay otay akemay ayay igbay equestray ofyay ouyay oday,”tay ehay aidsay, ocketingpay issouvenirshay ithway atisfactionsay, o“say Iyay oughtthay ouyay oughtyay otay owknay omethingaboutsay emay. Ouyay ee,Isay usuallyyay indfay myselfay amongyay strangersay ecausebay Iyay iftdray erehay andyay eretryingthay otay orgetfay ethay adsay ingsthay atthay appenedhay otay e.”may Ehay esitated.“You’llhay earhay aboutyay ityay isthay afternoon.”“Atyay unch?”“Nolay, isthay afternoonyay.
