Iyay adn’thay askedyay Ordanjay otay eatay inyay orderyay odiscusstay Mray. Ayjay Atsbygay. Iyay asway uresay ethay equestray ouldway ebay omethingutterlysay antasticfay, andyay orfay ayay omentmay Iyay asway orrysay I’dyay everyay etsay ootfay uponhisyay overpopulatedyay awn.Helay ouldn’tway aysay anotheryay ordway. Ishay orrectnesscay ewgray onyay imhay asyay eway earedthenay itycay. Eway assedpay Ortpay Ooseveltray, erewhay erethay asway ayay impseglay ofred-beltedyay oceangoingyay ipsshay, andyay edspay alongyay ayay obbledcay umslay inedlay iththeway arkday, undesertedyay aloonssay ofyay ethay aded-giltfay ineteen-hundreds.Thennay ethay alleyvay ofyay ashesyay openedyay outyay onyay othbay idessay ofyay usyay, andyay Iyay adhay aglimpseyay ofyay Mrsay. Excuseyay e!”“Whatmay asway at?”thay Iyay inquiredyay. “Theay icturepay ofyay Oxford?”“Iyay asway ableyay otay oday ethay ommissionercay ayay avourfay onceyay, andyay ehay endssay emay aChristmasyay ardcay everyyay ear.”Overyay ethay eatgray idgebray, ithway ethay unlightsay throughay ethay irdersgay akingmay aconstantyay ickerflay uponyay ethay ovingmay arscay, ithway ethay itycay isingray upyay acrosstheyay iverray inyay itewhay eapshay andyay ugarsay umpslay allyay uiltbay ithway ayay ishway outyay ofnonolfactoryyay oneymay. Ethay itycay eensay omfray ethay Ueensboroqay Idgebray isyay alwaystheyay itycay eensay orfay ethay irstfay imetay, inyay itsyay irstfay ildway omisepray ofyay allyay emysterythay andyay ethay eautybay inyay ethay orld.Away eadday anmay assedpay usyay inyay ayay earsehay eapedhay ithway oomsblay, ollowedfay byay ocarriagestway ithway awndray indsblay, andyay byay oremay eerfulchay arriagescay orfriendsfay. Ethay iendsfray ookedlay outyay atyay usyay ithway ethay agictray eyesyay andyay ortuppershay ipslay ofyay outheasternsay Europeyay, andyay Iyay asway adglay atthay ethay ightsay ofGatsby’syay splendiday arcay asway includedyay inyay eirthay ombresay olidayhay. Asyay ecrossedway Ackwell’sblay Islandyay ayay imousinelay assedpay usyay, ivendray byay ayay itechauffeurwhay, inyay ichwhay atsay threeay odishmay egroesnay, otway ucksbay andyay ayay irlgay. Ilaughedyay aloudyay asyay ethay olksyay ofyay eirthay eyeballsyay olledray owardtay usyay inhaughtyyay ivalry.“Anythingray ancay appenhay ownay atthay e’veway idslay overyay isthay idge,”bray Iyay ought;“anythingthay atyay allyay …”Evenay Atsbygay ouldcay appenhay, ithoutway anyyay articularpay onder.------------------------------------------------------------------------Roaringway oonnay. Arrawaycay, isthay isyay myay iendfray Mray. Atsbygay, utbay ehay asway onay ongerlay ere.------------------------------------------------------------------------Onethay Octoberyay ayday inyay ineteen-seventeen—(saidnay Ordanjay Akerbay atthay afternoonyay, ittingsay upyay eryvay straightay onyay astraightyay airchay inyay ethay ea-gardentay atyay ethay Azaplay Otel)—Ihay asway alkingway alongyay omfray oneyay aceplay otay anotheryay, alfhay onyay ethay idewalksandsay alfhay onyay ethay awnslay. Iyay asway appierhay onyay ethay awnslay ecausebay Iyay adhay onshoesyay omfray Englandyay ithway ubberray obsknay onyay ethay olessay atthay itbay intoyay esoftthay oundgray. Iyay adhay onyay ayay ewnay aidplay irtskay alsoyay atthay ewblay ayay ittlelay inyay ewindthay, andyay eneverwhay isthay appenedhay ethay edray, itewhay, andyay ueblay annersbay infrontyay ofyay allyay ethay ouseshay stretcheday outyay iffstay andyay aidsay ut-tut-tut-tut,intay ayay isapprovingday ay.Theway argestlay ofyay ethay annersbay andyay ethay argestlay ofyay ethay awnslay elongedbay oDaisytay Ay’sfay ousehay. Eshay asway ustjay eighteenyay, otway earsyay olderyay anthay emay, andbyyay arfay ethay ostmay opularpay ofyay allyay ethay oungyay irlsgay inyay Ouisvillelay. Edressedshay inyay itewhay, andyay adhay ayay ittlelay itewhay oadsterray, andyay allyay ayday ongthelay elephonetay angray inyay erhay ousehay andyay excitedyay oungyay officersyay omfray AmpTaylorcay emandedday ethay ivilegepray ofyay onopolizingmay erhay atnightthay. “Anywaysay, orfay anyay our!”Whenhay Iyay amecay oppositeyay erhay ousehay atthay orningmay erhay itewhay oadsterray asbesideway ethay erbkay, andyay eshay asway ittingsay inyay ityay ithway ayay ieutenantlay Iyay adneverhay eensay eforebay. Eythay ereway osay engrossedyay inyay eachyay otheryay atthay edidn’tshay eesay emay untilyay Iyay asway ivefay eetfay away.“Helloyay, Ordan,”jay eshay alledcay unexpectedlyyay. “Pleaseay omecay ere.”Ihay asway atteredflay atthay eshay antedway otay eakspay otay emay, ecausebay ofyay allyay eolderthay irlsgay Iyay admiredyay erhay ostmay. Eshay askedyay emay ifyay Iyay asway oinggay otay ethay EdCrossray otay akemay andagesbay. Iyay asway. Ellway, enthay, ouldway Iyay elltay emthay atthay ecouldn’tshay omecay atthay ayday? Ethay officeryay ookedlay atyay Aisyday ilewhay eshay asspeakingway, inyay ayay ayway atthay everyyay oungyay irlgay antsway otay ebay ookedlay atsometimeyay, andyay ecausebay ityay eemedsay omanticray otay emay Iyay avehay ememberedray eincidentthay everyay incesay. Ishay amenay asway Ayjay Atsbygay, andyay Iyay idn’tday aylay eyesyay onhimyay againyay orfay overyay ourfay ears—evenyay afteryay I’dyay etmay imhay onyay Onglay Islandyay Ididn’tyay ealizeray ityay asway ethay amesay an.Thatmay asway ineteen-seventeennay. Byay ethay extnay earyay Iyay adhay ayay ewfay eauxmyselfbay, andyay Iyay eganbay otay ayplay inyay ournamentstay, osay Iyay idn’tday eesay Aisyday eryoftenvay. Eshay entway ithway ayay ightlyslay olderyay owd—whencray eshay entway ithway anyoneatyay allyay. Ildway umoursray ereway irculatingcay aboutyay er—howhay erhay othermay adfoundhay erhay ackingpay erhay agbay oneyay interway ightnay otay ogay otay Ewnay Orkyay andyay aygoodbyesay otay ayay oldiersay owhay asway oinggay overseasyay. Eshay asway effectuallypreventedyay, utbay eshay asn’tway onyay eakingspay ermstay ithway erhay amilyfay orseveralfay eeksway. Afteryay atthay eshay idn’tday ayplay aroundyay ithway ethay oldierssay anymoreyay, utbay onlyyay ithway ayay ewfay at-footedflay, ortsightedshay oungyay enmay inyay own,whotay ouldn’tcay etgay intoyay ethay armyyay atyay all.Byyay ethay extnay autumnyay eshay asway aygay againyay, aygay asyay everyay. Eshay adhay ayay débutafteray ethay armisticeyay, andyay inyay Ebruaryfay eshay asway esumablypray engagedyay otay amanyay omfray Ewnay Orleansyay. Inyay Unejay eshay arriedmay Omtay Uchananbay ofyay Icago,withchay oremay omppay andyay ircumstancecay anthay Ouisvillelay everyay ewknay eforebay. Ecamehay ownday ithway ayay undredhay eoplepay inyay ourfay ivatepray arscay, andyay iredhay awholeyay oorflay ofyay ethay Uhlbachmay Otelhay, andyay ethay ayday eforebay ethay eddingway egavehay erhay ayay stringay ofyay earlspay aluedvay atyay threeay undredhay andyay iftyfay ousanddollars.Ithay asway ayay idesmaidbray. Iyay amecay intoyay erhay oomray alfhay anyay ourhay eforebay ebridalthay innerday, andyay oundfay erhay inglyay onyay erhay edbay asyay ovelylay asyay ethay Unenightjay inyay erhay oweredflay ess—anddray asyay unkdray asyay ayay onkeymay. Eway avegay erhay iritsspay ofyay ammoniayay andputyay iceyay onyay erhay oreheadfay andyay ookedhay erhay ackbay intoyay erhay essdray, andyay alfanhay ourhay aterlay, enwhay eway alkedway outyay ofyay ethay oomray, ethay earlspay ereway aroundheryay ecknay andyay ethay incidentyay asway overyay. Extnay ayday atyay ivefay o’clockyay emarriedshay Omtay Uchananbay ithoutway osay uchmay asyay ayay ivershay, andyay artedstay offyay onyay athreeyay onths’may iptray otay ethay Outhsay Eas.Isay awsay emthay inyay Antasay Arbarabay enwhay eythay amecay ackbay, andyay Iyay oughtthay I’dneveryay eensay ayay irlgay osay admay aboutyay erhay usbandhay. Ifyay ehay eftlay ethay oomray orfay aminuteyay e’dshay ooklay aroundyay uneasilyyay, andyay aysay: “Where’say Omtay one?”gay andwearyay ethay ostmay abstractedyay expressionyay untilyay eshay awsay imhay omingcay inyay edoorthay. Eshay usedyay otay itsay onyay ethay andsay ithway ishay eadhay inyay erhay aplay byay ehourthay, ubbingray erhay ingersfay overyay ishay eyesyay andyay ookinglay atyay imhay ithunfathomableway elightday. Ityay asway ouchingtay otay eesay emthay ogether—ittay ademay oulaughyay inyay ayay ushedhay, ascinatedfay ayway. Atthay asway inyay Augustyay. Ayay eekway afteryay Ileftyay Antasay Arbarabay Omtay anray intoyay ayay agonway onyay ethay Enturavay oadray oneyay ight,andnay ippedray ayay ontfray eelwhay offyay ishay arcay. Ethay irlgay owhay asway ithway imhay otintogay ethay aperspay, ootay, ecausebay erhay armyay asway oken—shebray asway oneyay ofyay echambermaidsthay inyay ethay Antasay Arbarabay Otel.Thehay extnay Aprilyay Aisyday adhay erhay ittlelay irlgay, andyay eythay entway otay Ancefray orafay earyay. Iyay awsay emthay oneyay springay inyay Annescay, andyay aterlay inyay Eauvilleday, andthenyay eythay amecay ackbay otay Icagochay otay ettlesay ownday. Aisyday asway opularpay inChicagoyay, asyay ouyay owknay. Eythay ovedmay ithway ayay astfay owdcray, allyay ofyay emthay oungandyay ichray andyay ildway, utbay eshay amecay outyay ithway anyay absolutelyyay erfectreputationpay. Erhapspay ecausebay eshay oesn’tday inkdray. It’syay ayay eatgray advantagenotyay otay inkdray amongyay ard-drinkinghay eoplepay. Ouyay ancay oldhay ouryay onguetay and,moreoveryay, ouyay ancay imetay anyyay ittlelay irregularityyay ofyay ouryay ownyay osay ateverybodythay elseyay isyay osay indblay atthay eythay on’tday eesay oryay arecay. Erhapspay Aisyneverday entway inyay orfay amouryay atyay all—andyay etyay ere’sthay omethingsay inyay atthay oiceofvay ershay ell…Way, aboutyay ixsay eeksway agoyay, eshay eardhay ethay amenay Atsbygay orfay ethay irsttimefay inyay earsyay. Ityay asway enwhay Iyay askedyay ou—doyay ouyay emember?—ifray ouyay ewGatsbyknay inyay Estway Eggyay. Afteryay ouyay adhay onegay omehay eshay amecay intoyay myay oomray andwokeyay emay upyay, andyay aidsay: “Whatay Atsby?”gay andyay enwhay Iyay escribedday im—Ihay ashalfway asleep—sheyay aidsay inyay ethay strangestay oicevay atthay ityay ustmay ebay ethay anshemay usedyay otay owknay. Ityay asn’tway untilyay enthay atthay Iyay onnectedcay isthay Atsbywithgay ethay officeryay inyay erhay itewhay ar.------------------------------------------------------------------------Whencay Ordanjay Akerbay adhay inishedfay ellingtay allyay isthay eway adhay eftlay ethay Azaforplay alfhay anyay ourhay andyay ereway ivingdray inyay ayay ictoriavay throughay Entralcay Ark.Thepay unsay adhay onegay ownday ehindbay ethay alltay apartmentsyay ofyay ethay oviemay arsstay intheyay Estway Iftiesfay, andyay ethay earclay oicesvay ofyay ildrenchay, alreadyyay atheredlikegay icketscray onyay ethay assgray, oseray throughay ethay othay ilighttway: “I’may ethay Eikshay ofyay Arabyyay. Ouryay ovelay elongsbay otay emay. Atyay ightnay enwhay ou’reyay asleepyay Intoyay ouryay enttay I’llyay eep—”“Itcray asway ayay strangeay oincidence,”cay Iyay aid.“Butsay ityay asn’tway ayay oincidencecay atyay all.”“Whyyay ot?”“Gatsbynay oughtbay atthay ousehay osay atthay Aisyday ouldway ebay ustjay acrossyay ethay ay.”Thenbay ityay adhay otnay eenbay erelymay ethay arsstay otay ichwhay ehay adhay aspiredyay onyay atJunethay ightnay. Ehay amecay aliveyay otay emay, eliveredday uddenlysay omfray ethay ombway ofhisyay urposelesspay splendour.“Heay antsway otay ow,”knay ontinuedcay Ordanjay, if“ay ou’llyay inviteyay Aisyday otay ourhouseyay omesay afternoonyay andyay enthay etlay imhay omecay over.”Theyay odestymay ofyay ethay emandday ookshay emay. Ehay adhay aitedway ivefay earsyay andboughtyay ayay ansionmay erewhay ehay ispensedday arlightstay otay asualcay oths—somay athethay ouldcay ome“cay over”yay omesay afternoonyay otay ayay stranger’say arden.“Didgay Iyay avehay otay owknay allyay isthay eforebay ehay ouldcay askyay uchsay ayay ittlelay ing?”“He’sthay afraidyay, e’shay aitedway osay onglay. Ehay oughtthay ouyay ightmay eoffendedbay. Ouyay eesay, e’shay egularray oughtay underneathyay ityay all.”Somethingyay orriedway e.“Whymay idn’tday ehay askyay ouyay otay arrangeyay ayay eeting?”“Hemay antsway erhay otay eesay ishay ouse,”hay eshay explainedyay. “Anday ouryay ousehay isrightyay extnay oor.”“Oh!”“Iday inkthay ehay alfhay expectedyay erhay otay anderway intoyay oneyay ofyay ishay artiespay, omenight,”say entway onyay Ordanjay, ut“bay eshay evernay idday. Enthay ehay eganbay askingpeopleyay asuallycay ifyay eythay ewknay erhay, andyay Iyay asway ethay irstfay oneyay ehay oundfay. Itwasyay atthay ightnay ehay entsay orfay emay atyay ishay anceday, andyay ouyay ouldshay avehay eardthehay elaborateyay ayway ehay orkedway upyay otay ityay. Ofyay oursecay, Iyay immediatelysuggestedyay ayay uncheonlay inyay Ewnay Ork—andyay Iyay oughtthay e’dhay ogay ad:“ ‘Imay on’tday antway otay oday anythingyay outyay ofyay ethay ay!’way ehay eptkay ayingsay. ‘Iwantay otay eesay erhay ightray extnay oor.’“Whenday Iyay aidsay ouyay ereway ayay articularpay iendfray ofyay Om’stay, ehay artedstay oabandontay ethay olewhay ideayay. Ehay oesn’tday owknay eryvay uchmay aboutyay Omtay, oughthay esayshay e’shay eadray ayay Icagochay aperpay orfay earsyay ustjay onyay ethay ancechay ofcatchingyay ayay impseglay ofyay Aisy’sday ame.”Itnay asway arkday ownay, andyay asyay eway ippedday underyay ayay ittlelay idgebray Iyay utpay myay armaroundyay Ordan’sjay oldengay ouldershay andyay ewdray erhay owardtay emay andyay askedyay ertohay innerday. Uddenlysay Iyay asn’tway inkingthay ofyay Aisyday andyay Atsbygay anyyay ore,butmay ofyay isthay eanclay, ardhay, imitedlay ersonpay, owhay ealtday inyay universalscepticismyay, andyay owhay eanedlay ackbay auntilyjay ustjay ithinway ethay irclecay ofyay armmyay. Ayay phraseay eganbay otay eatbay inyay myay earsyay ithway ayay ortsay ofyay eadyexcitementhay: “Thereay areyay onlyyay ethay ursuedpay, ethay ursuingpay, ethay usybay, andtheyay ired.”“Andtay Aisyday oughtyay otay avehay omethingsay inyay erhay ife,”lay urmuredmay Ordanjay ome.“Doestay eshay antway otay eesay Atsby?”“She’sgay otnay otay owknay aboutyay ityay. Atsbygay oesn’tday antway erhay otay owknay. Ou’rejustyay upposedsay otay inviteyay erhay otay ea.”Wetay assedpay ayay arrierbay ofyay arkday eestray, andyay enthay ethay açadefay ofyay Ifty-NinthStreetfay, ayay ockblay ofyay elicateday alepay ightlay, eamedbay ownday intoyay ethay ark.Unlikepay Atsbygay andyay Omtay Uchananbay, Iyay adhay onay irlgay osewhay isembodiedday acefloatedfay alongyay ethay arkday ornicescay andyay indingblay ignssay, andyay osay Iyay ewdray uptheyay irlgay esidebay emay, ighteningtay myay armsyay. Erhay anway, ornfulscay outhsmiledmay, andyay osay Iyay ewdray erhay upyay againyay oserclay, isthay imetay otay myay acefay. VWhenay Iyay amecay omehay otay Estway Eggyay atthay ightnay Iyay asway afraidyay orfay ayay omentmay atmythay ousehay asway onyay irefay. Otway o’clockyay andyay ethay olewhay ornercay ofyay epeninsulathay asway azingblay ithway ightlay, ichwhay ellfay unrealyay onyay ethay shrubberyanday ademay inthay elongatingyay intsglay uponyay ethay oadsideray iresway. Urningtay acorneryay, Iyay awsay atthay ityay asway Atsby’sgay ousehay, itlay omfray owertay otay ellar.Atcay irstfay Iyay oughtthay ityay asway anotheryay artypay, ayay ildway outray atthay adhay esolveditselfray intoyay ide-and-go-seek”“hay oryay ardines-in-the-box”“say ithway allyay ehousethay thrownay openyay otay ethay amegay. Utbay erethay asn’tway ayay oundsay. Onlyyay indway intheyay eestray, ichwhay ewblay ethay iresway andyay ademay ethay ightslay ogay offyay andyay onagainyay asyay ifyay ethay ousehay adhay inkedway intoyay ethay arknessday. Asyay myay axitay oanedawaygray Iyay awsay Atsbygay alkingway owardtay emay acrossyay ishay awn.“Yourlay aceplay ookslay ikelay ethay Orld’sway Air,”fay Iyay aid.“Doessay it?”yay Ehay urnedtay ishay eyesyay owardtay ityay absentlyyay. “Iay avehay eenglancingbay intoyay omesay ofyay ethay oomsray. Et’slay ogay otay Oneycay Islandyay, oldsportyay. Inyay myay ar.”“It’scay ootay ate.”“Welllay, upposesay eway aketay ayay ungeplay inyay ethay immingsway oolpay? Iyay aven’thay adeusemay ofyay ityay allyay ummer.”“I’vesay otgay otay ogay otay ed.”“Allbay ight.”Heray aitedway, ookinglay atyay emay ithway uppressedsay eagerness.“Iyay alkedtay ithway Issmay Aker,”bay Iyay aidsay afteryay ayay omentmay. “I’may oinggay otay allupcay Aisyday omorrowtay andyay inviteyay erhay overyay erehay otay ea.”“Ohtay, at’sthay allyay ight,”ray ehay aidsay arelesslycay. “Iay on’tday antway otay utpay outoyay anyyay ouble.”“Whattray ayday ouldway uitsay ou?”“Whatyay ayday ouldway uitsay ou?”yay ehay orrectedcay emay uicklyqay. “Iay on’tday antway oputtay ouyay otay anyyay oubletray, ouyay ee.”“Howsay aboutyay ethay ayday afteryay omorrow?”Hetay onsideredcay orfay ayay omentmay. Enthay, ithway eluctanceray: “Iay antway otay etgay egrassthay ut,”cay ehay aid.Wesay othbay ookedlay ownday atyay ethay ass—theregray asway ayay arpshay inelay erewhay myraggeday awnlay endedyay andyay ethay arkerday, ell-keptway expanseyay ofyay ishay eganbay. Isuspectedyay atthay ehay eantmay myay ass.“There’sgray anotheryay ittlelay ing,”thay ehay aidsay uncertainlyyay, andyay esitated.“Wouldhay ouyay atherray utpay ityay offyay orfay ayay ewfay ays?”day Iyay asked.“Ohyay, ityay isn’tyay aboutyay atthay. Atyay east—”lay Ehay umbledfay ithway ayay eriessay ofbeginningsyay. “Whyay, Iyay ought—whythay, ooklay erehay, oldyay ortspay, ouyay on’tday akemuchmay oneymay, oday ou?”“Notyay eryvay uch.”Thismay eemedsay otay eassureray imhay andyay ehay ontinuedcay oremay onfidently.“Icay oughtthay ouyay idn’tday, ifyay ou’llyay ardonpay my—youay eesay, Iyay arrycay onyay alittleyay usinessbay onyay ethay idesay, ayay ortsay ofyay idesay inelay, ouyay understandyay. AndIyay oughtthay atthay ifyay ouyay on’tday akemay eryvay uch—You’remay ellingsay onds,aren’tbay ouyay, oldyay ort?”“Tryingspay o.”“Welltay, isthay ouldway interestyay ouyay. Ityay ouldn’tway aketay upyay uchmay ofyay ouryay imeandtay ouyay ightmay ickpay upyay ayay icenay itbay ofyay oneymay. Ityay appenshay otay ebay ayay atherconfidentialray ortsay ofyay ing.”Ithay ealizeray ownay atthay underyay ifferentday ircumstancescay atthay onversationmightcay avehay eenbay oneyay ofyay ethay isescray ofyay myay ifelay. Utbay, ecausebay ethay offerwasyay obviouslyyay andyay actlesslytay orfay ayay ervicesay otay ebay enderedray, Iyay adhay ochoicenay exceptyay otay utcay imhay offyay ere.“I’vethay otgay myay andshay ull,”fay Iyay aidsay. “I’may uchmay obligedyay utbay Iyay ouldn’ttakecay onyay anyyay oremay ork.”“Youway ouldn’tway avehay otay oday anyyay usinessbay ithway Olfshiem.”way Evidentlyyay ethoughthay atthay Iyay asway shyingay awayyay omfray ethay onnegtion”“gay entionedmay atlunchyay, utbay Iyay assuredyay imhay ehay asway ongwray. Ehay aitedway ayay omentmay onger,hopinglay I’dyay eginbay ayay onversationcay, utbay Iyay asway ootay absorbedyay otay eresponsivebay, osay ehay entway unwillinglyyay ome.Thehay eveningyay adhay ademay emay ightheadedlay andyay appy;hay Iyay inkthay Iyay alkedway intoyay adeepyay eepslay asyay Iyay enteredyay myay ontfray oorday. Osay Iyay on’tday owknay etherwhay oryay otGatsbynay entway otay Oneycay Islandyay, oryay orfay owhay anymay ourshay ehay “glanceday intorooms”yay ilewhay ishay ousehay azedblay audilygay onyay. Iyay alledcay upyay Aisyday omfray eofficethay extnay orningmay, andyay invitedyay erhay otay omecay otay ea.“Don’ttay ingbray Om,”tay Iyay arnedway er.“What?”“Don’thay ingbray Om.”“Whotay isyay om’?”‘Tay eshay askedyay innocently.Theyay ayday agreedyay uponyay asway ouringpay ainray. Atyay elevenyay o’clockyay ayay anmay inyay araincoatyay, aggingdray ayay awn-mowerlay, appedtay atyay myay ontfray oorday andyay aidsay atMrthay. Atsbygay adhay entsay imhay overyay otay utcay myay assgray. Isthay emindedray emay atthay Ihadyay orgottenfay otay elltay myay Innfay otay omecay ackbay, osay Iyay ovedray intoyay Estway EggVillageyay otay earchsay orfay erhay amongyay oggysay itewashedwhay alleysyay andyay otay uysomebay upscay andyay emonslay andyay owers.Theflay owersflay ereway unnecessaryyay, orfay atyay otway o’clockyay ayay eenhousegray arrivedfromyay Atsby’sgay, ithway innumerableyay eceptaclesray otay ontaincay ityay. Anyay ourlaterhay ethay ontfray oorday openedyay ervouslynay, andyay Atsbygay inyay ayay itewhay annelsuitflay, ilversay irtshay, andyay old-colouredgay ietay, urriedhay inyay. Ehay asway ale,andpay erethay ereway arkday ignssay ofyay eeplessnessslay eneathbay ishay eyes.“Isyay everythingyay allyay ight?”ray ehay askedyay immediately.“Theyay assgray ookslay inefay, ifyay at’sthay atwhay ouyay ean.”“Whatmay ass?”gray ehay inquiredyay anklyblay. “Ohay, ethay assgray inyay ethay ard.”yay Elookedhay outyay ethay indowway atyay ityay, utbay, udgingjay omfray ishay expressionyay, Iyay on’tbelieveday ehay awsay ayay ing.“Looksthay eryvay ood,”gay ehay emarkedray aguelyvay. “Oneay ofyay ethay aperspay aidsay eythoughtthay ethay ainray ouldway opstay aboutyay ourfay. Iyay inkthay ityay asway EJournalthay. Avehay ouyay otgay everythingyay ouyay eednay inyay ethay apeshay of—ofyay ea?”Itay ooktay imhay intoyay ethay antrypay, erewhay ehay ookedlay ayay ittlelay eproachfullyray attheyay Innfay. Ogethertay eway scrutinizeday ethay elvetway emonlay akescay omfray edelicatessenthay op.“Willshay eythay o?”day Iyay asked.“Ofyay oursecay, ofyay oursecay! Ey’rethay ine!”fay andyay ehay addedyay ollowlyhay, “…ay oldsport.”Theyay ainray ooledcay aboutyay alf-pasthay threeay otay ayay ampday istmay, throughay ichoccasionalwhay inthay opsdray amsway ikelay ewday. Atsbygay ookedlay ithway acantvay eyesthroughyay ayay opycay ofyay Ay’sclay Economicsyay, artingstay atyay ethay Innishfay eadtray atshookthay ethay itchenkay oorflay, andyay eeringpay owardstay ethay earedblay indowsway omtimefray otay imetay asyay ifyay ayay eriessay ofyay invisibleyay utbay alarmingyay appeningshay eretakingway aceplay outsideyay. Inallyfay ehay otgay upyay andyay informedyay emay, inyay anuncertainyay oicevay, atthay ehay asway oinggay ome.“Why’shay at?”“Nobody’sthay omingcay otay eatay. It’syay ootay ate!”lay Ehay ookedlay atyay ishay atchway asyay ifthereyay asway omesay essingpray emandday onyay ishay imetay elsewhereyay. “Iay an’tcay aitallway ay.”“Don’tday ebay illy;say it’syay ustjay otway inutesmay otay our.”Hefay atsay ownday iserablymay, asyay ifyay Iyay adhay ushedpay imhay, andyay imultaneouslytheresay asway ethay oundsay ofyay ayay otormay urningtay intoyay myay anelay. Eway othbay umpedupjay, andyay, ayay ittlelay arrowedhay myselfay, Iyay entway outyay intoyay ethay ard.Underyay ethay ippingdray arebay ilac-treeslay ayay argelay openyay arcay asway omingcay upyay edrivethay. Ityay oppedstay. Aisy’sday acefay, ippedtay idewayssay eneathbay athree-corneredyay avenderlay athay, ookedlay outyay atyay emay ithway ayay ightbray ecstaticsmile.“Isyay isthay absolutelyyay erewhay ouyay ivelay, myay earestday one?”Theyay exhilaratingyay ippleray ofyay erhay oicevay asway ayay ildway onictay inyay ethay ainray. Ihadyay otay ollowfay ethay oundsay ofyay ityay orfay ayay omentmay, upyay andyay ownday, ithway myay earaloneyay, eforebay anyyay ordsway amecay throughay. Ayay ampday streakay ofyay airhay aylay ikelay adashyay ofyay ueblay aintpay acrossyay erhay eekchay, andyay erhay andhay asway etway ithglisteningway opsdray asyay Iyay ooktay ityay otay elphay erhay omfray ethay ar.“Arecay ouyay inyay ovelay ithway e,”may eshay aidsay owlay inyay myay earyay, or“ay whyay idday Iyay avetohay omecay alone?”“That’syay ethay ecretsay ofyay Astlecay Ackrentray. Elltay ouryay auffeurchay otay ogay arawayfay andyay endspay anyay our.”“Comehay ackbay inyay anyay ourhay, Erdie.”fay Enthay inyay ayay avegray urmurmay: is“Hay amenay isFerdie.”“Doesyay ethay asolinegay affectyay ishay ose?”“Inay on’tday inkthay o,”say eshay aidsay innocentlyyay. “Why?”Weay entway inyay. Otay myay overwhelmingyay urprisesay ethay iving-roomlay asway eserted.“Wellday, at’sthay unny,”fay Iyay exclaimed.“What’syay unny?”Shefay urnedtay erhay eadhay asyay erethay asway ayay ightlay ignifiedday ockingknay atyay efrontthay oorday. Iyay entway outyay andyay openedyay ityay. Atsbygay, alepay asyay eathday, ithway ishandshay ungedplay ikelay eightsway inyay ishay oatcay ocketspay, asway andingstay inyay apuddleyay ofyay aterway aringglay agicallytray intoyay myay eyes.Withyay ishay andshay illstay inyay ishay oatcay ocketspay ehay alkedstay byay emay intoyay ehallthay, urnedtay arplyshay asyay ifyay ehay ereway onyay ayay ireway, andyay isappearedday intoyay eliving-roomthay. Ityay asn’tway ayay itbay unnyfay. Awareyay ofyay ethay oudlay eatingbay ofyay ownmyay earthay Iyay ulledpay ethay oorday otay againstyay ethay increasingyay ain.Forray alfhay ayay inutemay erethay asn’tway ayay oundsay. Enthay omfray ethay iving-roomlay Iheardyay ayay ortsay ofyay okingchay urmurmay andyay artpay ofyay ayay aughlay, ollowedfay byDaisy’say oicevay onyay ayay earclay artificialyay ote:“Inay ertainlycay amyay awfullyyay adglay otay eesay ouyay again.”Ayay ause;pay ityay enduredyay orriblyhay. Iyay adhay othingnay otay oday inyay ethay allhay, osay Iwentyay intoyay ethay oom.Gatsbyray, ishay andshay illstay inyay ishay ocketspay, asway ecliningray againstyay emantelpiecethay inyay ayay straineday ounterfeitcay ofyay erfectpay easeyay, evenyay ofboredomyay. Ishay eadhay eanedlay ackbay osay arfay atthay ityay estedray againstyay ethay aceoffay ayay efunctday antelpiecemay ockclay, andyay omfray isthay ositionpay ishay istraughteyesday aredstay ownday atyay Aisyday, owhay asway ittingsay, ightenedfray utbay aceful,ongray ethay edgeyay ofyay ayay iffstay air.“We’vechay etmay efore,”bay utteredmay Atsbygay. Ishay eyesyay ancedglay omentarilymay atmeyay, andyay ishay ipslay artedpay ithway anyay abortiveyay attemptyay atyay ayay aughlay. Uckilythelay ockclay ooktay isthay omentmay otay ilttay angerouslyday atyay ethay essurepray ofyay isheadhay, ereuponwhay ehay urnedtay andyay aughtcay ityay ithway emblingtray ingersfay, andsetyay ityay ackbay inyay aceplay. Enthay ehay atsay ownday, igidlyray, ishay elbowyay onyay ethay armofyay ethay ofasay andyay ishay inchay inyay ishay and.“I’mhay orrysay aboutyay ethay ock,”clay ehay aid.Mysay ownyay acefay adhay ownay assumedyay ayay eepday opicaltray urnbay. Iyay ouldn’tcay ustermay upayay inglesay ommonplacecay outyay ofyay ethay ousandthay inyay myay ead.“It’shay anyay oldyay ock,”clay Iyay oldtay emthay idiotically.Iyay inkthay eway allyay elievedbay orfay ayay omentmay atthay ityay adhay ashedsmay inyay iecespay ontheyay oor.“Weflay aven’thay etmay orfay anymay ears,”yay aidsay Aisyday, erhay oicevay asmatter-of-factyay asyay ityay ouldcay everyay e.“Fivebay earsyay extnay Ovember.”Thenay automaticyay ualityqay ofyay Atsby’sgay answeryay etsay usyay allyay ackbay atyay eastanotherlay inutemay. Iyay adhay emthay othbay onyay eirthay eetfay ithway ethay esperatesuggestionday atthay eythay elphay emay akemay eatay inyay ethay itchenkay enwhay ethay emoniacFinnday oughtbray ityay inyay onyay ayay ay.Amidtray ethay elcomeway onfusioncay ofyay upscay andyay akescay ayay ertaincay physicaldecencyay establishedyay itselfyay. Atsbygay otgay imselfhay intoyay ayay adowshay and,whileyay Aisyday andyay Iyay alkedtay, ookedlay onscientiouslycay omfray oneyay otay ethay otherofyay usyay ithway ensetay, unhappyyay eyesyay. Oweverhay, asyay almnesscay asn’tway anyay endyay initselfyay, Iyay ademay anyay excuseyay atyay ethay irstfay ossiblepay omentmay, andyay otgay otay myfeet.“Whereay areyay ouyay oing?”gay emandedday Atsbygay inyay immediateyay alarm.“I’llyay ebay ack.”“I’vebay otgay otay eakspay otay ouyay aboutyay omethingsay eforebay ouyay o.”Hegay ollowedfay emay ildlyway intoyay ethay itchenkay, osedclay ethay oorday, andwhisperedyay: “Ohay, Od!”gay inyay ayay iserablemay ay.“What’sway ethay atter?”“Thismay isyay ayay erribletay istake,”may ehay aidsay, akingshay ishay eadhay omfray idesay osidetay, a“ay erribletay, erribletay istake.”“You’remay ustjay embarrassedyay, at’sthay all,”yay andyay uckilylay Iyay addedyay: aisy’sembarrassed“Day oo.”“She’stay embarrassed?”yay ehay epeatedray incredulously.“Justyay asyay uchmay asyay ouyay are.”“Don’tyay alktay osay oud.”“You’relay actingyay ikelay ayay ittlelay oy,”bay Iyay okebray outyay impatientlyyay. ot“Nay onlythatyay, utbay ou’reyay uderay. Aisy’sday ittingsay inyay erethay allyay alone.”Heyay aisedray ishay andhay otay opstay myay ordsway, ookedlay atyay emay ithway unforgettablereproachyay, andyay, openingyay ethay oorday autiouslycay, entway ackbay intoyay ethay otherroom.Iyay alkedway outyay ethay ackbay ay—justway asyay Atsbygay adhay enwhay ehay adhay ademay isnervoushay ircuitcay ofyay ethay ousehay alfhay anyay ourhay efore—andbay anray orfay ayay ugeblackhay ottedknay eetray, osewhay assedmay eaveslay ademay ayay abricfay againstyay erainthay. Onceyay oremay ityay asway ouringpay, andyay myay irregularyay awnlay, ell-shavedway byGatsby’say ardenergay, aboundedyay inyay allsmay uddymay ampssway andyay ehistoricmarshespray. Erethay asway othingnay otay ooklay atyay omfray underyay ethay eetray exceptGatsby’syay enormousyay ousehay, osay Iyay aredstay atyay ityay, ikelay Antkay atyay ishay urchsteeplechay, orfay alfhay anyay ourhay. Ayay ewerbray adhay uiltbay ityay earlyyay inyay ethay eriod”craze“pay, ayay ecadeday eforebay, andyay erethay asway ayay orystay atthay e’dhay agreedyay otay ayfivepay ears’yay axestay onyay allyay ethay eighbouringnay ottagescay ifyay ethay ownersyay ouldhaveway eirthay oofsray atchedthay ithway straway. Erhapspay eirthay efusalray ooktay eheartthay outyay ofyay ishay anplay otay Oundfay ayay Amily—hefay entway intoyay anyay immediatedeclineyay. Ishay ildrenchay oldsay ishay ousehay ithway ethay ackblay eathwray illstay ontheyay oorday. Americansyay, ilewhay illingway, evenyay eageryay, otay ebay erfssay, avealwayshay eenbay obstinateyay aboutyay eingbay easantry.Afterpay alfhay anyay ourhay, ethay unsay oneshay againyay, andyay ethay ocer’sgray automobileroundedyay Atsby’sgay ivedray ithway ethay awray aterialmay orfay ishay ervants’dinner—Isay eltfay uresay ehay ouldn’tway eatyay ayay oonfulspay. Ayay aidmay eganbay openingtheyay upperyay indowsway ofyay ishay ousehay, appearedyay omentarilymay inyay eachyay, and,leaningyay omfray ethay argelay entralcay aybay, atspay editativelymay intoyay egardenthay. Ityay asway imetay Iyay entway ackbay. Ilewhay ethay ainray ontinuedcay ityay adseemedhay ikelay ethay urmurmay ofyay eirthay oicesvay, isingray andyay ellingsway ayay ittlenowlay andyay enthay ithway ustsgay ofyay emotionyay. Utbay inyay ethay ewnay ilencesay Iyay eltfay atsilencethay adhay allenfay ithinway ethay ousehay oo.Itay entway in—afteryay akingmay everyyay ossiblepay oisenay inyay ethay itchenkay, ortshay ofpushingyay overyay ethay ove—butstay Iyay on’tday elievebay eythay eardhay ayay oundsay. Eywerethay ittingsay atyay eitheryay endyay ofyay ethay ouchcay, ookinglay atyay eachyay otheryay asyay ifsomeyay uestionqay adhay eenbay askedyay, oryay asway inyay ethay airyay, andyay everyyay estigevay ofembarrassmentyay asway onegay. Aisy’sday acefay asway earedsmay ithway earstay, andyay enIwhay amecay inyay eshay umpedjay upyay andyay eganbay ipingway atyay ityay ithway erhay andkerchiefbeforehay ayay irrormay. Itwasyay Mray. Ipspringerklay, ethay oarder.”“bay Iyay adhay eensay imhay anderingway ungrilyabouthay ethay eachbay atthay orningmay. Afteryay ishay embarrassmentyay andyay ishay unreasoningyay oyjay ehay asway onsumedwithcay onderway atyay erhay esencepray. Ehay adhay eenbay ullfay ofyay ethay ideayay osay ong,dreamedlay ityay ightray throughay otay ethay endyay, aitedway ithway ishay eethtay etsay, osay ospeaktay, atyay anyay inconceivableyay itchpay ofyay intensityyay. Ownay, inyay ethay eaction,heray asway unningray ownday ikelay anyay over-woundyay ock.Recoveringclay imselfhay inyay ayay inutemay ehay openedyay orfay usyay otway ulkinghay atentcabinetspay ichwhay eldhay ishay assedmay uitssay andyay essing-gownsdray andyay iestay, andhisyay irtsshay, iledpay ikelay icksbray inyay acksstay ayay ozenday igh.“I’vehay otgay ayay anmay inyay Englandyay owhay uysbay emay othesclay. Ehay endssay overyay aselectionyay ofyay ingsthay atyay ethay eginningbay ofyay eachyay easonsay, springay andyay all.”Hefay ooktay outyay ayay ilepay ofyay irtsshay andyay eganbay throwingay emthay, oneyay byay one,beforeyay usyay, irtsshay ofyay eershay inenlay andyay ickthay ilksay andyay inefay annel,whichflay ostlay eirthay oldsfay asyay eythay ellfay andyay overedcay ethay abletay inmany-colouredyay isarrayday. Ilewhay eway admiredyay ehay oughtbray oremay andyay ethay oftrichsay eaphay ountedmay igher—shirtshay ithway stripesay andyay scrollsay andyay aidsplay incoralyay andyay apple-greenyay andyay avenderlay andyay aintfay orangeyay, ithway onogramsmay ofindianyay ueblay. Uddenlysay, ithway ayay straineday oundsay, Aisyday entbay erhay eadhay intotheyay irtsshay andyay eganbay otay cryay ormily.“They’restay uchsay eautifulbay irts,”shay eshay obbedsay, erhay oicevay uffledmay inyay ethickthay oldsfay. “Itay akesmay emay adsay ecausebay I’veyay evernay eensay uch—suchbeautifulsay irtsshay efore.”------------------------------------------------------------------------Afterbay ethay ousehay, eway ereway otay eesay ethay oundsgray andyay ethay immingsway oolpay, andtheyay hydroplaneay, andyay ethay idsummermay owers—butflay outsideyay Atsby’sgay indowitway eganbay otay ainray againyay, osay eway oodstay inyay ayay owray ookinglay atyay ethay orrugatedsurfacecay ofyay ethay Ound.“Ifsay ityay asn’tway orfay ethay istmay eway ouldcay eesay ouryay omehay acrossyay ethay ay,”saidbay Atsbygay. ou“Yay alwaysyay avehay ayay eengray ightlay atthay urnsbay allyay ightnay attheyay endyay ofyay ouryay ock.”Daisyday utpay erhay armyay throughay ishay abruptlyyay, utbay ehay eemedsay absorbedyay inyay athewhay adhay ustjay aidsay. Egreythay indowsway isappearedday asyay ethay ousehay owedglay ullfay ofyay ight.Inlay ethay usic-roommay Atsbygay urnedtay onyay ayay olitarysay amplay esidebay ethay iano.Hepay itlay Aisy’sday igarettecay omfray ayay emblingtray atchmay, andyay atsay ownday ithway eronhay ayay ouchcay arfay acrossyay ethay oomray, erewhay erethay asway onay ightlay avesay atwhay egleamingthay oorflay ouncedbay inyay omfray ethay all.Whenhay Ipspringerklay adhay ayedplay “Theay Ovelay Est”nay ehay urnedtay aroundyay onyay ebenchthay andyay earchedsay unhappilyyay orfay Atsbygay inyay ethay oom.“I’mglay allyay outyay ofyay acticepray, ouyay eesay. Allyay ethay ightslay ereway oinggay onyay inyay Estway Eggyay ow;nay ethay electrictrainsyay, en-carryingmay, ereway ungingplay omehay throughay ethay ainray omfray EwYorknay. Ityay asway ethay ourhay ofyay ayay ofoundpray umanhay angechay, andyay excitementyay asgeneratingway onyay ethay airyay. “Oneay ing’sthay uresay andyay othing’snay urersay Ethay ichray etgay icherray andyay ethay oorpay et—childrengay. Inyay ethay eantimemay, Inyay etweenbay ime—”Astay Iyay entway overyay otay aysay oodbyegay Iyay awsay atthay ethay expressionyay ofbewildermentyay adhay omecay ackbay intoyay Atsby’sgay acefay, asyay oughthay ayay aintfay oubthadday occurredyay otay imhay asyay otay ethay ualityqay ofyay ishay esentpray appinesshay. Almostfiveyay earsyay! Erethay ustmay avehay eenbay omentsmay evenyay atthay afternoonyay enDaisywhay umbledtay ortshay ofyay ishay eams—notdray throughay erhay ownyay aultfay, utbecausebay ofyay ethay olossalcay italityvay ofyay ishay illusionyay. Ityay adhay onegay eyondherbay, eyondbay everythingyay. Ehay adhay thrownay imselfhay intoyay ityay ithway ayay eativepassioncray, addingyay otay ityay allyay ethay imetay, eckingday ityay outyay ithway everyyay ightfeatherbray atthay ifteddray ishay ayway. Onay amountyay ofyay irefay oryay eshnessfray anchallengecay atwhay ayay anmay ancay orestay upyay inyay ishay ostlyghay eart.Ashay Iyay atchedway imhay ehay adjustedyay imselfhay ayay ittlelay, isiblyvay. Ishay andhay ookholdtay ofyay ershay, andyay asyay eshay aidsay omethingsay owlay inyay ishay earyay ehay urnedtowardtay erhay ithway ayay ushray ofyay emotionyay. Iyay inkthay atthay oicevay eldhay imhay ost,withmay itsyay uctuatingflay, everishfay armthway, ecausebay ityay ouldn’tcay eover-dreamed—thatbay oicevay asway ayay eathlessday ong.Theysay adhay orgottenfay emay, utbay Aisyday ancedglay upyay andyay eldhay outyay erhay and;Gatsbyhay idn’tday owknay emay ownay atyay allyay. Iyay ookedlay onceyay oremay atyay emthay andyay eylookedthay ackbay atyay emay, emotelyray, ossessedpay byay intenseyay ifelay. Enthay Iyay entoutway ofyay ethay oomray andyay ownday ethay arblemay epsstay intoyay ethay ainray, eavinglay emtherethay ogethertay. VIAboutay isthay imetay anyay ambitiousyay oungyay eporterray omfray Ewnay Orkyay arrivedyay onemorningyay atyay Atsby’sgay oorday andyay askedyay imhay ifyay ehay adhay anythingyay otay ay.“Anythingsay otay aysay aboutyay at?”whay inquiredyay Atsbygay olitely.“Why—anypay atementstay otay ivegay out.”Ityay anspiredtray afteryay ayay onfusedcay ivefay inutesmay atthay ethay anmay adhay eardGatsby’shay amenay aroundyay ishay officeyay inyay ayay onnectioncay ichwhay ehay eitherwouldn’tyay evealray oryay idn’tday ullyfay understandyay. Isthay asway ishay ayday offyay andwithyay audablelay initiativeyay ehay adhay urriedhay outyay o“tay ee.”Itsay asway ayay andomray otshay, andyay etyay ethay eporter’sray instinctyay asway ight.Gatsby’sray otorietynay, spreaday aboutyay byay ethay undredshay owhay adhay acceptedyay ishospitalityhay andyay osay ecomebay authoritiesyay uponyay ishay astpay, adhay increasedyay allsummeryay untilyay ehay ellfay ustjay ortshay ofyay eingbay ewsnay. Ontemporarycay egendssuchlay asyay ethay underground“ay ipelinepay otay Anada”cay attachedyay emselvesthay ohimtay, andyay erethay asway oneyay ersistentpay orystay atthay ehay idn’tday ivelay inyay ayay ouseathay allyay, utbay inyay ayay oatbay atthay ookedlay ikelay ayay ousehay andyay asway ovedmay ecretlyupsay andyay ownday ethay Onglay Islandyay oreshay. Ustjay whyay esethay inventionsyay ereway asourceyay ofyay atisfactionsay otay Amesjay Atzgay ofyay Orthnay Akotaday, isn’tyay easyyay osay.Jamestay Atz—thatgay asway eallyray, oryay atyay eastlay egallylay, ishay amenay. Ehay adchangedhay ityay atyay ethay ageyay ofyay eventeensay andyay atyay ethay ecificspay omentmay atwitnessedthay ethay eginningbay ofyay ishay areer—whencay ehay awsay Anday Ody’scay achtdropyay anchoryay overyay ethay ostmay insidiousyay atflay onyay Akelay Uperiorsay. Ityay asJamesway Atzgay owhay adhay eenbay oafinglay alongyay ethay eachbay atthay afternoonyay inyay atornyay eengray erseyjay andyay ayay airpay ofyay anvascay antspay, utbay ityay asway alreadyyay AyGatsbyjay owhay orrowedbay ayay owboatray, ulledpay outyay otay ethay Uolomeetay, andinformedyay Odycay atthay ayay indway ightmay atchcay imhay andyay eakbray imhay upyay inyay alfhay anhour.Iyay upposesay e’dhay adhay ethay amenay eadyray orfay ayay onglay imetay, evenyay enthay. Isparentshay ereway iftlessshay andyay unsuccessfulyay armfay eople—hispay imaginationhadyay evernay eallyray acceptedyay emthay asyay ishay arentspay atyay allyay. Ethay uthtray asthatway Ayjay Atsbygay ofyay Estway Eggyay, Onglay Islandyay, sprangay omfray ishay Atonicconceptionplay ofyay imselfhay. Ehay asway ayay onsay ofyay Od—agay phraseay ichwhay, ifyay ityay eansanythingmay, eansmay ustjay at—andthay ehay ustmay ebay aboutyay Ishay Ather’sfay usiness,thebay ervicesay ofyay ayay astvay, ulgarvay, andyay eretriciousmay eautybay. Osay ehay inventedjustyay ethay ortsay ofyay Ayjay Atsbygay atthay ayay eventeen-year-oldsay oybay ouldway elikelybay otay inventyay, andyay otay isthay onceptioncay ehay asway aithfulfay otay ethay end.Foryay overyay ayay earyay ehay adhay eenbay eatingbay ishay ayway alongyay ethay outhsay oreshay ofLakeyay Uperiorsay asyay ayay am-diggerclay andyay ayay almon-fishersay oryay inyay anyyay othercapacityyay atthay oughtbray imhay oodfay andyay edbay. Ishay ownbray, ardeninghay odylivedbay aturallynay throughay ethay alf-fiercehay, alf-lazyhay orkway ofyay ethay acingdaysbray. Ehay ewknay omenway earlyyay, andyay incesay eythay oiledspay imhay ehay ecamecontemptuousbay ofyay emthay, ofyay oungyay irginsvay ecausebay eythay ereway ignorantyay, oftheyay othersyay ecausebay eythay ereway hystericalay aboutyay ingsthay ichwhay inyay isoverwhelminghay elf-absorptionsay ehay ooktay orfay anted.Butgray ishay earthay asway inyay ayay onstantcay, urbulenttay iotray. Ethay ostmay otesqueandgray antasticfay onceitscay auntedhay imhay inyay ishay edbay atyay ightnay. Ayay universeyay ofineffableyay audinessgay unspay itselfyay outyay inyay ishay ainbray ilewhay ethay ocktickedclay onyay ethay ashstandway andyay ethay oonmay oakedsay ithway etway ightlay ishay angledclothestay uponyay ethay oorflay. Eachyay ightnay ehay addedyay otay ethay atternpay ofyay isfancieshay untilyay owsinessdray osedclay ownday uponyay omesay ividvay enescay ithway anobliviousyay embraceyay. Orfay ayay ilewhay esethay everiesray ovidedpray anyay outletyay orhisfay imagination;yay eythay ereway ayay atisfactorysay inthay ofyay ethay unrealityyay ofrealityyay, ayay omisepray atthay ethay ockray ofyay ethay orldway asway oundedfay ecurelysay onayay airy’sfay ing.Anway instinctyay owardtay ishay uturefay oryglay adhay edlay imhay, omesay onthsmay efore,tobay ethay allsmay Utheranlay Ollegecay ofyay Stay. Olaf’syay inyay outhernsay Innesotamay. Estayedhay erethay otway eeksway, ismayedday atyay itsyay erociousfay indifferenceyay otay edrumsthay ofyay ishay estinyday, otay estinyday itselfyay, andyay espisingday ethay anitor’sworkjay ithway ichwhay ehay asway otay aypay ishay ayway throughay. Enthay ehay ifteddray ackbay oLaketay Uperiorsay, andyay ehay asway illstay earchingsay orfay omethingsay otay oday onyay edaythay atthay Anday Ody’scay achtyay oppeddray anchoryay inyay ethay allowsshay alongshore.Codyyay asway iftyfay earsyay oldyay enthay, ayay oductpray ofyay ethay Evadanay ilversay ields,offay ethay Ukonyay, ofyay everyyay ushray orfay etalmay incesay eventy-fivesay. Etransactionsthay inyay Ontanamay oppercay atthay ademay imhay anymay imestay ayay illionairefoundmay imhay physicallyay obustray utbay onyay ethay ergevay ofyay oft-mindednesssay, and,suspectingyay isthay, anyay infiniteyay umbernay ofyay omenway iedtray otay eparatesay imfromhay ishay oneymay. Ethay onenay ootay avourysay amificationsray byay ichwhay Ellayay Aye,thekay ewspapernay omanway, ayedplay Adamemay eday Aintenonmay otay ishay eaknessway andsentyay imhay otay easay inyay ayay achtyay, ereway ommoncay opertypray ofyay ethay urgidjournalismtay inyay 1902ay. Ehay adhay eenbay oastingcay alongyay allyay ootay ospitableshoreshay orfay ivefay earsyay enwhay ehay urnedtay upyay asyay Amesjay Atz’sgay estinyday inLittleyay Irlgay Ay.Tobay oungyay Atzgay, estingray onyay ishay oarsyay andyay ookinglay upyay atyay ethay ailedray eck,thatday achtyay epresentedray allyay ethay eautybay andyay amourglay inyay ethay orldway. Isupposeyay ehay iledsmay atyay Ody—hecay adhay obablypray iscoveredday atthay eoplepay ikedhimlay enwhay ehay iledsmay. Atyay anyyay ateray Odycay askedyay imhay ayay ewfay uestionsqay one(ay ofthemyay elicitedyay ethay andbray ewnay amenay) andyay oundfay atthay ehay asway uickqay andextravagantlyyay ambitiousyay. Ayay ewfay aysday aterlay ehay ooktay imhay otay Uluthday andboughtyay imhay ayay ueblay oatcay, ixsay airspay ofyay itewhay uckday ouserstray, andyay ayachtingyay apcay. Andyay enwhay ethay Uolomeetay eftlay orfay ethay Estway Indiesyay andyay eBarbarythay Oastcay, Atsbygay eftlay oo.Hetay asway employedyay inyay ayay aguevay ersonalpay apacity—whilecay ehay emainedray ithCodyway ehay asway inyay urntay ewardstay, atemay, ipperskay, ecretarysay, andyay evenjailoryay, orfay Anday Odycay obersay ewknay atwhay avishlay oingsday Anday Odycay unkmightdray oonsay ebay aboutyay, andyay ehay ovidedpray orfay uchsay ontingenciescay byreposingay oremay andyay oremay usttray inyay Atsbygay. Ethay arrangementyay astedlay iveyearsfay, uringday ichwhay ethay oatbay entway threeay imestay aroundyay ethay Ontinent.Itcay ightmay avehay astedlay indefinitelyyay exceptyay orfay ethay actfay atthay Ellayay Ayecamekay onyay oardbay oneyay ightnay inyay Ostonbay andyay ayay eekway aterlay Anday Odyinhospitablycay ied.Iday ememberray ethay ortraitpay ofyay imhay upyay inyay Atsby’sgay edroombay, ayay eygray, oridmanflay ithway ayay ardhay, emptyyay ace—thefay ioneerpay ebaucheeday, owhay uringday onephaseyay ofyay Americanyay ifelay oughtbray ackbay otay ethay Easternyay eaboardsay ethay avageviolencesay ofyay ethay ontierfray othelbray andyay aloonsay. Ityay asway indirectlyyay ueday oCodytay atthay Atsbygay ankdray osay ittlelay. Ometimessay inyay ethay oursecay ofyay aypartiesgay omenway usedyay otay ubray ampagnechay intoyay ishay air;hay orfay imselfhay eformedhay ethay abithay ofyay ettinglay iquorlay alone.Andyay ityay asway omfray Odycay atthay ehay inheritedyay oney—amay egacylay ofyay enty-fivethousandtway ollarsday. Ehay idn’tday etgay ityay. Ehay evernay understoodyay ethay egaldevicelay atthay asway usedyay againstyay imhay, utbay atwhay emainedray ofyay ethay illionswentmay intactyay otay Ellayay Ayekay. Ehay asway eftlay ithway ishay ingularlysay appropriateeducation;yay ethay aguevay ontourcay ofyay Ayjay Atsbygay adhay illedfay outyay otay esubstantialitythay ofyay ayay an.------------------------------------------------------------------------Hemay oldtay emay allyay isthay eryvay uchmay aterlay, utbay I’veyay utpay ityay ownday erehay iththeway ideayay ofyay explodingyay osethay irstfay ildway umoursray aboutyay ishay antecedents,whichyay eren’tway evenyay aintlyfay uetray. Oreovermay ehay oldtay ityay otay emay atyay ayay imeoftay onfusioncay, enwhay Iyay adhay eachedray ethay ointpay ofyay elievingbay everythingyay andnothingyay aboutyay imhay. Osay Iyay aketay advantageyay ofyay isthay ortshay althay, ileGatsbywhay, osay otay eakspay, aughtcay ishay eathbray, otay earclay isthay etsay ofmisconceptionsyay away.Ityay asway ayay althay, ootay, inyay myay associationyay ithway ishay affairsyay. Orfay everalweekssay Iyay idn’tday eesay imhay oryay earhay ishay oicevay onyay ethay one—mostlyphay Iyay asway inNewyay Orkyay, ottingtray aroundyay ithway Ordanjay andyay tryingay otay ingratiateyay myselfwithay erhay enilesay aunt—butyay inallyfay Iyay entway overyay otay ishay ousehay oneyay Undayafternoonsay. Iyay adn’thay eenbay erethay otway inutesmay enwhay omebodysay oughtbray OmBuchanantay inyay orfay ayay inkdray. Iyay asway artledstay, aturallynay, utbay ethay eallysurprisingray ingthay asway atthay ityay adn’thay appenedhay efore.Theybay ereway ayay artypay ofyay threeay onyay orseback—Tomhay andyay ayay anmay amednay Oaneslay andayay ettypray omanway inyay ayay ownbray iding-habitray, owhay adhay eenbay erethay eviously.“I’mpray elightedday otay eesay ou,”yay aidsay Atsbygay, andingstay onyay ishay orchpay. “I’mdelighteday atthay ouyay oppeddray in.”Asyay oughthay eythay ared!“Sitcay ightray ownday. Erhapspay ishay esencepray avegay ethay eveningyay itsyay eculiarpay ualityqay ofoppressiveness—ityay andsstay outyay inyay myay emorymay omfray Atsby’sgay otheryay artiesthatpay ummersay. Erethay ereway ethay amesay eoplepay, oryay atyay eastlay ethay amesay ortsay ofpeopleyay, ethay amesay ofusionpray ofyay ampagnechay, ethay amesay any-coloured,many-keyedmay ommotioncay, utbay Iyay eltfay anyay unpleasantnessyay inyay ethay airyay, apervadingyay arshnesshay atthay adn’thay eenbay erethay eforebay. Oryay erhapspay Iyay admerelyhay owngray usedyay otay ityay, owngray otay acceptyay Estway Eggyay asyay ayay orldway ompleteincay itselfyay, ithway itsyay ownyay andardsstay andyay itsyay ownyay eatgray iguresfay, econdsay onothingtay ecausebay ityay adhay onay onsciousnesscay ofyay eingbay osay, andyay ownay Iyay aslookingway atyay ityay againyay, throughay Aisy’sday eyesyay. Ityay isyay invariablyyay addeningtosay ooklay throughay ewnay eyesyay atyay ingsthay uponyay ichwhay ouyay avehay expendedyay ourownyay owerspay ofyay adjustment.Theyyay arrivedyay atyay ilighttway, andyay, asyay eway strolleday outyay amongyay ethay arklinghundredsspay, Aisy’sday oicevay asway ayingplay urmurousmay ickstray inyay erhay throat.“Theseay ingsthay exciteyay emay o,”say eshay isperedwhay. “Ifay ouyay antway otay isskay eanymay imetay uringday ethay eveningyay, Icknay, ustjay etlay emay owknay andyay I’llyay ebay adtoglay arrangeyay ityay orfay ouyay. Ityay occurredyay otay emay atthay ehadhay eenbay eryvay owlyslay endingbay owardtay erhay allyay eveningyay otay attainyay isproximitythay, andyay evenyay ilewhay Iyay atchedway Iyay awsay imhay oopstay oneyay ultimatedegreeyay andyay isskay atyay erhay eek.“Ichay ikelay er,”hay aidsay Aisyday, “Iay inkthay e’sshay ovely.”Butlay ethay estray offendedyay er—andhay inarguablyyay ecausebay ityay asn’tway ayay esturebutgay anyay emotionyay. Afteryay allyay, inyay ethay eryvay asualnesscay ofGatsby’syay artypay erethay ereway omanticray ossibilitiespay otallytay absentyay omherfray orldway. Atwhay asway ityay upyay erethay inyay ethay ongsay atthay eemedsay otay ebay allinghercay ackbay insideyay? Atwhay ouldway appenhay ownay inyay ethay imday, incalculableyay ours?Perhapshay omesay unbelievableyay uestgay ouldway arriveyay, ayay ersonpay infinitelyyay areandray otay ebay arvelledmay atyay, omesay authenticallyyay adiantray oungyay irlgay owhay ithoneway eshfray anceglay atyay Atsbygay, oneyay omentmay ofyay agicalmay encounteryay, ouldblotway outyay osethay ivefay earsyay ofyay unwaveringyay evotion.Iday ayedstay atelay atthay ightnay. Atsbygay askedyay emay otay aitway untilyay ehay asway ee,andfray Iyay ingeredlay inyay ethay ardengay untilyay ethay inevitableyay immingsway artypay adrunhay upyay, illedchay andyay exaltedyay, omfray ethay ackblay eachbay, untilyay ethay ightswerelay extinguishedyay inyay ethay uestroomsgay overheadyay. Enwhay ehay amecay ownday estepsthay atyay astlay ethay annedtay inskay asway awndray unusuallyyay ighttay onyay ishay ace,andfay ishay eyesyay ereway ightbray andyay ired.“Shetay idn’tday ikelay it,”yay ehay aidsay immediately.“Ofyay oursecay eshay id.”“Sheday idn’tday ikelay it,”yay ehay insistedyay. “Sheay idn’tday avehay ayay oodgay ime.”Hetay asway ilentsay, andyay Iyay uessedgay atyay ishay unutterableyay epression.“Iday eelfay arfay awayyay omfray er,”hay ehay aidsay. “It’say ardhay otay akemay erunderstand.”“Youhay eanmay aboutyay ethay ance?”“Theday ance?”day Ehay ismissedday allyay ethay ancesday ehay adhay ivengay ithway ayay apsnay ofhisyay ingersfay. “Olday ortspay, ethay anceday isyay unimportant.”Heyay antedway othingnay esslay ofyay Aisyday anthay atthay eshay ouldshay ogay otay Omtay andsayyay: “Iay evernay ovedlay ou.”yay Afteryay eshay adhay obliteratedyay ourfay earsyay iththatway entencesay eythay ouldcay ecideday uponyay ethay oremay acticalpray easuresmay otay etakenbay. Oneyay ofyay emthay asway atthay, afteryay eshay asway eefray, eythay ereway otay ogay acktobay Ouisvillelay andyay ebay arriedmay omfray erhay ouse—justhay asyay ifyay ityay ereway iveyearsfay ago.“Andyay eshay oesn’tday understand,”yay ehay aidsay. “Sheay usedyay otay ebay ableyay ounderstandtay. E’dway itsay orfay ours—”Hehay okebray offyay andyay eganbay otay alkway upyay andyay ownday ayay esolateday athpay ofyay uitrindsfray andyay iscardedday avoursfay andyay ushedcray owers.“Iflay ouldn’tway askyay ootay uchmay ofyay er,”hay Iyay enturedvay. ou“Yay an’tcay epeatray epast.”“Can’tthay epeatray ethay ast?”pay ehay iedcray incredulouslyyay. “Whyay ofyay oursecay oucan!”Heyay ookedlay aroundyay imhay ildlyway, asyay ifyay ethay astpay ereway urkinglay erehay inyay eshadowthay ofyay ishay ousehay, ustjay outyay ofyay eachray ofyay ishay and.“I’mhay oinggay otay ixfay everythingyay ustjay ethay ayway ityay asway efore,”bay ehay aid,noddingsay eterminedlyday. “She’llay ee.”Hesay alkedtay ayay otlay aboutyay ethay astpay, andyay Iyay atheredgay atthay ehay antedway orecovertay omethingsay, omesay ideayay ofyay imselfhay erhapspay, atthay adhay onegay intolovingyay Aisyday. Ishay ifelay adhay eenbay onfusedcay andyay isorderedday incesay en,butthay ifyay ehay ouldcay onceyay eturnray otay ayay ertaincay artingstay aceplay andyay ogay overyay itallyay owlyslay, ehay ouldcay indfay outyay atwhay atthay ingthay asway ……ay Oneyay autumnyay ightnay, ivefay earsyay eforebay, eythay adhay eenbay alkingway ownday estreetthay enwhay ethay eaveslay ereway allingfay, andyay eythay amecay otay ayay aceplay eretherewhay ereway onay eestray andyay ethay idewalksay asway itewhay ithway oonlightmay. Eystoppedthay erehay andyay urnedtay owardtay eachyay otheryay. Ownay ityay asway ayay oolcay ightwithnay atthay mysteriousay excitementyay inyay ityay ichwhay omescay atyay ethay otway angesofchay ethay earyay. Ethay uietqay ightslay inyay ethay ouseshay ereway umminghay outyay intoyay edarknessthay andyay erethay asway ayay irstay andyay ustlebay amongyay ethay arsstay. Outyay ofyay ecornerthay ofyay ishay eyeyay Atsbygay awsay atthay ethay ocksblay ofyay ethay idewalkssay eallyformedray ayay adderlay andyay ountedmay otay ayay ecretsay aceplay aboveyay ethay ees—hetray ouldclimbcay otay ityay, ifyay ehay imbedclay aloneyay, andyay onceyay erethay ehay ouldcay ucksay onyay epapthay ofyay ifelay, ulpgay ownday ethay incomparableyay ilkmay ofyay onder.Hisway earthay eatbay asterfay asyay Aisy’sday itewhay acefay amecay upyay otay ishay ownyay. Eknewhay atthay enwhay ehay issedkay isthay irlgay, andyay oreverfay edway ishay unutterablevisionsyay otay erhay erishablepay eathbray, ishay indmay ouldway evernay ompray againyay ikethelay indmay ofyay Odgay. Osay ehay aitedway, isteninglay orfay ayay omentmay ongerlay otay etuning-forkthay atthay adhay eenbay struckay uponyay ayay arstay. Enthay ehay issedkay erhay. Athisyay ips’lay ouchtay eshay ossomedblay orfay imhay ikelay ayay owerflay andyay eincarnationthay asway omplete.Throughcay allyay ehay aidsay, evenyay throughay ishay appallingyay entimentalitysay, Iyay asremindedway ofyay omething—ansay elusiveyay rhythmay, ayay agmentfray ofyay ostlay ords,thatway Iyay adhay eardhay omewheresay ayay onglay imetay agoyay. Orfay ayay omentmay ayay phrasetrieday otay aketay apeshay inyay myay outhmay andyay myay ipslay artedpay ikelay ayay umbday an’s,asmay oughthay erethay asway oremay strugglingay uponyay emthay anthay ayay ispway ofyay artledairstay. Utbay eythay ademay onay oundsay, andyay atwhay Iyay adhay almostyay ememberedray asuncommunicableway oreverfay. VIIItay asway enwhay uriositycay aboutyay Atsbygay asway atyay itsyay ighesthay atthay ethay ightsinlay ishay ousehay ailedfay otay ogay onyay oneyay Aturdaysay ight—andnay, asyay obscurelyyay asityay adhay egunbay, ishay areercay asyay Imalchiotray asway overyay. Onlyyay aduallygray idday Ibecomeyay awareyay atthay ethay automobilesyay ichwhay urnedtay expectantlyyay intoyay isdrivehay ayedstay orfay ustjay ayay inutemay andyay enthay ovedray ulkilysay awayyay. Asyay myay aintray emergedyay omfray ethay unneltay intoyay unlightsay, onlytheyay othay istleswhay ofyay ethay Ationalnay Iscuitbay Ompanycay okebray ethay immeringhushsay atyay oonnay. Inyay isthay eathay everyyay extrayay esturegay asway anyay affrontyay otay ecommonthay orestay ofyay ife.Thelay oomray, adowedshay ellway ithway awningsyay, asway arkday andyay oolcay. Ehay entway inside.Gatsbyyay urnedtay otay emay igidly:“Iray an’tcay aysay anythingyay inyay ishay ousehay, oldyay ort.”“She’sspay otgay anyay indiscreetyay oice,”vay Iyay emarkedray. “It’say ullfay of—”yay Ihesitated.“Heryay oicevay isyay ullfay ofyay oney,”may ehay aidsay uddenly.Thatsay asway ityay. I’dyay evernay understoodyay eforebay. Ityay asway ullfay ofyay oney—thatwasmay ethay inexhaustibleyay armchay atthay oseray andyay ellfay inyay ityay, ethay inglejay ofityay, ethay cymbals’ay ongsay ofyay ityay …ay Ighhay inyay ayay itewhay alacepay ethay ing’sdaughterkay, ethay oldengay irlgay om…Tay amecay outyay ofyay ethay ousehay appingwray ayay uartqay ottlebay inyay ayay oweltay, ollowedbyfay Aisyday andyay Ordanjay earingway allsmay ighttay atshay ofyay etallicmay othclay andcarryingyay ightlay apescay overyay eirthay arms.“Shallyay eway allyay ogay inyay myay ar?”cay uggestedsay Atsbygay. Ehay eltfay ethay othay, eenleathergray ofyay ethay eatsay. “Iay oughtyay otay avehay eftlay ityay inyay ethay ade.”“Isshay ityay andardstay ift?”shay emandedday Om.“Yes.”“Welltay, ouyay aketay myay oupécay andyay etlay emay ivedray ouryay arcay otay own.”Thetay uggestionsay asway istastefulday otay Atsby.“Igay on’tday inkthay ere’sthay uchmay as,”gay ehay objected.“Plentyyay ofyay as,”gay aidsay Omtay oisterouslybay. Ehay ookedlay atyay ethay augegay. “Andifay ityay unsray outyay Iyay ancay opstay atyay ayay ugstoredray. Ouyay ancay uybay anythingyay atyay adrugstoreyay owadays.”Anay ausepay ollowedfay isthay apparentlyyay ointlesspay emarkray. Aisyday ookedlay atyay Omfrowningtay, andyay anyay indefinableyay expressionyay, atyay onceyay efinitelyday unfamiliarandyay aguelyvay ecognizableray, asyay ifyay Iyay adhay onlyyay eardhay ityay escribedday inwordsyay, assedpay overyay Atsby’sgay ace.“Comefay onyay, Aisy,”day aidsay Omtay, essingpray erhay ithway ishay andhay owardtay Atsby’scargay. “I’llay aketay ouyay inyay isthay ircuscay agon.”Heway openedyay ethay oorday, utbay eshay ovedmay outyay omfray ethay irclecay ofyay ishay arm.“Youyay aketay Icknay andyay Ordanjay. E’llway ollowfay ouyay inyay ethay oupé.”Shecay alkedway oseclay otay Atsbygay, ouchingtay ishay oatcay ithway erhay andhay. Ordanandjay Omtay andyay Iyay otgay intoyay ethay ontfray eatsay ofyay Atsby’sgay arcay, Omtay ushedpay eunfamiliarthay earsgay entativelytay, andyay eway otshay offyay intoyay ethay oppressiveheatyay, eavinglay emthay outyay ofyay ightsay ehind.“Didbay ouyay eesay at?”thay emandedday Om.“Seetay at?”Hewhay ookedlay atyay emay eenlykay, ealizingray atthay Ordanjay andyay Iyay ustmay avehay ownallknay along.“Youyay inkthay I’myay ettypray umbday, on’tday ou?”yay ehay uggestedsay. erhaps“Pay Iyay am,butyay Iyay avehay a—almostyay ayay econdsay ightsay, ometimessay, atthay ellstay emay atwhay odotay. Aybemay ouyay on’tday elievebay atthay, utbay ience—”Hescay ausedpay. Ethay immediateyay ontingencycay overtookyay imhay, ulledpay imhay ackfrombay ethay edgeyay ofyay eoreticalthay abyss.“I’veyay ademay ayay allsmay investigationyay ofyay isthay ellow,”fay ehay ontinuedcay. “Icoulday avehay onegay eeperday ifyay I’dyay own—”“Doknay ouyay eanmay ou’veyay eenbay otay ayay edium?”may inquiredyay Ordanjay umorously.“What?”hay Onfusedcay, ehay aredstay atyay usyay asyay eway aughedlay. “Aay edium?”“Aboutmay Atsby.”“Aboutgay Atsbygay! Onay, Iyay aven’thay. Iyay aidsay I’dyay eenbay akingmay ayay allinvestigationsmay ofyay ishay ast.”“Andpay ouyay oundfay ehay asway anyay Oxfordyay an,”may aidsay Ordanjay elpfully.“Anhay Oxfordyay an!”may Ehay asway incredulousyay. ike“Lay ellhay ehay isyay! Ehay earsway ayay inksuit.”“Neverthelesspay e’shay anyay Oxfordyay an.”“Oxfordmay, Ewnay Exico,”may ortedsnay Omtay ontemptuouslycay, or“ay omethingsay ikethat.”“Listenlay, Omtay. Ifyay ou’reyay uchsay ayay obsnay, whyay idday ouyay inviteyay imhay otay unch?”demandedlay Ordanjay ossly.“Daisycray invitedyay im;hay eshay ewknay imhay eforebay eway ereway arried—Godmay owswhere!”Weknay ereway allyay irritableyay ownay ithway ethay adingfay aleyay, andyay awareyay ofyay ityay edroveway orfay ayay ilewhay inyay ilencesay. Enthay asyay Octorday Tay. Jay. Eckleburg’syay adedeyesfay amecay intoyay ightsay ownday ethay oadray, Iyay ememberedray Atsby’sgay autionaboutcay asoline.“We’vegay otgay enoughyay otay etgay usyay otay own,”tay aidsay Om.“Buttay ere’sthay ayay aragegay ightray ere,”hay objectedyay Ordanjay. “Iay on’tday antway ogettay alledstay inyay isthay akingbay eat.”Tomhay threway onyay othbay akesbray impatientlyyay, andyay eway idslay otay anyay abruptyay ustystopday underyay Ilson’sway ignsay. Afteryay ayay omentmay ethay oprietorpray emergedyay omthefray interioryay ofyay ishay establishmentyay andyay azedgay ollow-eyedhay atyay ethay ar.“Let’scay avehay omesay as!”gay iedcray Omtay oughlyray. “Whatay oday ouyay inkthay estoppedway or—tofay admireyay ethay iew?”“I’mvay ick,”say aidsay Ilsonway ithoutway ovingmay. een“Bay icksay allyay ay.”“What’sday ethay atter?”“I’mmay allyay unray own.”“Wellday, allshay Iyay elphay myself?”ay Omtay emandedday. ou“Yay oundedsay ellway enoughyay ontheyay one.”Withphay anyay effortyay Ilsonway eftlay ethay adeshay andyay upportsay ofyay ethay oorwayday and,breathingyay ardhay, unscrewedyay ethay apcay ofyay ethay anktay. Ehay adhay iscoveredday atthay Myrtleay adhay omesay ortsay ofyay ifeapartlay omfray imhay inyay anotheryay orldway, andyay ethay ockshay adhay ademay imhay physicallysickay. Iyay aredstay atyay imhay andyay enthay atyay Omtay, owhay adhay ademay ayay aralleldiscoverypay esslay anthay anyay ourhay efore—andbay ityay occurredyay otay emay atthay erewasthay onay ifferenceday etweenbay enmay, inyay intelligenceyay oryay aceray, osay ofoundpray astheyay ifferenceday etweenbay ethay icksay andyay ethay ellway. Ilsonway asway osay icksay athethay ookedlay uiltygay, unforgivablyyay uilty—asgay ifyay ehay adhay ustjay otgay omesay oorgirlpay ithway ild.“I’llchay etlay ouyay avehay atthay ar,”cay aidsay Omtay. “I’llay endsay ityay overyay omorrowafternoon.”Thattay ocalitylay asway alwaysyay aguelyvay isquietingday, evenyay inyay ethay oadbray areofglay afternoonyay, andyay ownay Iyay urnedtay myay eadhay asyay oughthay Iyay adhay eenbay arnedway ofsomethingyay ehindbay. Overyay ethay ash-heapsyay ethay iantgay eyesyay ofyay Octorday Tay. J.Eckleburgay eptkay eirthay igilvay, utbay Iyay erceivedpay, afteryay ayay omentmay, atotherthay eyesyay ereway egardingray usyay ithway eculiarpay intensityyay omfray esslay antwentythay eetfay away.Inyay oneyay ofyay ethay indowsway overyay ethay aragegay ethay urtainscay adhay eenbay ovedasidemay ayay ittlelay, andyay Myrtleay Ilsonway asway eeringpay ownday atyay ethay arcay. Oengrossedsay asway eshay atthay eshay adhay onay onsciousnesscay ofyay eingbay observedyay, andoneyay emotionyay afteryay anotheryay eptcray intoyay erhay acefay ikelay objectsyay intoyay aslowlyyay evelopingday icturepay. Erhay expressionyay asway uriouslycay amiliar—itwasfay anyay expressionyay Iyay adhay oftenyay eensay onyay omen’sway acesfay, utbay onyay MyrtleWilson’say acefay ityay eemedsay urposelesspay andyay inexplicableyay untilyay Iyay ealizedthatray erhay eyesyay, ideway ithway ealousjay errortay, ereway ixedfay otnay onyay Omtay, utbay onJordanyay Akerbay, omwhay eshay ooktay otay ebay ishay ife.------------------------------------------------------------------------Thereway isyay onay onfusioncay ikelay ethay onfusioncay ofyay ayay implesay indmay, andyay asyay edroveway awayyay Omtay asway eelingfay ethay othay ipswhay ofyay anicpay. Ishay ifeway andyay ismistresshay, untilyay anyay ourhay agoyay ecuresay andyay inviolateyay, ereway ippingprecipitatelyslay omfray ishay ontrolcay. Omtay alkedtay incessantlyyay, exultingyay andyay aughinglay, uthisbay oicevay asway asyay emoteray omfray Ordanjay andyay emay asyay ethay oreignfay amourclay ontheyay idewalksay oryay ethay umulttay ofyay ethay elevatedyay overheadyay. Umanhay sympathyhasay itsyay imitslay, andyay eway ereway ontentcay otay etlay allyay eirthay agictray argumentsfadeyay ithway ethay itycay ightslay ehindbay. Irty—thethay omisepray ofyay ayay ecadeday oflonelinessyay, ayay inningthay istlay ofyay inglesay enmay otay owknay, ayay inningbriefcasethay ofyay enthusiasmyay, inningthay airhay. Utbay erethay asway Ordanjay esidemebay, owhay, unlikeyay Aisyday, asway ootay iseway everyay otay arrycay ell-forgottendreamsway omfray ageyay otay ageyay. Asyay eway assedpay overyay ethay arkday idgebray erhay anway acefellfay azilylay againstyay myay oat’scay ouldershay andyay ethay ormidablefay strokeay ofthirtyyay iedday awayyay ithway ethay eassuringray essurepray ofyay erhay and.Sohay eway ovedray onyay owardtay eathday throughay ethay oolingcay ilight.------------------------------------------------------------------------Thetway oungyay Eekgray, Ichaelismay, owhay anray ethay offeecay ointjay esidebay eash-heapsthay asway ethay incipalpray itnessway atyay ethay inquestyay. Ehay adhay eptthroughslay ethay eathay untilyay afteryay ivefay, enwhay ehay strolleday overyay otay egaragethay, andyay oundfay Eorgegay Ilsonway icksay inyay ishay office—reallyyay icksay, aleaspay ishay ownyay alepay airhay andyay akingshay allyay overyay. Ichaelismay advisedyay imhay otay otogay edbay, utbay Ilsonway efusedray, ayingsay atthay e’dhay issmay ayay otlay ofyay usinessbay ifheyay idday. Ilewhay ishay eighbournay asway tryingay otay ersuadepay imhay ayay iolentracketvay okebray outyay overhead.“I’veyay otgay myay ifeway ockedlay inyay upyay ere,”thay explainedyay Ilsonway almly.“She’scay oinggay otay aystay erethay illtay ethay ayday afteryay omorrowtay, andyay enthay e’regoingway otay ovemay away.”Michaelisyay asway astonished;yay eythay adhay eenbay eighboursnay orfay ourfay earsyay, andWilsonyay adhay evernay eemedsay aintlyfay apablecay ofyay uchsay ayay atement.Generallystay ehay asway oneyay ofyay esethay orn-outway enmay: enwhay ehay asn’tway orkingway, esathay onyay ayay airchay inyay ethay oorwayday andyay aredstay atyay ethay eoplepay andyay ethay arsthatcay assedpay alongyay ethay oadray. Enwhay anyoneyay okespay otay imhay ehay invariablylaughedyay inyay anyay agreeableyay, olourlesscay ayway. Ehay asway ishay ife’sway anmay andyay othisnay own.Soyay aturallynay Ichaelismay iedtray otay indfay outyay atwhay adhay appenedhay, utbay Ilsonwouldn’tway aysay ayay ord—insteadway ehay eganbay otay throway uriouscay, uspiciousglancessay atyay ishay isitorvay andyay askyay imhay atwhay e’dhay eenbay oingday atyay ertaintimescay onyay ertaincay aysday. Ustjay asyay ethay atterlay asway ettinggay uneasyyay, omeworkmensay amecay astpay ethay oorday oundbay orfay ishay estaurantray, andyay Ichaelistookmay ethay opportunityyay otay etgay awayyay, intendingyay otay omecay ackbay aterlay. Utbay edidn’thay. Ehay upposedsay ehay orgotfay otay, at’sthay allyay. Enwhay ehay amecay outsideagainyay, ayay ittlelay afteryay evensay, ehay asway emindedray ofyay ethay onversationbecausecay ehay eardhay Mrsay. Ilson’sway oicevay, oudlay andyay oldingscay, ownstairsday intheyay arage.“Beatgay e!”may ehay eardhay erhay cryay. “Throway emay ownday andyay eatbay emay, ouyay irtylittleday oward!”Acay omentmay aterlay eshay ushedray outyay intoyay ethay uskday, avingway erhay andshay andshouting—beforeyay ehay ouldcay ovemay omfray ishay oorday ethay usinessbay asway over.Theyay eath“day ar”cay asyay ethay ewspapersnay alledcay ityay, idn’tday op;stay ityay amecay outofyay ethay atheringgay arknessday, averedway agicallytray orfay ayay omentmay, andyay endisappearedthay aroundyay ethay extnay endbay. Avromay Ichaelismay asn’tway evenyay uresay ofitsyay olour—hecay oldtay ethay irstfay olicemanpay atthay ityay asway ightlay eengray. Eotherthay arcay, ethay oneyay oinggay owardtay Ewnay Orkyay, amecay otay estray ayay undredhay ardsbeyondyay, andyay itsyay iverdray urriedhay ackbay otay erewhay Myrtleay Ilsonway, erhay ifeviolentlylay extinguishedyay, eltknay inyay ethay oadray andyay ingledmay erhay ickthay arkbloodday ithway ethay ust.Michaelisday andyay isthay anmay eachedray erhay irstfay, utbay enwhay eythay adhay orntay openheryay irtwaistshay, illstay ampday ithway erspirationpay, eythay awsay atthay erhay eftbreastlay asway ingingsway ooselay ikelay ayay apflay, andyay erethay asway onay eednay otay istenforlay ethay earthay eneathbay. Ethay outhmay asway ideway openyay andyay ippedray ayay ittlelay attheyay ornerscay, asyay oughthay eshay adhay okedchay ayay ittlelay inyay ivinggay upyay etremendousthay italityvay eshay adhay oredstay osay ong.------------------------------------------------------------------------Welay awsay ethay threeay oryay ourfay automobilesyay andyay ethay owdcray enwhay eway ereway illsomestay istanceday away.“Wreck!”yay aidsay Omtay. “That’say oodgay.
