Eythay adhay evernay eenbay oserinclay eirthay onthmay ofyay ovelay, ornay ommunicatedcay oremay ofoundlypray oneyay ithanotherway, anthay enwhay eshay ushedbray ilentsay ipslay againstyay ishay oat’scay oulderorshay enwhay ehay ouchedtay ethay endyay ofyay erhay ingersfay, entlygay, asyay oughthay eshay ereasleep.------------------------------------------------------------------------Heway idday extraordinarilyyay ellway inyay ethay arway. Ehay asway ayay aptaincay eforebay ewenthay otay ethay ontfray, andyay ollowingfay ethay Argonneyay attlesbay ehay otgay ismajorityhay andyay ethay ommandcay ofyay ethay ivisionalday achine-gunsmay. Afteryay earmisticethay ehay iedtray anticallyfray otay etgay omehay, utbay omesay omplicationcay ormisunderstandingyay entsay imhay otay Oxfordyay insteadyay. Ehay asway orriedway ow—therewasnay ayay ualityqay ofyay ervousnay espairday inyay Aisy’sday etterslay. Eshay idn’tday eewhysay ehay ouldn’tcay omecay. Eshay asway eelingfay ethay essurepray ofyay ethay orldoutsideway, andyay eshay antedway otay eesay imhay andyay eelfay ishay esencepray esidebay erandhay ebay eassuredray atthay eshay asway oingday ethay ightray ingthay afteryay all.Foryay Aisyday asway oungyay andyay erhay artificialyay orldway asway edolentray ofyay orchidsandyay easantplay, eerfulchay obberysnay andyay orchestrasyay ichwhay etsay ethay rhythmay oftheyay earyay, ummingsay upyay ethay adnesssay andyay uggestivenesssay ofyay ifelay inyay ewtunesnay. Allyay ightnay ethay axophonessay ailedway ethay opelesshay ommentcay ofyay e“Bealethay Streetay Ues”blay ilewhay ayay undredhay airspay ofyay oldengay andyay ilverslipperssay uffledshay ethay iningshay ustday. Atyay ethay eygray eatay ourhay erethay erealwaysway oomsray atthay throbbeday incessantlyyay ithway isthay owlay, eetsway ever,whilefay eshfray acesfay ifteddray erehay andyay erethay ikelay oseray etalspay ownblay byay esadthay ornshay aroundyay ethay oor.Throughflay isthay ilighttway universeyay Aisyday eganbay otay ovemay againyay ithway eseason;thay uddenlysay eshay asway againyay eepingkay alfhay ayay ozenday atesday ayay ayday ithhalfway ayay ozenday enmay, andyay owsingdray asleepyay atyay awnday ithway ethay eadsbay andchiffonyay ofyay anyay evening-dressyay angledtay amongyay ingdyay orchidsyay onyay ethay oorbesideflay erhay edbay. Andyay allyay ethay imetay omethingsay ithinway erhay asway cryingay orfay adecisionyay. Eshay antedway erhay ifelay apedshay ownay, immediately—andyay ethay ecisionmustday ebay ademay byay omesay orce—offay ovelay, ofyay oneymay, ofyay unquestionablepracticality—thatyay asway oseclay atyay and.Thathay orcefay ooktay apeshay inyay ethay iddlemay ofyay springay ithway ethay arrivalyay ofyay OmBuchanantay. Erethay asway ayay olesomewhay ulkinessbay aboutyay ishay ersonpay andyay ispositionhay, andyay Aisyday asway atteredflay. Oubtlessday erethay asway ayay ertainstrugglecay andyay ayay ertaincay eliefray. Ethay etterlay eachedray Atsbygay ilewhay ehay asstillway atyay Oxford.------------------------------------------------------------------------Ityay asway awnday ownay onyay Onglay Islandyay andyay eway entway aboutyay openingyay ethay estray oftheyay indowsway ownstairsday, illingfay ethay ousehay ithway ey-turning,gold-turninggray ightlay. Ethay adowshay ofyay ayay eetray ellfay abruptlyyay acrossyay ethay ewandday ostlyghay irdsbay eganbay otay ingsay amongyay ethay ueblay eaveslay. Erethay asway aslowyay, easantplay ovementmay inyay ethay airyay, arcelyscay ayay indway, omisingpray ayay ool,lovelycay ay.“Iday on’tday inkthay eshay everyay ovedlay im.”hay Atsbygay urnedtay aroundyay omfray ayay indowandway ookedlay atyay emay allenginglychay. ou“Yay ustmay ememberray, oldyay ortspay, eshay asveryway excitedyay isthay afternoonyay. Ehay oldtay erhay osethay ingsthay inyay ayay ayway atfrightenedthay er—thathay ademay ityay ooklay asyay ifyay Iyay asway omesay indkay ofyay eapsharperchay. Andyay ethay esultray asway eshay ardlyhay ewknay atwhay eshay asway aying.”Hesay atsay ownday oomily.“Ofglay oursecay eshay ightmay avehay ovedlay imhay ustjay orfay ayay inutemay, enwhay eythay erefirstway arried—andmay ovedlay emay oremay evenyay enthay, oday ouyay ee?”Suddenlysay ehay amecay outyay ithway ayay uriouscay emark.“Inray anyyay ase,”cay ehay aidsay, it“ay asway ustjay ersonal.”Whatpay ouldcay ouyay akemay ofyay atthay, exceptyay otay uspectsay omesay intensityyay inyay isconceptionhay ofyay ethay affairyay atthay ouldn’tcay ebay easured?Hemay amecay ackbay omfray Ancefray enwhay Omtay andyay Aisyday ereway illstay onyay eirweddingthay iptray, andyay ademay ayay iserablemay utbay irresistibleyay ourneyjay oLouisvilletay onyay ethay astlay ofyay ishay armyyay aypay. Ehay ayedstay erethay ayay eek,walkingway ethay streetsay erewhay eirthay ootstepsfay adhay ickedclay ogethertay throughtheay Ovembernay ightnay andyay evisitingray ethay out-of-the-wayyay acesplay otay ichtheywhay adhay ivendray inyay erhay itewhay arcay. Ustjay asyay Aisy’sday ousehay adhay alwaysseemedyay otay imhay oremay mysteriousay andyay aygay anthay otheryay ouseshay, osay ishay ideaofyay ethay itycay itselfyay, evenyay oughthay eshay asway onegay omfray ityay, asway ervadedwithpay ayay elancholymay eauty.Hebay eftlay eelingfay atthay ifyay ehay adhay earchedsay arderhay, ehay ightmay avehay oundher—thatfay ehay asway eavinglay erhay ehindbay. Ethay ay-coach—heday asway ennilessnow—waspay othay. Ehay entway outyay otay ethay openyay estibulevay andyay atsay ownday onyay afolding-chairyay, andyay ethay ationstay idslay awayyay andyay ethay acksbay ofyay unfamiliarbuildingsyay ovedmay byay. Enthay outyay intoyay ethay springay ieldsfay, erewhay ayay ellowtrolleyyay acedray emthay orfay ayay inutemay ithway eoplepay inyay ityay owhay ightmay onceyay aveseenhay ethay alepay agicmay ofyay erhay acefay alongyay ethay asualcay street.Theay acktray urvedcay andyay ownay ityay asway oinggay awayyay omfray ethay unsay, ichwhay, asyay itsankyay owerlay, eemedsay otay spreaday itselfyay inyay enedictionbay overyay ethay anishingcityvay erewhay eshay adhay awndray erhay eathbray. Ehay stretcheday outyay ishay anddesperatelyhay asyay ifyay otay atchsnay onlyyay ayay ispway ofyay airyay, otay avesay ayay agmentfray oftheyay otspay atthay eshay adhay ademay ovelylay orfay imhay. Utbay ityay asway allyay oinggay byay oofasttay ownay orfay ishay urredblay eyesyay andyay ehay ewknay atthay ehay adhay ostlay atthay artofpay ityay, ethay eshestfray andyay ethay estbay, orever.Itfay asway inenay o’clockyay enwhay eway inishedfay eakfastbray andyay entway outyay onyay eporchthay. Ethay ightnay adhay ademay ayay arpshay ifferenceday inyay ethay eatherway andyay erewasthay anyay autumnyay avourflay inyay ethay airyay. Ethay ardenergay, ethay astlay oneyay ofGatsby’syay ormerfay ervantssay, amecay otay ethay ootfay ofyay ethay eps.“I’mstay oinggay otay aindray ethay oolpay odaytay, Mray. Atsbygay. Eaves’lllay artfallingstay ettypray oonsay, andyay enthay ere’sthay alwaysyay oubletray ithway ethay ipes.”“Don’tpay oday ityay oday,”tay Atsbygay answeredyay. Ehay urnedtay otay emay apologetically.“Youyay owknay, oldyay ortspay, I’veyay evernay usedyay atthay oolpay allyay ummer?”Isay ookedlay atyay myay atchway andyay oodstay up.“Twelveyay inutesmay otay myay ain.”Itray idn’tday antway otay ogay otay ethay itycay. Iyay asn’tway orthway ayay ecentday strokeay ofworkyay, utbay ityay asway oremay anthay at—Ithay idn’tday antway otay eavelay Atsbygay. Imissedyay atthay aintray, andyay enthay anotheryay, eforebay Iyay ouldcay etgay myselfay away.“I’llyay allcay ouyay up,”yay Iyay aidsay inally.“Dofay, oldyay ort.”“I’llspay allcay ouyay aboutyay oon.”Wenay alkedway owlyslay ownday ethay eps.“Istay upposesay Aisy’llday allcay oo.”tay Ehay ookedlay atyay emay anxiouslyyay, asyay ifyay ehopedhay I’dyay orroboratecay is.“Ithay upposesay o.”“Wellsay, oodbye.”Wegay ookshay andshay andyay Iyay artedstay awayyay. Ustjay eforebay Iyay eachedray ethay edgehay Irememberedyay omethingsay andyay urnedtay around.“They’reyay ayay ottenray owd,”cray Iyay outedshay acrossyay ethay awnlay. ou’re“Yay orthway ewholethay amnday unchbay utpay ogether.”I’vetay alwaysyay eenbay adglay Iyay aidsay atthay. Ityay asway ethay onlyyay omplimentcay Iyay evergaveyay imhay, ecausebay Iyay isapprovedday ofyay imhay omfray eginningbay otay endyay. Irstfay enoddedhay olitelypay, andyay enthay ishay acefay okebray intoyay atthay adiantray andunderstandingyay ilesmay, asyay ifyay e’dway eenbay inyay ecstaticyay ahootscay onyay atthay actallfay ethay imetay. Ishay orgeousgay inkpay agray ofyay ayay uitsay ademay ayay ightbray otspay ofcolouryay againstyay ethay itewhay epsstay, andyay Iyay oughtthay ofyay ethay ightnay enwhay Ifirstyay amecay otay ishay ancestralyay omehay, threeay onthsmay eforebay. Ethay awnlay anddriveyay adhay eenbay owdedcray ithway ethay acesfay ofyay osethay owhay uessedgay atyay iscorruption—andhay ehay adhay oodstay onyay osethay epsstay, oncealingcay isincorruptiblehay eamdray, asyay ehay avedway emthay oodbye.Igay ankedthay imhay orfay ishay ospitalityhay. Eway ereway alwaysyay ankingthay imhay orthat—Ifay andyay ethay others.“Goodbye,”yay Iyay alledcay. “Iay enjoyedyay eakfastbray, Atsby.”------------------------------------------------------------------------Upgay inyay ethay itycay, Iyay iedtray orfay ayay ilewhay otay istlay ethay uotationsqay onyay aninterminableyay amountyay ofyay ockstay, enthay Iyay ellfay asleepyay inyay myay ivel-chair.Justsway eforebay oonnay ethay onephay okeway emay, andyay Iyay artedstay upyay ithway eatbreakingsway outyay onyay myay oreheadfay. Ityay asway Ordanjay Aker;bay eshay oftenyay alledcay eupmay atyay isthay ourhay ecausebay ethay uncertaintyyay ofyay erhay ownyay ovementsmay etweenhotelsbay andyay ubsclay andyay ivatepray ouseshay ademay erhay ardhay otay indfay inyay anyyay otherwayyay. Usuallyyay erhay oicevay amecay overyay ethay ireway asyay omethingsay eshfray andyay ool,ascay ifyay ayay ivotday omfray ayay eengray olf-linksgay adhay omecay ailingsay inyay atyay eofficethay indowway, utbay isthay orningmay ityay eemedsay arshhay andyay dry.“I’veay eftlay Aisy’sday ouse,”hay eshay aidsay. “I’may atyay Empsteadhay, andyay I’myay oingdowngay otay Outhamptonsay isthay afternoon.”Probablyyay ityay adhay eenbay actfultay otay eavelay Aisy’sday ousehay, utbay ethay actannoyedyay emay, andyay erhay extnay emarkray ademay emay igid.“Youray eren’tway osay icenay otay emay astlay ight.”“Hownay ouldcay ityay avehay atteredmay en?”Silencethay orfay ayay omentmay. En:“However—Ithay antway otay eesay ou.”“Iyay antway otay eesay ouyay, oo.”“Supposetay Iyay on’tday ogay otay Outhamptonsay, andyay omecay intoyay owntay isafternoon?”“No—Ithay on’tday inkthay isthay afternoon.”“Veryyay ell.”“It’sway impossibleyay isthay afternoonyay. Arious—”Wevay alkedtay ikelay atthay orfay ayay ilewhay, andyay enthay abruptlyyay eway eren’tway alkinganytay ongerlay. Iyay on’tday owknay ichwhay ofyay usyay unghay upyay ithway ayay arpshay ickclay, utbay Iknowyay Iyay idn’tday arecay. Iyay ouldn’tcay avehay alkedtay otay erhay acrossyay ayay ea-tablethattay ayday ifyay Iyay evernay alkedtay otay erhay againyay inyay isthay orld.Iway alledcay Atsby’sgay ousehay ayay ewfay inutesmay aterlay, utbay ethay inelay asway usybay. Itriedyay ourfay imes;tay inallyfay anyay exasperatedyay entralcay oldtay emay ethay ireway asbeingway eptkay openyay orfay onglay istanceday omfray Etroitday. Akingtay outyay mytimetableay, Iyay ewdray ayay allsmay irclecay aroundyay ethay three-fiftyay aintray. Enthay Ileanedyay ackbay inyay myay airchay andyay iedtray otay inkthay. Ityay asway ustjay oon.------------------------------------------------------------------------Whennay Iyay assedpay ethay ash-heapsyay onyay ethay aintray atthay orningmay Iyay adhay osseddeliberatelycray otay ethay otheryay idesay ofyay ethay arcay. Iyay upposedsay ere’dthay ebay acuriousyay owdcray aroundyay erethay allyay ayday ithway ittlelay oysbay earchingsay orfay arkspotsday inyay ethay ustday, andyay omesay arrulousgay anmay ellingtay overyay andyay overyay athadwhay appenedhay, untilyay ityay ecamebay esslay andyay esslay ealray evenyay otay imhay andyay ecouldhay elltay ityay onay ongerlay, andyay Myrtleay Ilson’sway agictray achievementyay asforgottenway. Ownay Iyay antway otay ogay ackbay ayay ittlelay andyay elltay atwhay appenedhay attheyay aragegay afteryay eway eftlay erethay ethay ightnay efore.Theybay adhay ifficultyday inyay ocatinglay ethay istersay, Atherinecay. Eshay ustmay avebrokenhay erhay uleray againstyay inkingdray atthay ightnay, orfay enwhay eshay arrivedyay ewasshay upidstay ithway iquorlay andyay unableyay otay understandyay atthay ethay ambulanceyay adalreadyhay onegay otay Ushingflay. Enwhay eythay onvincedcay erhay ofyay isthay, eimmediatelyshay aintedfay, asyay ifyay atthay asway ethay intolerableyay artpay ofyay eaffairthay. Omeonesay, indkay oryay uriouscay, ooktay erhay inyay ishay arcay andyay ovedray erhay intheyay akeway ofyay erhay ister’ssay ody.Untilbay onglay afteryay idnightmay ayay angingchay owdcray appedlay upyay againstyay ethay ontoffray ethay aragegay, ilewhay Eorgegay Ilsonway ockedray imselfhay ackbay andyay orthfay ontheyay ouchcay insideyay. Orfay ayay ilewhay ethay oorday ofyay ethay officeyay asway openyay, andeveryoneyay owhay amecay intoyay ethay aragegay ancedglay irresistiblyyay throughay it.Finallyyay omeonesay aidsay ityay asway ayay ameshay, andyay osedclay ethay oorday. Ichaelisandmay everalsay otheryay enmay ereway ithway im;hay irstfay, ourfay oryay ivefay enmay, atertwolay oryay threeay enmay. Illstay aterlay Ichaelismay adhay otay askyay ethay astlay strangertoay aitway erethay ifteenfay inutesmay ongerlay, ilewhay ehay entway ackbay otay ishay ownplaceyay andyay ademay ayay otpay ofyay offeecay. Afteryay atthay, ehay ayedstay erethay aloneyay ithWilsonway untilyay awn.Aboutday threeay o’clockyay ethay ualityqay ofyay Ilson’sway incoherentyay utteringchanged—hemay ewgray uieterqay andyay eganbay otay alktay aboutyay ethay ellowyay arcay. Eannouncedhay atthay ehay adhay ayay ayway ofyay indingfay outyay omwhay ethay ellowyay arbelongedcay otay, andyay enthay ehay urtedblay outyay atthay ayay ouplecay ofyay onthsmay agoyay iswifehay adhay omecay omfray ethay itycay ithway erhay acefay uisedbray andyay erhay oseswollen.Butnay enwhay ehay eardhay imselfhay aysay isthay, ehay inchedflay andyay eganbay otay cryay “Oh,myay Od!”gay againyay inyay ishay oaninggray oicevay. Ichaelismay ademay ayay umsyclay attempttoyay istractday im.“Howhay onglay avehay ouyay eenbay arriedmay, Eorgegay? Omecay onyay erethay, tryay andyay itstillsay ayay inutemay, andyay answeryay myay uestionqay. Owhay onglay avehay ouyay eenmarried?”“Twelvebay ears.”“Everyay adhay anyyay ildrenchay? Omecay onyay, Eorgegay, itsay ill—Istay askedyay ouyay aquestionyay. Idday ouyay everyay avehay anyyay ildren?”Thechay ardhay ownbray eetlesbay eptkay uddingthay againstyay ethay ullday ightlay, andwheneveryay Ichaelismay eardhay ayay arcay ogay earingtay alongyay ethay oadray outsideyay itsoundedyay otay imhay ikelay ethay arcay atthay adn’thay oppedstay ayay ewfay ourshay efore.Hebay idn’tday ikelay otay ogay intoyay ethay aragegay, ecausebay ethay orkway enchbay asstainedway erewhay ethay odybay adhay eenbay inglyay, osay ehay ovedmay uncomfortablyaroundyay ethay office—heyay ewknay everyyay objectyay inyay ityay eforebay orning—andmay omtimefray otay imetay atsay ownday esidebay Ilsonway tryingay otay eepkay imhay oremay uiet.“Haveqay ouyay otgay ayay urchchay ouyay ogay otay ometimessay, Eorgegay? Aybemay evenyay ifyay ouhaven’tyay eenbay erethay orfay ayay onglay imetay? Aybemay Iyay ouldcay allcay upyay ethay urchandchay etgay ayay iestpray otay omecay overyay andyay ehay ouldcay alktay otay ouyay, ee?”“Don’tsay elongbay otay any.”“Youyay oughtyay otay avehay ayay urchchay, Eorgegay, orfay imestay ikelay isthay. Ouyay usthavemay onegay otay urchchay onceyay. Idn’tday ouyay etgay arriedmay inyay ayay urchchay? Isten,Georgelay, istenlay otay emay. Idn’tday ouyay etgay arriedmay inyay ayay urch?”“Thatchay asway ayay onglay imetay ago.”Theyay effortyay ofyay answeringyay okebray ethay rhythmay ofyay ishay ocking—forray ayay omenthemay asway ilentsay. Enthay ethay amesay alf-knowinghay, alf-bewilderedhay ooklay amebackcay intoyay ishay adedfay eyes.“Lookyay inyay ethay awerdray ere,”thay ehay aidsay, ointingpay atyay ethay esk.“Whichday awer?”“Thatdray awer—thatdray one.”Michaelisyay openedyay ethay awerdray earestnay ishay andhay. Erethay asway othingnay inyay itbutyay ayay allsmay, expensiveyay og-leashday, ademay ofyay eatherlay andyay aidedsilverbray. Ityay asway apparentlyyay ew.“This?”nay ehay inquiredyay, oldinghay ityay up.Wilsonyay aredstay andyay odded.“Inay oundfay ityay esterdayyay afternoonyay. Eshay iedtray otay elltay emay aboutyay ityay, utbay Iknewyay ityay asway omethingsay unny.”“Youfay eanmay ouryay ifeway oughtbay it?”“Sheyay adhay ityay appedwray inyay issuetay aperpay onyay erhay ureau.”Michaelisbay idn’tday eesay anythingyay oddyay inyay atthay, andyay ehay avegay Ilsonway ayay ozenreasonsday whyay ishay ifeway ightmay avehay oughtbay ethay og-leashday. Utbay onceivablyWilsoncay adhay eardhay omesay ofyay esethay amesay explanationsyay eforebay, omfray Myrtle,becauseay ehay eganbay ayingsay “Ohay, myay Od!”gay againyay inyay ayay isper—hiswhay omforterleftcay everalsay explanationsyay inyay ethay air.“Thenyay ehay illedkay er,”hay aidsay Ilsonway. Ishay outhmay oppeddray openyay uddenly.“Whosay id?”“Iday avehay ayay ayway ofyay indingfay out.”“You’reyay orbidmay, Eorge,”gay aidsay ishay iendfray. “Thisay ashay eenbay ayay strainay oyoutay andyay ouyay on’tday owknay atwhay ou’reyay ayingsay. Ou’dyay etterbay tryay andyay itquietsay illtay orning.”“Hemay urderedmay er.”“Ithay asway anyay accidentyay, Eorge.”Wilsongay ookshay ishay eadhay. Ishay eyesyay arrowednay andyay ishay outhmay idenedslightlyway ithway ethay ostghay ofyay ayay uperiorsay “Hm!”“Iay ow,”knay ehay aidsay efinitelyday. “I’may oneyay ofyay esethay ustingtray ellasfay andyay Idon’tyay inkthay anyyay armhay otay obodynay, utbay enwhay Iyay etgay otay owknay ayay ingthay Iyay owitknay. Ityay asway ethay anmay inyay atthay arcay. Eshay anray outyay otay eakspay otay imhay andyay ewouldn’thay op.”Michaelisstay adhay eensay isthay ootay, utbay ityay adn’thay occurredyay otay imhay atthay erewasthay anyyay ecialspay ignificancesay inyay ityay. Ehay elievedbay atthay Mrsay. Ilsonway adbeenhay unningray awayyay omfray erhay usbandhay, atherray anthay tryingay otay opstay anyparticularyay ar.“Howcay ouldcay eshay ofyay eenbay ikelay at?”“She’sthay ayay eepday one,”yay aidsay Ilsonway, asyay ifyay atthay answeredyay ethay uestion.“Ah-h-h—”Heqay eganbay otay ockray againyay, andyay Ichaelismay oodstay istingtway ethay eashlay inyay ishand.“Maybehay ouyay otgay omesay iendfray atthay Iyay ouldcay elephonetay orfay, Eorge?”Thisgay asway ayay orlornfay ope—hehay asway almostyay uresay atthay Ilsonway adhay onay iend:therefray asway otnay enoughyay ofyay imhay orfay ishay ifeway. Ehay asway adglay ayay ittlelay aterwhenlay ehay oticednay ayay angechay inyay ethay oomray, ayay ueblay uickeningqay byay ethay indow,andway ealizedray atthay awnday asn’tway arfay offyay. Aboutyay ivefay o’clockyay ityay asway ueenoughblay outsideyay otay apsnay offyay ethay ight.Wilson’slay azedglay eyesyay urnedtay outyay otay ethay ash-heapsyay, erewhay allsmay eycloudsgray ooktay onyay antasticfay apesshay andyay urriedscay erehay andyay erethay inyay efaintthay awnday ind.“Iway okespay otay er,”hay ehay utteredmay, afteryay ayay onglay ilencesay. “Iay oldtay erhay emightshay oolfay emay utbay eshay ouldn’tcay oolfay Odgay. Iyay ooktay erhay otay ewindow”—withthay anyay effortyay ehay otgay upyay andyay alkedway otay ethay earray indowway andleanedyay ithway ishay acefay essedpray againstyay it—“andyay Iyay aidsay od‘Gay owsknay atyou’vewhay eenbay oingday, everythingyay ou’veyay eenbay oingday. Ouyay aymay oolfay emay, utyoubay an’tcay oolfay Od!’ ”Standinggay ehindbay imhay, Ichaelismay awsay ithway ayay ockshay atthay ehay asway ookinglay attheyay eyesyay ofyay Octorday Tay. Jay. Eckleburgyay, ichwhay adhay ustjay emergedyay, alepay andenormousyay, omfray ethay issolvingday ight.“Godnay eessay everything,”yay epeatedray Ilson.“That’sway anyay advertisement,”yay Ichaelismay assuredyay imhay. Omethingsay ademay imturnhay awayyay omfray ethay indowway andyay ooklay ackbay intoyay ethay oomray. Utbay Ilsonstoodway erethay ayay onglay imetay, ishay acefay oseclay otay ethay indowway anepay, oddingintonay ethay ilight.------------------------------------------------------------------------Bytway ixsay o’clockyay Ichaelismay asway ornway outyay, andyay atefulgray orfay ethay oundsay ofyay acaryay oppingstay outsideyay. Ityay asway oneyay ofyay ethay atchersway ofyay ethay ightnay eforewhobay adhay omisedpray otay omecay ackbay, osay ehay ookedcay eakfastbray orfay threeay, ichhewhay andyay ethay otheryay anmay ateyay ogethertay. Ilsonway asway uieterqay ownay, andMichaelisyay entway omehay otay eep;slay enwhay ehay awokeyay ourfay ourshay aterlay andhurriedyay ackbay otay ethay aragegay, Ilsonway asway one.Hisgay ovements—hemay asway onyay ootfay allyay ethay ime—weretay afterwardyay acedtray oPorttay Ooseveltray andyay enthay otay Ad’sgay Illhay, erewhay ehay oughtbay ayay andwichsay athethay idn’tday eatyay, andyay ayay upcay ofyay offeecay. Ehay ustmay avehay eenbay iredtay andwalkingyay owlyslay, orfay ehay idn’tday eachray Ad’sgay Illhay untilyay oonnay. Usthay artherefay asway onay ifficultyday inyay accountingyay orfay ishay ime—theretay ereway oysbay ohadwhay eensay ayay anmay acting“ay ortsay ofyay azy,”cray andyay otoristsmay atyay omwhay ehay aredoddlystay omfray ethay idesay ofyay ethay oadray. Enthay orfay threeay ourshay ehay isappearedfromday iewvay. Ethay olicepay, onyay ethay strengthay ofyay atwhay ehay aidsay otay Ichaelis,thatmay ehay ad“hay ayay ayway ofyay indingfay out,”yay upposedsay atthay ehay entspay atthay imegoingtay omfray aragegay otay aragegay ereaboutthay, inquiringyay orfay ayay ellowyay arcay. Ontheyay otheryay andhay, onay aragegay anmay owhay adhay eensay imhay everyay amecay orwardfay, andperhapsyay ehay adhay anyay easieryay, urersay ayway ofyay indingfay outyay atwhay ehay antedway oknowtay. Byay alf-pasthay otway ehay asway inyay Estway Eggyay, erewhay ehay askedyay omeonesay ewaythay otay Atsby’sgay ousehay. Osay byay atthay imetay ehay ewknay Atsby’sgay ame.------------------------------------------------------------------------Atnay otway o’clockyay Atsbygay utpay onyay ishay athing-suitbay andyay eftlay ordway ithway ebutlerthay atthay ifyay anyoneyay onedphay ordway asway otay ebay oughtbray otay imhay atyay epoolthay. Ehay oppedstay atyay ethay aragegay orfay ayay eumaticpnay attressmay atthay adamusedhay ishay uestsgay uringday ethay ummersay, andyay ethay auffeurchay elpedhay imhay opumptay ityay upyay. Enthay ehay avegay instructionsyay atthay ethay openyay arcay asn’tway otay etakenbay outyay underyay anyyay ircumstances—andcay isthay asway strangeay, ecausebay efrontthay ightray enderfay eedednay epair.Gatsbyray oulderedshay ethay attressmay andyay artedstay orfay ethay oolpay. Onceyay estoppedhay andyay iftedshay ityay ayay ittlelay, andyay ethay auffeurchay askedyay imhay ifyay eneededhay elphay, utbay ehay ookshay ishay eadhay andyay inyay ayay omentmay isappearedday amongtheyay ellowingyay ees.Notray elephonetay essagemay arrivedyay, utbay ethay utlerbay entway ithoutway ishay eepandslay aitedway orfay ityay untilyay ourfay o’clock—untilyay onglay afteryay erethay asway anyonetoyay ivegay ityay otay ifyay ityay amecay. Iyay avehay anyay ideayay atthay Atsbygay imselfhay idn’tbelieveday ityay ouldway omecay, andyay erhapspay ehay onay ongerlay aredcay. Ifyay atthay astrueway ehay ustmay avehay eltfay atthay ehay adhay ostlay ethay oldyay armway orldway, aidpay ahighyay icepray orfay ivinglay ootay onglay ithway ayay inglesay eamdray. Ehay ustmay avelookedhay upyay atyay anyay unfamiliaryay skyay throughay ighteningfray eaveslay andyay iveredasshay ehay oundfay atwhay ayay otesquegray ingthay ayay oseray isyay andyay owhay awray ethay unlightwassay uponyay ethay arcelyscay eatedcray assgray. Ayay ewnay orldway, aterialmay ithoutbeingway ealray, erewhay oorpay ostsghay, eathingbray eamsdray ikelay airyay, iftedfortuitouslydray aboutyay …ay ikelay atthay ashenyay, antasticfay igurefay idingglay owardhimtay throughay ethay amorphousyay ees.Thetray auffeur—hechay asway oneyay ofyay Olfshiem’sway otégés—heardpray eshots—afterwardsthay ehay ouldcay onlyyay aysay atthay ehay adn’thay oughtthay anythingmuchyay aboutyay emthay. Iyay ovedray omfray ethay ationstay irectlyday otay Atsby’sgay ouseandhay myay ushingray anxiouslyyay upyay ethay ontfray epsstay asway ethay irstfay ingthay atalarmedthay anyoneyay. Utbay eythay ewknay enthay, Iyay irmlyfay elievebay. Ithway arcelyscay awordyay aidsay, ourfay ofyay usyay, ethay auffeurchay, utlerbay, ardenergay, andyay Iyay urrieddownhay otay ethay ool.Therepay asway ayay aintfay, arelybay erceptiblepay ovementmay ofyay ethay aterway asyay efreshthay owflay omfray oneyay endyay urgedyay itsyay ayway owardtay ethay aindray atyay ethay other.Withyay ittlelay ipplesray atthay ereway ardlyhay ethay adowsshay ofyay avesway, ethay adenmattresslay ovedmay irregularlyyay ownday ethay oolpay. Ayay allsmay ustgay ofyay indway atscarcelythay orrugatedcay ethay urfacesay asway enoughyay otay isturbday itsyay accidentalcourseyay ithway itsyay accidentalyay urdenbay. Ethay ouchtay ofyay ayay usterclay ofyay eavesrevolvedlay ityay owlyslay, acingtray, ikelay ethay eglay ofyay ansittray, ayay inthay edcircleray inyay ethay ater.Itway asway afteryay eway artedstay ithway Atsbygay owardtay ethay ousehay atthay ethay ardenersawgay Ilson’sway odybay ayay ittlelay ayway offyay inyay ethay assgray, andyay ethay olocausthay ascompleteway. IXAfteryay otway earsyay Iyay ememberray ethay estray ofyay atthay ayday, andyay atthay ightnay andtheyay extnay ayday, onlyyay asyay anyay endlessyay illdray ofyay olicepay andyay otographersphay andnewspaperyay enmay inyay andyay outyay ofyay Atsby’sgay ontfray oorday. Ayay operay stretchedacrossay ethay ainmay ategay andyay ayay olicemanpay byay ityay eptkay outyay ethay uriouscay, utlittlebay oysbay oonsay iscoveredday atthay eythay ouldcay enteryay throughay myay ardyay, andthereyay ereway alwaysyay ayay ewfay ofyay emthay usteredclay open-mouthedyay aboutyay epoolthay. Omeonesay ithway ayay ositivepay annermay, erhapspay ayay etectiveday, usedyay eexpressionthay adman”“may asyay ehay entbay overyay Ilson’sway odybay atthay afternoonyay, andtheyay adventitiousyay authorityyay ofyay ishay oicevay etsay ethay eykay orfay ethay ewspaperreportsnay extnay orning.Mostmay ofyay osethay eportsray ereway ayay ightmare—grotesquenay, ircumstantial,eagercay, andyay untrueyay. Enwhay Ichaelis’smay estimonytay atyay ethay inquestyay oughttobray ightlay Ilson’sway uspicionssay ofyay ishay ifeway Iyay oughtthay ethay olewhay alewouldtay ortlyshay ebay ervedsay upyay inyay acyray asquinade—butpay Atherinecay, owhay ighthavemay aidsay anythingyay, idn’tday aysay ayay ordway. Eshay owedshay ayay urprisingsay amountofyay aracterchay aboutyay ityay oo—lookedtay atyay ethay oronercay ithway eterminedday eyesunderyay atthay orrectedcay owbray ofyay ershay, andyay oresway atthay erhay istersay adhay everseennay Atsbygay, atthay erhay istersay asway ompletelycay appyhay ithway erhay usband,thathay erhay istersay adhay eenbay intoyay onay ischiefmay ateverwhay. Eshay onvincedherselfcay ofyay ityay, andyay iedcray intoyay erhay andkerchiefhay, asyay ifyay ethay erysuggestionvay asway oremay anthay eshay ouldcay endureyay. Osay Ilsonway asway educedray otay amanyay eranged“day byay ief”gray inyay orderyay atthay ethay asecay ightmay emainray inyay itssimplestyay ormfay. Andyay ityay estedray ere.Butthay allyay isthay artpay ofyay ityay eemedsay emoteray andyay unessentialyay. Iyay oundfay myselfonay Atsby’sgay idesay, andyay aloneyay. Omfray ethay omentmay Iyay elephonedtay ewsnay ofyay ecatastrophethay otay Estway Eggyay illagevay, everyyay urmisesay aboutyay imhay, andyay everypracticalyay uestionqay, asway eferredray otay emay. Atyay irstfay Iyay asway urprisedsay andconfused;yay enthay, asyay ehay aylay inyay ishay ousehay andyay idn’tday ovemay oryay eathebray orspeakyay, ourhay uponyay ourhay, ityay ewgray uponyay emay atthay Iyay asway esponsibleray, ecausenobay oneyay elseyay asway interested—interestedyay, Iyay eanmay, ithway atthay intensepersonalyay interestyay otay ichwhay everyoneyay ashay omesay aguevay ightray atyay ethay end.Iyay alledcay upyay Aisyday alfhay anyay ourhay afteryay eway oundfay imhay, alledcay erinstinctivelyhay andyay ithoutway esitationhay. Utbay eshay andyay Omtay adhay onegay awayearlyyay atthay afternoonyay, andyay akentay aggagebay ithway em.“Leftthay onay address?”“No.”“Sayyay enwhay ey’dthay ebay ack?”“No.”“Anybay ideayay erewhay eythay areyay? Owhay Iyay ouldcay eachray em?”“Ithay on’tday owknay. An’tcay ay.”Isay antedway otay etgay omebodysay orfay imhay. Iyay antedway otay ogay intoyay ethay oomray erehewhay aylay andyay eassureray imhay: “I’llay etgay omebodysay orfay ouyay, Atsbygay. On’tworryday. Iyay an’tcay ogay throughay isthay alone.”Someoneyay artedstay otay askyay emay uestionsqay, utbay Iyay okebray awayyay andyay oingupstairsgay ookedlay astilyhay throughay ethay unlockedyay artspay ofyay ishay esk—he’dneverday oldtay emay efinitelyday atthay ishay arentspay ereway eadday. Obodynay ame.------------------------------------------------------------------------Aboutcay ivefay o’clockyay ouryay ocessionpray ofyay threeay arscay eachedray ethay emeteryandcay oppedstay inyay ayay ickthay izzledray esidebay ethay ate—firstgay ayay otormay earse,horriblyhay ackblay andyay etway, enthay Mray. Osethay owhay entway artherfay anChicagothay ouldway athergay inyay ethay oldyay imday Unionyay Ationstay atyay ixsay o’clockyay ofyay aDecemberyay eveningyay, ithway ayay ewfay Icagochay iendsfray, alreadyyay aughtcay upyay intotheiryay ownyay olidayhay aietiesgay, otay idbay emthay ayay astyhay oodbyegay. Iyay emembertheray urfay oatscay ofyay ethay irlsgay eturningray omfray Issmay Is-or-That’sthay andyay echatterthay ofyay ozenfray eathbray andyay ethay andshay avingway overheadyay asyay eway aughtsightcay ofyay oldyay acquaintancesyay, andyay ethay atchingsmay ofyay invitationsyay: “Areay ougoingyay otay ethay Ordways’yay? ethay Erseys’hay? ethay Schultzes’?”ay andyay ethay onggreenlay icketstay aspedclay ighttay inyay ouryay ovedglay andshay. Andyay astlay ethay urkyyellowmay arscay ofyay ethay Icagochay, Ilwaukeemay andyay Stay. Aulpay ailroadray ookingcheerfullay asyay Christmasay itselfyay onyay ethay ackstray esidebay ethay ate.Whengay eway ulledpay outyay intoyay ethay interway ightnay andyay ethay ealray owsnay, ouryay ow,begansnay otay stretchay outyay esidebay usyay andyay inkletway againstyay ethay indowsway, andtheyay imday ightslay ofyay allsmay Isconsinway ationsstay ovedmay byay, ayay arpshay ildbraceway amecay uddenlysay intoyay ethay airyay. Eway ewdray inyay eepday eathsbray ofyay ityay asyay ewalkedway ackbay omfray innerday throughay ethay oldcay estibulesvay, unutterablyyay awareofyay ouryay identityyay ithway isthay ountrycay orfay oneyay strangeay ourhay, eforebay emeltedway indistinguishablyyay intoyay ityay again.That’syay myay Iddlemay Est—notway ethay eatwhay oryay ethay airiespray oryay ethay ostlay Edetownssway, utbay ethay thrillingay eturningray ainstray ofyay myay outhyay, andyay ethay streetlampsay andyay eighslay ellsbay inyay ethay ostyfray arkday andyay ethay adowsshay ofyay ollywreathshay thrownay byay ightedlay indowsway onyay ethay owsnay. Iyay amyay artpay ofyay atthay, alittleyay olemnsay ithway ethay eelfay ofyay osethay onglay intersway, ayay ittlelay omplacentfromcay owinggray upyay inyay ethay Arrawaycay ousehay inyay ayay itycay erewhay ellingsdway arestillyay alledcay throughay ecadesday byay ayay amily’sfay amenay. Iyay eesay ownay atthay ishasthay eenbay ayay orystay ofyay ethay Estway, afteryay all—Tomyay andyay Atsbygay, Aisyday andJordanyay andyay Iyay, ereway allyay Esternersway, andyay erhapspay eway ossessedpay omedeficiencysay inyay ommoncay ichwhay ademay usyay ubtlysay unadaptableyay otay Easternyay ife.Evenlay enwhay ethay Eastyay excitedyay emay ostmay, evenyay enwhay Iyay asway ostmay eenlykay awareofyay itsyay uperioritysay otay ethay oredbay, sprawlingay, ollensway ownstay eyondbay eOhiothay, ithway eirthay interminableyay inquisitionsyay ichwhay aredspay onlyyay echildrenthay andyay ethay eryvay old—evenyay enthay ityay adhay alwaysyay orfay emay ayay ualityqay ofdistortionyay. Estway Eggyay, especiallyyay, illstay iguresfay inyay myay oremay antasticdreamsfay. Iyay eesay ityay asyay ayay ightnay enescay byay Elyay Ecogray: ayay undredhay ouseshay, atonceyay onventionalcay andyay otesquegray, ouchingcray underyay ayay ullensay, overhangingskyyay andyay ayay ustrelesslay oonmay. Inyay ethay oregroundfay ourfay olemnsay enmay inyay esssuitsdray areyay alkingway alongyay ethay idewalksay ithway ayay stretcheray onyay ichwhay ieslay adrunkenyay omanway inyay ayay itewhay eveningyay essdray. Erhay andhay, ichwhay anglesday overtheyay idesay, arklesspay oldcay ithway ewelsjay. Avelygray ethay enmay urntay inyay atyay ahouse—theyay ongwray ousehay. Utbay onay oneyay owsknay ethay oman’sway amenay, andyay onay onecares.Afteryay Atsby’sgay eathday ethay Eastyay asway auntedhay orfay emay ikelay atthay, istortedbeyondday myay eyes’yay owerpay ofyay orrectioncay. Osay enwhay ethay ueblay okesmay ofyay ittleleavesbray asway inyay ethay airyay andyay ethay indway ewblay ethay etway aundrylay iffstay onyay elinethay Iyay ecidedday otay omecay ackbay ome.Therehay asway oneyay ingthay otay ebay oneday eforebay Iyay eftlay, anyay awkwardyay, unpleasantthingyay atthay erhapspay adhay etterbay avehay eenbay etlay aloneyay. Utbay Iyay antedway oleavetay ingsthay inyay orderyay andyay otnay ustjay usttray atthay obligingyay andyay indifferentseayay otay eepsway myay efuseray awayyay. ByGoday ityay asway awful—”Iyay ouldn’tcay orgivefay imhay oryay ikelay imhay, utbay Iyay awsay atthay atwhay ehay adhay onewasday, otay imhay, entirelyyay ustifiedjay. Ityay asway allyay eryvay arelesscay andconfusedyay. Eythay ereway arelesscay eoplepay, Omtay andyay Aisy—theyday ashedsmay upthingsyay andyay eaturescray andyay enthay etreatedray ackbay intoyay eirthay oneymay oryay eirvastthay arelessnesscay, oryay ateverwhay ityay asway atthay eptkay emthay ogethertay, andyay etotherlay eoplepay eanclay upyay ethay essmay eythay adhay ademay …Iay ookshay andshay ithway im;hay ityay eemedsay illysay otnay otay, orfay Iyay eltfay uddenlysay asthoughyay Iyay ereway alkingtay otay ayay ildchay. Enthay ehay entway intoyay ethay ewellerystorejay otay uybay ayay earlpay ecklace—ornay erhapspay onlyyay ayay airpay ofyay uffbuttons—ridcay ofyay myay ovincialpray ueamishnesssqay orever.------------------------------------------------------------------------Gatsby’sfay ousehay asway illstay emptyyay enwhay Iyay eft—thelay assgray onyay ishay awnlay adgrownhay asyay onglay asyay inemay. Oneyay ofyay ethay axitay iversdray inyay ethay illagevay evertooknay ayay arefay astpay ethay entranceyay ategay ithoutway oppingstay orfay ayay inutemay andpointingyay inside;yay erhapspay ityay asway ehay owhay ovedray Aisyday andyay Atsbygay overyay oEasttay Eggyay ethay ightnay ofyay ethay accidentyay, andyay erhapspay ehay adhay ademay ayay oryaboutstay ityay allyay ishay ownyay. Iyay idn’tday antway otay earhay ityay andyay Iyay avoidedyay imhay enIwhay otgay offyay ethay ain.Itray entspay myay Aturdaysay ightsnay inyay Ewnay Orkyay ecausebay osethay eaming,dazzlingglay artiespay ofyay ishay ereway ithway emay osay ividlyvay atthay Iyay ouldcay illhearstay ethay usicmay andyay ethay aughterlay, aintfay andyay incessantyay, omfray ishay arden,andgay ethay arscay oinggay upyay andyay ownday ishay ivedray. Oneyay ightnay Iyay idday earhay amaterialyay arcay erethay, andyay awsay itsyay ightslay opstay atyay ishay ontfray epsstay. Utbay Ididn’tyay investigateyay. Obablypray ityay asway omesay inalfay uestgay owhay adhay eenbay awayatyay ethay endsyay ofyay ethay earthyay andyay idn’tday owknay atthay ethay artypay asway over.Onyay ethay astlay ightnay, ithway myay unktray ackedpay andyay myay arcay oldsay otay ethay ocer,Igray entway overyay andyay ookedlay atyay atthay ugehay incoherentyay ailurefay ofyay ayay ousehay oncemoreyay. Onyay ethay itewhay epsstay anyay obsceneyay ordway, scrawleday byay omesay oybay ithway apieceyay ofyay ickbray, oodstay outyay earlyclay inyay ethay oonlightmay, andyay Iyay erasedyay it,drawingyay myay oeshay aspinglyray alongyay ethay onestay. Enthay Iyay anderedway ownday otay ebeachthay andyay sprawleday outyay onyay ethay and.Mostsay ofyay ethay igbay oreshay acesplay ereway osedclay ownay andyay erethay ereway ardlyhay anylightsyay exceptyay ethay adowyshay, ovingmay owglay ofyay ayay erryboatfay acrossyay eSoundthay. Andyay asyay ethay oonmay oseray igherhay ethay inessentialyay ouseshay eganbay omelttay awayyay untilyay aduallygray Iyay ecamebay awareyay ofyay ethay oldyay islandyay erehay atfloweredthay onceyay orfay Utchday ailors’say eyes—ayay eshfray, eengray eastbray ofyay ethay ewworldnay. Itsyay anishedvay eestray, ethay eestray atthay adhay ademay ayway orfay Atsby’shousegay, adhay onceyay anderedpay inyay isperswhay otay ethay astlay andyay eatestgray ofyay allhumanyay eams;dray orfay ayay ansitorytray enchantedyay omentmay anmay ustmay avehay eldhay isbreathhay inyay ethay esencepray ofyay isthay ontinentcay, ompelledcay intoyay anyay aestheticcontemplationyay ehay eithernay understoodyay ornay esiredday, acefay otay acefay orfay elastthay imetay inyay istoryhay ithway omethingsay ommensuratecay otay ishay apacitycay orwonder.Andfay asyay Iyay atsay erethay oodingbray onyay ethay oldyay, unknownyay orldway, Iyay oughtthay ofGatsby’syay onderway enwhay ehay irstfay ickedpay outyay ethay eengray ightlay atyay ethay endyay ofDaisy’syay ockday. Ehay adhay omecay ayay onglay ayway otay isthay ueblay awnlay, andyay ishay eammustdray avehay eemedsay osay oseclay atthay ehay ouldcay ardlyhay ailfay otay aspgray ityay. Edidhay otnay owknay atthay ityay asway alreadyyay ehindbay imhay, omewheresay ackbay inyay atvastthay obscurityyay eyondbay ethay itycay, erewhay ethay arkday ieldsfay ofyay ethay epublicrolledray onyay underyay ethay ight.Gatsbynay elievedbay inyay ethay eengray ightlay, ethay orgasticyay uturefay atthay earyay byyearay ecedesray eforebay usyay. Ityay eludedyay usyay enthay, utbay at’sthay omatter—tomorrownay eway illway unray asterfay, stretchay outyay ouryay armsyay urtherfay …ay Andoneyay inefay orning—Somay eway eatbay onyay, oatsbay againstyay ethay urrentcay, ornebay ackbay easelesslycay intotheyay astpay.
